The '''COVID-19 pandemic in Italy''' is part of the [[COVID-19 pandemic|pandemic]] of [[coronavirus disease 2019]] ({{nowrap|COVID-19}}) caused by [[severe acute respiratory syndrome coronavirus&nbsp;2]] ({{nowrap|SARS-CoV-2}}). The virus was first confirmed to have spread to [[Italy]] on 31 January 2020, when two Chinese tourists in Rome tested positive for the virus.<ref name="Corriere_20Jan">{{cite web |title=Coronavirus: Primi due casi in Italia|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_gennaio_30/coronavirus-italia-corona-9d6dc436-4343-11ea-bdc8-faf1f56f19b7.shtml |website=Corriere della sera |accessdate=31 January 2020 |date=31 January 2020|language=it}}</ref> One week later an Italian man repatriated back to Italy from the city of [[Wuhan]], China, was hospitalised and confirmed as the third case in Italy.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-italy-idUSKBN20F0UI|title=First Italian dies of coronavirus as outbreak flares in north|date=21 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=6 March 2020}}</ref> Clusters of cases were later detected in [[Lombardy]] and [[Veneto]] on 21 February,<ref name="ThomReut_IT_16cluster_21Feb">{{cite news | last1= Anzolin | first1= Elisa | last2= Amante | first2= Angelo | title= Coronavirus outbreak grows in northern Italy, 16 cases reported in one day | date=21 February 2020 | agency=[[Thomson Reuters]] | url= https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-italy/coronavirus-outbreak-grows-in-northern-italy-16-cases-reported-in-one-day-idUSKBN20F0UI |accessdate=21 February 2020 |archive-url= https://web.archive.org/web/20200221225322/https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-italy/coronavirus-outbreak-grows-in-northern-italy-16-cases-reported-in-one-day-idUSKBN20F0UI |archive-date= 21 February 2020 |url-status=live}}</ref> with the first deaths on 22 February.<ref name="CorrieredSera_76_recent_cases">{{cite news | language =it | title= Coronavirus: primi casi a Milano. Cosa sappiamo dei nuovi contagi in Lombardia, Veneto e Piemonte |trans-title = Coronavirus: first case in Milan. What we know about new infections in Lombardy, Veneto and Piemont<!-- trans-title is the English translation --> | date= 2020-02-22 |newspaper= [[Corriere della Sera]] | url= https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_22/coronavirus-italia-nuovi-contagi-lombardia-veneto-245e72d4-5540-11ea-8418-2150c9ca483e.shtml |accessdate=2020-02-22 |archive-url= https://web.archive.org/web/20200222225105/https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_22/coronavirus-italia-nuovi-contagi-lombardia-veneto-245e72d4-5540-11ea-8418-2150c9ca483e.shtml |archive-date= 2020-02-22 |url-status=live <!-- live|dead|unfit|usurped --> |url-access = <!-- (subscription/registration/limited)&nbsp;default=free -->}}</ref> By the beginning of March, the virus had spread to all regions of Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus. Colpite tutte le regioni. La Protezione civile: ecco i numeri aggiornati |url=https://www.avvenire.it/attualita/pagine/coronavirus-aggiornamento-5-marzo-2020 |accessdate=19 March 2020 |work=Avvenire |date=5 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref> On 6 March 2020, the Italian College of Anesthesia, Analgesia, Resuscitation and Intensive Care (SIAARTI) published [[medical ethics]] recommendations regarding [[triage]] protocols that needed to be employed.<ref>{{cite techreport|url=http://www.siaarti.it/SiteAssets/News/COVID19%20-%20documenti%20SIAARTI/SIAARTI%20-%20Covid19%20-%20Raccomandazioni%20di%20etica%20clinica.pdf|title=Raccomandazioni di etica clinica per l’ammissione a trattamenti intensivi e per la loro sospensione, in condizioni eccezionali di squilibrio tra necessità e risorse disponibili|institution=Italian College of Anesthesia, Analgesia, Resuscitation and Intensive Care (SIAARTI)|language=it|date=6 March 2020|access-date=12 March 2020|url-status=live|format=PDF|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200312202813/http://www.siaarti.it/SiteAssets/News/COVID19%20-%20documenti%20SIAARTI/SIAARTI%20-%20Covid19%20-%20Raccomandazioni%20di%20etica%20clinica.pdf|archive-date=12 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.theatlantic.com/ideas/archive/2020/03/who-gets-hospital-bed/607807/|title=The Extraordinary Decisions Facing Italian Doctors|last=Mounk|first=Yascha|date=11 March 2020|work=[[The Atlantic]]|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200312233745/https://www.theatlantic.com/ideas/archive/2020/03/who-gets-hospital-bed/607807/|archive-date=12 March 2020|access-date=12 March 2020|quote=Now the Italian College of Anesthesia, Analgesia, Resuscitation and Intensive Care (SIAARTI) has published guidelines for the criteria that doctors and nurses should follow in these extraordinary circumstances. The document begins by likening the moral choices facing Italian doctors to the forms of wartime triage that are required in the field of "catastrophe medicine."}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.politico.eu/article/coronavirus-italy-doctors-tough-calls-survival/|title=Italian doctors on coronavirus frontline face tough calls on whom to save|last=Privitera|first=Greta|date=11 March 2020|work=[[Politico]]|url-status=live|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200312125640/https://www.politico.eu/article/coronavirus-italy-doctors-tough-calls-survival/|archive-date=12 March 2020|access-date=12 March 2020|quote=…the Italian Society of Anesthesia, Analgesia, Resuscitation and Intensive Care, who co-authored new guidelines on how to prioritize treatment of coronavirus cases in hospitals…}}</ref>

On 31 January, the Italian government suspended all flights to and from China and declared a state of emergency. In February, eleven municipalities in [[northern Italy]] were identified as the centres of the two main Italian clusters and placed under quarantine. The majority of positive cases in other regions traced back to these two clusters.<ref name=":8">{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/22/news/coronavirus_in_italia_aggiornamento_ora_per_ora-249241616/|title=Coronavirus in Italia: aggiornamento ora per ora|date=22 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> 
On 8 March 2020, Prime Minister [[Giuseppe Conte]] expanded the quarantine to all of Lombardy and 14 other northern provinces, and on the following day to all of Italy, [[COVID-19 pandemic lockdown in Italy|placing more than 60 million people in lockdown]].<ref>{{cite web |title=Coronavirus: Northern Italy quarantines 16 million people |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-51787238 |website=BBC |accessdate=8 March 2020 |date=8 March 2020}}</ref><ref name="auto">{{cite news |title=All of Italy to be placed on coronavirus lockdown |url=https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/world-europe-51810673 |accessdate=9 March 2020 |work=BBC News |date=9 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://news.sky.com/story/coronavirus-italy-sees-largest-daily-rise-in-deaths-and-confirmed-cases-11953192|title=Coronavirus: Italy deaths jump to 463, with 300 in just one region|publisher=Sky News|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref> On 11 March 2020, Conte prohibited nearly all commercial activity except for supermarkets and pharmacies.<ref name=":12">{{cite web|url=https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/merkel-coronavirus-germany/2020/03/11/e276252a-6399-11ea-8a8e-5c5336b32760_story.html|title=Italy ramps up coronavirus lockdown, Merkel warns virus could infect two-thirds of Germany|last1=Harlan|first1=Chico|last2=Morris|first2=Loveday|website=The Washington Post|access-date=12 March 2020}}</ref><ref name=":13">{{Cite news|last=Rome|first=Eric Sylvers in Milan and Giovanni Legorano in|url=https://www.wsj.com/articles/italy-hardens-nationwide-quarantine-11583962093|title=Italy Hardens Nationwide Quarantine|date=12 March 2020|work=The Wall Street Journal|access-date=12 March 2020|issn=0099-9660}}</ref> On 21 March, the Italian government closed all non-essential businesses and industries, and restricted movement of people.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Safi |first1=Michael |last2=Giuffrida |first2=Angela |last3=Farrer |first3=Martin |title=Coronavirus: Italy bans any movement inside country as toll nears 5,500 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/22/italian-pm-warns-of-worst-crisis-since-ww2-as-coronavirus-deaths-leap-by-almost-800 |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=22 March 2020}}</ref> In May, many restrictions were gradually eased,<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus: Italy takes 'calculated risk' in easing restrictions - PM |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-52687448 |accessdate=16 September 2020 |work=BBC News |date=16 May 2020}}</ref> and on 3 June freedom of movement across regions and other European countries was restored.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Fraser |first1=Alex |title=Italians on the move again as lockdown restrictions ease |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-italy/italians-on-the-move-again-as-lockdown-restrictions-ease-idUSKBN23A1EY |accessdate=16 September 2020 |work=Reuters |date=3 June 2020 |language=en}}</ref>

{{As of|2020|12|02}}, Italy has 761,230 active cases, one of the highest in the world.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://gisanddata.maps.arcgis.com/apps/opsdashboard/index.html#/bda7594740fd40299423467b48e9ecf6|title=Coronavirus COVID-19 Global Cases by the Center for Systems Science and Engineering (CSSE) at Johns Hopkins |access-date=25 March 2020}}</ref> Overall, there have been 1,641,610 confirmed cases and 57,045 deaths (a rate of 945 <!--PLEASE KEEP UPDATED--> deaths per million population)<ref>[https://www.worldometers.info/coronavirus/#countries Coronavirus cases: Reported Cases and Deaths by Country]. [[Worldometer]].</ref> while there have been 823,335 recoveries or dismissals.<ref name="Min_Salute_Situazione">{{cite web|url=http://www.salute.gov.it/portale/nuovocoronavirus/dettaglioContenutiNuovoCoronavirus.jsp?lingua=italiano&id=5351&area=nuovoCoronavirus&menu=vuoto|title=Covid-19 – Situazione in Italia|website=salute.gov.it|publisher=Ministero della Salute|language=it|accessdate=4 May 2020}}</ref> By 2 December, Italy had tested about 13,167,000 people.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.salute.gov.it/imgs/C_17_notizie_4623_0_file.pdf |title=Aggiornamento 27/04/2020 Ore 17.00 |date=27 April 2020 |access-date=28 March 2020}}</ref> Due to the limited number of tests performed, the real number of infected people in Italy, as in other countries, is estimated to be higher than the official count.<ref>{{cite report |last1=Flaxman |first1=Seth |last2=Swapnil |first2=Mishra |last3=Gandy |first3=Axel |display-authors=etal |title=Report 13: Estimating the number of infections and the impact of non-pharmaceutical interventions on COVID-19 in 11 European countries |date=30 March 2020 |pages=1–35 |doi=10.25561/77731 |url=https://spiral.imperial.ac.uk:8443/handle/10044/1/77731 |accessdate=31 March 2020 |publisher=Imperial College London}}</ref><ref>{{Cite journal |last1=Lau |first1=Hien |last2=Khosrawipour |first2=Veria |last3=Kocbach |first3=Piotr |last4=Mikolajczyk |first4=Agata |last5=Ichii |first5=Hirohito |last6=Schubert |first6=Justyna |last7=Bania |first7=Jacek |last8=Khosrawipour |first8=Tanja |date=14 March 2020 |title=Internationally lost COVID-19 cases |url=http://www.sciencedirect.com/science/article/pii/S1684118220300736 |journal=Journal of Microbiology, Immunology and Infection  |volume=53 |issue=3 |pages=454–458 |doi=10.1016/j.jmii.2020.03.013 |pmid=32205091 |pmc=7102572 |issn=1684-1182}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=The total number of Italian coronavirus cases could be '10 times higher' than known tally, according to one official |url=https://www.cnbc.com/2020/03/24/italian-coronavirus-cases-seen-10-times-higher-than-official-tally.html |accessdate=31 March 2020 |publisher=CNBC |date=24 March 2020 }}</ref> In May 2020, the [[Italian National Institute of Statistics]] (Istat) estimated 11,000 more deaths for COVID-19 in Italy than the confirmed ones.<ref>[https://www.istat.it/it/files/2020/05/Rapporto_Istat_ISS.pdf Impatto dell'epidemia COVID-19 sulla mortalità totale della popolazione residente], ''Istituto Nazionale di Statistica''</ref><ref>[https://www.agi.it/cronaca/news/2020-05-04/altri-morti-covid-istat-8511670/ Per l'Istat ci sono 11 mila morti in più collegabili al Covid-19], ''AGI – Agenzia Italiana''</ref> This estimation was later confirmed in October 2020, by a second Istat report.<ref>[https://www.istat.it/it/archivio/240401 Decessi e cause di morte: costa produce l'Istat], ''Istituto Nazionale di Statistica''</ref><ref>[https://twitter.com/Ruffino_Lorenzo/status/1319306546929635332 "Istat ha rilasciato i nuovi dati sulla mortalità. Ci sono tutti i 7.903 comuni italiani fino al 31 agosto. Si vede chiaramente l'impatto del coronavirus su marzo e aprile. Da marzo ad agosto nel 2020 sono morte 47.000 persone in più della media del 2015-19."], ''Lorenzo Ruffino'' – ''[[Twitter]]''</ref> Moreover, in August 2020, the [[Ministry of Health (Italy)|Ministry of Health]] estimated that nearly 1.5 million Italians have been infected by SARS-CoV-2 since the beginning of the pandemic.<ref>[https://www.ilsole24ore.com/art/gli-italiani-colpiti-covid-sono-15-milioni-meta-lombardia-letalita-scende-25percento-ADftekh?refresh_ce=1 Gli italiani colpiti dal Covid sono 1,5 milioni, metà in Lombardia: letalità scende al 2,5%. A Bergamo uno su 4 ha gli anticorpi], ''Il Sole 24 Ore''</ref>

==Background==
On 31 December 2019, the Health Commission of [[Wuhan]], Hubei, China, informed the [[World Health Organization|WHO]] about a cluster of acute pneumonia cases with unknown origin in its province. On 9 January 2020, the [[Chinese Center for Disease Control and Prevention]] (CCDC) reported the identification of a [[novel coronavirus]] (later identified as the [[Severe acute respiratory syndrome coronavirus 2|SARS-CoV-2]]) as the cause.<ref>{{cite web |title=Covid-19 – Situazione nel mondo |url=http://www.salute.gov.it/portale/nuovocoronavirus/dettaglioContenutiNuovoCoronavirus.jsp?lingua=italiano&id=5338&area=nuovoCoronavirus&menu=vuoto |website=salute.gov.it |accessdate=4 March 2020 |language=IT}}</ref> In late January 2020, following the [[COVID-19 pandemic in mainland China|developments of COVID-19 outbreak in mainland China]], on 3 February, Italy set up enhanced screening measures, including thermal cameras and medical staff at airports.<ref name=":0" />

{{Update section |date=March 2020}}
{{COVID-19 pandemic data/Italy medical cases chart}}{{anchor|COVID chart}}

===January 2020: First confirmed cases===
On 31 January, the first two cases of COVID-19 were confirmed in [[Rome]]. A Chinese couple, originally from Wuhan, who had arrived in Italy on 23 January via [[Milan Malpensa Airport]], travelled from the airport to [[Verona]], then to Parma, arriving in Rome on 28 January. The next afternoon, they developed a cough, and by evening the man had a fever; the couple were taken to the [[Lazzaro Spallanzani National Institute for Infectious Diseases]] where they tested positive for SARS-CoV-2 and were hospitalised.<ref name="prima">{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_gennaio_31/virus-primi-due-casi-italia-due-cinesi-marito-moglie-italia-dieci-giorni-e365df1c-43b3-11ea-bdc8-faf1f56f19b7.shtml|title=Prima a Milano, poi l'hotel a Roma: le tappe dei 7 giorni di viaggio della coppia contagiata|last=Frignani|first=Rinaldo|date=31 January 2020|website=Corriere della Sera|language=it|access-date=7 March 2020}}</ref><ref name="Corriere_20Jan"/> On 2 February, a team from the same institute composed of scientists Maria Rosaria Capobianchi, Francesca Colavita, and Concetta Castilletti isolated the genomic sequence of the virus and uploaded it to [[GenBank]].<ref>{{cite news |last1=Armstrong |first1=Mark |title=Italian scientists isolate DNA sequence of coronavirus |url=https://www.euronews.com/2020/02/02/italian-scientists-isolate-dna-sequence-of-coronavirus |accessdate=5 April 2020 |work=euronews |date=2 February 2020 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=https://tg24.sky.it/cronaca/photogallery/2020/02/02/coronavirus-italia-spallanzani-roma.html |work=[[Sky TG24]]|accessdate=2 February 2020|language=it|title=Le tre ricercatrici che hanno isolato il Coronavirus allo Spallanzani di Roma.}}</ref>

On 31 January, the Italian government suspended all flights to and from China and declared a state of emergency with the duration of six months. Prime Minister [[Giuseppe Conte]] said Italy was the first EU country to take this kind of precautionary measure.<ref name="thelocal-flight">{{cite web|url=https://www.thelocal.it/20200131/italy-suspends-all-china-flights-after-coronavirus-cases-confirmed-in-rome/|title=Italy suspends all China flights as coronavirus cases confirmed in Rome|date=31 January 2020|website=THELOCAL|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> The government also introduced thermal scanners and temperature checks on international passengers arriving at Italian airports.<ref name=":0">{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_04/coronavirus-controlli-gli-scanner-termici-aeroporti-italiani-c10b73d2-4796-11ea-bec1-6ac729c309c6.shtml|title=Coronavirus, controlli con gli scanner termici negli aeroporti italiani|last=Berberi|first=Leonard|date=2 April 2020|website=Corriere della Sera|language=it|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

On 6 February, an Italian repatriated from Wuhan tested positive for COVID-19, bringing the total number of cases in Italy to three.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnn.com/asia/live-news/coronavirus-outbreak-02-06-20-intl-hnk/index.html|title=February 6 coronavirus news|first1=Jessie |last1=Yeung |first2=Adam |last2=Renton |first3=Steve|last3=George|date=6 February 2020|publisher=CNN}}</ref>

On 22 February, the repatriated Italian recovered and was discharged from the hospital.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.open.online/2020/02/22/coronavirus-bollettino-dello-spallanzani-guarito-il-ricercatore-italiano-verra-dimesso-oggi/|title=Coronavirus, bollettino dello Spallanzani: guarito il ricercatore italiano, verrà dimesso oggi. Niccolò "sta benissimo" – Il video|date=22 February 2020|website=Open|language=it-IT|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref> On 22 and 26 February, the two previously infected Chinese tourists tested negative for COVID-19 at Lazzaro Spallanzani National Institute in Rome.<ref name=":2">{{cite web|url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/mondo/coronavirus_diretta_morti_contagi_oggi_ultime_notizie_26_febbraio_2020-5075865.html|title=Coronavirus, diretta. Contagi a quota 424, primo caso in Puglia, 12 morti. Lombardia, Fontana è negativo, ma resta in isolamento per 14 giorni|website=Il Messaggero}}</ref>

===February–March 2020: Clusters in Northern Italy===
[[Lombardy]] is a densely habitated area with about 10 million habitants. The outbreak there came to light when a 38-year-old Italian tested positive in [[Codogno]], a [[comune]] in the [[province of Lodi]]. On 14 February, he felt unwell and went to see a doctor in [[Castiglione d'Adda]]. He was prescribed treatments for influenza.<ref name="Repubblica_Codogno_doctors" /> On 16 February, as the man's condition worsened, he went to Codogno Hospital, reporting respiratory problems.<ref name="Repubblica_Codogno_doctors">{{Cite news |title=Codogno, i medici dell'ospedale in trincea: "Quelle accuse del premier fanno più male della malattia"|language=it |work=la Repubblica |date=26 February 2020 |url= https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/codogno_i_medici_dell_ospedale_in_trincea_quelle_accuse_del_premier_fanno_piu_male_della_malattia_-249593374/ |accessdate=26 February 2020}}</ref> Initially there was no suspicion of COVID-19, so no additional precautionary measures were taken, and the virus was able to infect other patients and health workers.<ref name="urlMailand:NZZ">{{cite web |url=https://www.nzz.ch/international/mailand-coronavirus-epidemie-begann-in-spital-ld.1542330 |title=Mailand: Coronavirus-Epidemie begann in Spital |accessdate=24 February 2020 |website= nzz.ch (Neue Zurcher Zeitung)}}</ref> Later, the patient, his pregnant wife and a friend tested positive.<ref name="Repubblica_Codogno_doctors" /> On 20 February, three more cases were confirmed after the patients reported symptoms of [[pneumonia]].<ref name=":1">{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, primi tre contagi in Italia: 38enne, sua moglie e un amico in terapia intensiva. La donna insegna in un liceo |language=it |publisher=La Repubblica |url= https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/21/news/coronavirus_a_milano_contaggiato_38enne_e_un_italiano_ricoverato_a_codogno-249121707/?ref=RHPPTP-BH-I249146878-C12-P1-S1.12-T1 |accessdate=21 February 2020 |date=21 February 2020}}</ref> Thereafter, extensive screenings and checks were performed on everyone that had possibly been in contact with or near the infected subjects.<ref name="Messaggero_22Feb">{{cite news |url= https://www.ilmessaggero.it/italia/coronavirus_diretta_lombardia_codogno_italiano_ultime_notizie-5064423.html |title=Coronavirus, diretta: morto uomo di 78 anni a Padova, è la prima vittima italiana |website=Il Messaggero |date=22 February 2020 |accessdate=22 February 2020 |language=it}}</ref> It was subsequently reported that the origin of these cases had a possible connection to the first European local transmission that occurred in [[Munich]], Germany, on 19 January 2020.<ref name="Repubblica_Munich_Codogno">{{cite news |last1=Luna |first1=Riccardo |title=Coronavirus: il paziente tedesco |url=https://rep.repubblica.it/pwa/generale/2020/03/05/news/coronavirus-250377117/ |accessdate=11 March 2020 |work=La Repubblica |date=5 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

Doctors in Codogno stated that the 38-year-old patient led an active social life in the weeks before his illness and potentially interacted with dozens of people before spreading the virus at their Hospital.<ref name="Repubblica_Codogno_doctors" /><ref name="urlMailand:NZZ" /> Afterward, he was transferred to [[Policlinico San Matteo]] in [[Pavia]],<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://www.liberoquotidiano.it/news/italia/13566825/coronavirus-paziente-uno-codogno-trasferimento-pavia.html |title=Coronavirus, il 38enne paziente uno di Codogno trasferito nella notte a Pavia |website=liberoquotidiano.it |accessdate=25 February 2020}}</ref> and his wife to [[Ospedale Luigi Sacco|Sacco Hospital]] in Milan.<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://edition.cnn.com/asia/live-news/coronavirus-outbreak-02-25-20-hnk-intl/h_485832164169510b66e7bb07479c75b0 |title=Italian authorities identify first known patient to have caught coronavirus in Lombardy |first1=Helen |last1=Regan |first2=Adam |last2=Renton |date=25 February 2020 |publisher=CNN |accessdate=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |url= https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/25/news/coronavirus_paziente_1_ancora_grave_ma_stazionario_la_moglie_incinta_sta_bene-249550115/ |title=Coronavirus, "paziente 1" ancora grave ma stazionario, la moglie incinta sta bene |language=it |date=25 February 2020 |work=la Repubblica |accessdate=25 February 2020}}</ref>

[[File:Emergenza coronavirus (49496308758).jpg|thumb|upright=1.13|[[Protezione Civile|Civil Protection]] volunteers carrying out health checks at [[Guglielmo Marconi Airport]]]]
On 21 February 16 more cases were confirmed – 14 in Lombardy, including the doctor who prescribed treatments to the 38-year-old Codogno man,<ref name="Repubblica_Codogno_doctors" /> and two in [[Veneto]]. On 22 February, a 77-year-old woman from [[Casalpusterlengo]], who suffered from pneumonia and had visited the same emergency room as the 38-year-old from Codogno, died in Lombardy.<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/lombardia/coronavirus-morta-una-donna-in-lombardia-seconda-vittima-italiana_15150431-202002a.shtml|title=Coronavirus, morta una donna in Lombardia: seconda vittima italiana |website=Tgcom24 |language=it |accessdate=22 February 2020}}</ref> Including the 78-year-old man who died in Veneto, the number of cases in Italy rose to 79.<ref name="CorrieredSera_76_recent_cases" /><ref>{{Cite news |title=Coronavirus, in Veneto la prima vittima, Adriano Trevisan, 78 anni. Venti contagiati in Italia. Conte: "Nuove misure" |date=22 February 2020 |work=la Repubblica |url= https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/22/news/cina_coronavirus_italia_virus_wuhan_influenza_codogno_lombardia_veneto_adriano_trevisan-249215365/}}</ref> Of the 76 newly discovered cases, 54 were found in Lombardy, including one patient in [[San Raffaele Hospital]] in Milan<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_22/coronavirus-italia-nuovi-contagi-lombardia-veneto-245e72d4-5540-11ea-8418-2150c9ca483e.shtml |title=Coronavirus, due casi a Milano |first=Simona |last=Ravizza |date=22 February 2020 |website=Corriere della Sera |language=it |accessdate=23 February 2020}}</ref> and eight patients in [[Policlinico San Matteo]] in [[Pavia]],<ref>{{Cite news |title=Coronavirus, a Pavia 8 pazienti ricoverati al San Matteo: anche una coppia di medici |language=it |website=Il Messaggero |date=22 February 2020 |url= https://www.ilmessaggero.it/italia/coronavirus_pavia_medici_contagiati_pieve_porto_morone_chignolo_po_cosa_sta_succedendo_22_febbraio_2020-5068178.html |accessdate=23 February 2020}}</ref> 17 in Veneto, two in [[Emilia-Romagna]], two in [[Lazio]] and one in [[Piedmont]].<ref>{{Cite news |first=Simona |last=Ravizza |title=Coronavirus, due casi a Milano |date=22 February 2020 |language=it |website=Corriere della Sera |url= https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_22/coronavirus-italia-nuovi-contagi-lombardia-veneto-245e72d4-5540-11ea-8418-2150c9ca483e.shtml |accessdate=22 February 2020}}</ref>

A secondary cluster of infections occurred in the region of [[Veneto]], which was initially thought to be the result of a farmer being infected when visiting the primary source in Codogno.<ref name="urlMailand:NZZ"/> The farmer was tested, and the following day, the test was confirmed negative.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.padova24ore.it/negativo-al-test-sul-corona-virus-contadino-albettone-joe-formaggio-occorre-senso-responsabilita/|title=Negativo al test sul corona virus il contadino di Albettone. Joe Formaggio: "Occorre senso di responsabilità"|date=24 February 2020|website=Padova24Ore|language=it-IT|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> On 21 February 2020, two people tested positive in Veneto. The next day, one of them, a 78-year-old man, died at the Schiavonia Hospital in [[Monselice]], making him the first fatality in Italy. The man lived in the municipality of [[Vò]], which was put under quarantine.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/22/news/adriano_trevisan_la_prima_vittima_di_coronavirus_in_italia-249260446/|title=Adriano Trevisan, la prima vittima di coronavirus in Italia|date=22 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

On 23 February, a 68-year-old woman with cancer from [[Trescore Cremasco]] died in [[Crema, Lombardy|Crema]]. The number of cases in Italy rose to 152, including fourteen patients being treated at Policlinico San Matteo in Pavia.<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/23/news/coronavirus_italia-249329434/ |title=Coronavirus, terza vittima in Italia: è una donna ricoverata a Crema. 152 casi positivi |date=23 February 2020 |website=la Repubblica |language=it |access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |url= https://www.globalist.it/news/2020/02/23/coronavirus-sale-a-14-il-numero-dei-casi-ricoverati-a-pavia-2053548.html |title=Coronavirus, sale a 14 il numero dei casi ricoverati a Pavia |publisher=globalist.it |language=it |accessdate=24 February 2020}}</ref> On 24 February, an 84-year-old man with pre-existing medical conditions from [[Villa di Serio]] died in [[Bergamo]] while hospitalised in the Papa Giovanni XXIII Hospital.<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://www.huffingtonpost.it/entry/quarto-morto-in-italia-per-il-coronavirus-aveva-84-anni_it_5e5381b7c5b6b82aa65555f4 |title=Quarto morto in Italia per il coronavirus, aveva 84 anni |date=24 February 2020 |website=L'HuffPost |language=it |accessdate=24 February 2020}}</ref> An 88-year-old man from [[Caselle Landi]], who resided in Codogno, died on the same day.<ref>{{Cite news |url= https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/coronavirus-quarta-vittima-a-bergamo-in-lombardia-scoperti-150-casi_15242453-202002a.shtml |title=Coronavirus, in Italia si contano sei vittime e 230 contagi &#124; In Lombardia il numero maggiore dei casi |website=Tgcom24}}</ref><ref name="Repubblica_24Jan" /> An 80-year-old man from [[Castiglione d’Adda]] died at the Luigi Sacco Hospital in Milan. Additional cases involving six minors were identified in Lombardy. A 4-year-old girl from Castiglione d'Adda was admitted to Policlinico San Matteo in Pavia, and a 15-year-old was hospitalised in Seriate Hospital in Bergamo. Two 10-year-olds from [[Cremona]] and Lodi tested positive and were discharged. A 17-year-old from [[Valtellina]] who attended a school in Codogno, and a school friend from [[Sondrio]], also tested positive.<ref name=":2" /><ref name="TwelfthVictim" /><ref name=":3">{{Cite news |url= https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/coronavirus-325-i-casi-in-italia-il-contagio-si-allarga-a-9-regioni-11-le-vittime_15336711-202002a.shtml |title=Coronavirus, 12 le vittime in Italia: in Lombardia contagiati anche sei minori – Guarita la cinese ricoverata allo Spallanzani |website=Tgcom24 |language=it |accessdate=26 February 2020}}</ref> Officials in [[Apulia]] confirmed that a 33-year-old man from [[Taranto]], who returned from Codogno on 24 February, tested positive and was admitted to San Giuseppe Moscati Hospital.<ref>{{Cite news |title=Coronavirus, primo paziente positivo in Puglia. I medici nella zona rossa: "Noi lasciati soli" |language=it |work=la Repubblica |date=27 February 2020 |url= https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/27/news/coronavirus_in_lombardia_vertice_tra_i_prefetti_a_fine_settimana_decisione_su_riapertura_scuole_e_stadi-249689409/ |accessdate=27 February 2020}}</ref> Officials in [[Abruzzo]] confirmed that a 50-year-old man from [[Brianza]], Lombardy tested positive and was admitted to the intensive-care unit at Giuseppe Mazzini Hospital at [[Teramo]]. He and his family were staying in his holiday home at [[Roseto degli Abruzzi]].<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" /><ref>{{Cite news |title=Coronavirus: primo caso in Abruzzo, è un turista Brianza |language=it |work=la Repubblica |date=27 February 2020 |url= https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/27/news/coronavirus_primo_caso_in_abruzzo_e_un_turista_brianza-249686482/ |accessdate=27 February 2020}}</ref> On 28 February, four people died, including an 85-year-old Lombardy resident in one of the quarantine zones at a hospital in Piacenza, a 77-year-old and two others over the age of 80.<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" /> {{As of|2020|03|01|df=y}}, there were 984 confirmed cases and 73 recoveries in Lombardy.<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" /><ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, in Italia 1.694 casi: 41 i morti. I dati regione per regione al 1 marzo |url=https://www.corriere.it/salute/malattie_infettive/20_marzo_01/coronavirus-italia-positivi-sono-1577-34-morti-83-guariti-dati-1-marzo-215bf998-5be0-11ea-ae74-e93752023e91.shtml |accessdate=2 March 2020 |work=Corriere della Sera |date=3 January 2020 |language=it}}</ref> On the same day, Veneto governor Luca Zaia mentioned that after the first two cases, he ordered all 3,300 Vò residents to be tested. Of 6,800 swabs, 1.7% were confirmed positive. This epidemiological study would be used for outbreak investigation by the [[University of Padua]].<ref name=":10">{{cite web|url=http://www.ansa.it/sito/notizie/cronaca/2020/02/28/zaia-da-test-vo-studio-epidemiologico_2c3d88f3-6a4a-4e00-b255-9e1e2feb2768.html|title=Zaia, da test Vo' studio epidemiologico – Cronaca|date=28 February 2020|website=Agenzia ANSA|language=it|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

On 4 March, Emilia-Romagna's regional minister of health, Raffaele Donini, and minister for territories, Barbara Lori, were declared positive for COVID-19.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/03/04/coronavirus-la-diretta-positivi-2-assessori-dellemilia-romagna-ce-donini-salute-pronto-nuovo-piano-durgenza-per-terapie-intensive/5724878/|title=Coronavirus, la diretta – Positivi 2 assessori dell'Emilia-Romagna: c'è Donini (Salute). Pronto nuovo piano d'urgenza per terapie intensive|date=4 March 2020|website=Il Fatto Quotidiano}}</ref> Governor [[Stefano Bonaccini]] and the other members of the regional government tested negative.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://bologna.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/04/news/coronavirus_positivo_l_assessore_regionale_alla_sanita_donini-250207091/|title=Coronavirus, Emilia Romagna: positivo l'assessore regionale alla Sanità Donini|date=4 March 2020|website=la Repubblica}}</ref>

On 8 March, Prime Minister [[Giuseppe Conte]] extended the [[quarantine]] lockdown to cover the whole region of Lombardy and 14 other [[Northern Italy|northern provinces]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-51787238|title=Coronavirus: Northern Italy quarantines 16 million people|website=BBC|date=8 March 2020}}</ref> On 10 March, Prime Minister Conte increased the quarantine lockdown to cover all of Italy, including travel restrictions and a ban on public gatherings.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-51810673|title=Coronavirus: Italy extends emergency measures nationwide|website=BBC|date=10 March 2020}}</ref> By 14 March, no new cases were detected in the municipality of [[Vò]].<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, a Vo' Euganeo nessun nuovo caso positivo |url=https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/veneto/coronavirus-a-vo-euganeo-nessun-nuovo-caso-positivo_16143366-202002a.shtml |accessdate=18 March 2020 |work=Tgcom24 |date=14 March 2020 |language=IT}}</ref>

On 25 March, the [[Associated Press]] dubbed the [[UEFA Champions League]] match between Bergamo club [[Atalanta B.C.]] and Spanish club [[CF Valencia|Valencia]] at the [[San Siro]] in Milan on 19 February as "Game Zero". The match was the first time Atalanta has progressed to a [[2019–2020 UEFA Champions League knockout phase|Champions League round of 16 match]], and had an attendance of over 40,000 people – about one-third of Bergamo's population. By 24 March, almost 7,000 people in the [[province of Bergamo]] had tested positive for COVID-19, and more than 1,000 people had died from the virus – making Bergamo the most hard-hit province in all of Italy during the pandemic.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://apnews.com/ae59cfc0641fc63afd09182bb832ebe2|title=Game Zero: Spread of virus linked to Champions League match|agency=Associated Press|date=25 March 2020}}</ref>

=== March 2020: Spread to other regions ===
[[File:Trasporto di pazienti in bio-contenimento - 7.jpg|thumb|right|upright=1.13|[[Paramedic]]s carrying a patient under [[biocontainment]], in [[Cervia]]]]
On 25 February, the first case in [[Florence]], Tuscany involved a 63-year-old entrepreneur with companies in Asia who had returned from [[the Philippines]] and [[Singapore]] on 6 January. He tested positive and was admitted to Santa Maria Annunziata Hospital.<ref name=":2" /><ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Tuscany">{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/25/news/coronavirus_toscana-249520102/|title=Coronavirus, primi casi a Firenze e a Palermo. 270 casi in Italia. Salgono a 206 in Lombardia e 38 in Veneto|date=25 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

The first case in [[Rimini]] involved a 71-year-old man from [[Cattolica]] who returned from [[Romania]] on 22 February. He tested positive and was admitted to Infermi Hospital.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://bologna.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/coronavirus_il_71enne_riminese_risultato_positivo_e_rientrato_dalla_romania-249606750/|title=Coronavirus, il paziente 1 in Romagna è un cuoco riminese. Chiuso il ristorante|date=26 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.chiamamicitta.it/coronavirus-a-rimini-venturi-caso-spinoso-paziente-ha-avuto-molti-contatti/|title=Coronavirus, a Rimini caso anomalo. Venturi: "Paziente ha viaggiato molto"|date=25 February 2020|website=Chiamamicitta|language=it-IT|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> A 51-year-old man from [[Piandimeleto]] who went to Romania with the man also tested positive and underwent self-quarantine at home.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.digi24.ro/stiri/actualitate/un-italian-care-l-a-insotit-in-romania-pe-barbatul-de-71-de-ani-infectat-are-si-el-coronavirus-1266637|title=Primul italian venit în România ar fi infectat cu coronavirus trei persoane în Italia|website=digi24.ro|language=ro|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> On 26 February, one of the people with whom he had interacted in Romania tested positive.<ref name=":5">{{cite web|url=https://www.digi24.ro/stiri/actualitate/primul-caz-de-coronavirus-in-romania-1266806|title=Primul caz de coronavirus în România. Suspiciuni despre un al doilea caz în Gorj|trans-title=First coronavirus case in Romania. Suspicions about a second case in Gorj|language=ro|website=Digi24|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

On 26 February, the [[Norwegian Institute of Public Health]] confirmed that a 26-year-old Norwegian man living in Florence tested positive and had been admitted to Santa Maria Annunziata Hospital. He had been staying in Norway for 14 days and had returned to Florence five days before becoming ill.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.lanazione.it/firenze/cronaca/coronavirus-toscana-1.5046897|title=Coronavirus in Toscana: quattro positivi, altri due casi di contagio a Firenze / Diretta|last=Nazione|first=La|date=26 February 2020|website=La Nazione|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.thelocal.no/20200226/norwegian-student-tests-positive-for-coronavirus-in-italy|title=Norwegian student tests positive for coronavirus in Italy|website=thelocal.no|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

[[File:CoViD-19 IT.svg|thumb|220px|left|Number of cases (blue) and number of deaths (red) on a [[logarithmic scale]].]]
The passenger ferry ''GNV Rhapsody'' was placed under isolation in the port of Genoa with 58 crew members on board after a passenger tested positive for the virus after having sailed to Tunisia on the ship.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.portnews.it/en/coronavirus-gnv-rhapsody-in-isolation/|title=Coronavirus, GNV Rhapsody in isolation|date=4 March 2020|website=PortNews|access-date=10 March 2020}}</ref>

On 7 March, [[President of Lazio]] and leader of the [[Democratic Party (Italy)|Democratic Party]], [[Nicola Zingaretti]], tested positive for COVID-19.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/roma/news/coronavirus_zingaretti_positivo_nicola_lazio_isolamento_famiglia-5096996.html|title=Coronavirus, Zingaretti positivo: sto bene, sono in isolamento. Controlli sullo staff. La solidarietà della politica|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref> Ten days before, he was in Milan attending public events.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/27/foto/coronavirus_zingaretti_pd_milano-249756747/1/#1|title="Milano non-si ferma per il coronavirus": spritz e tramezzini con il segretario Pd Zingaretti|date=27 February 2020|accessdate=22 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/italy-pandemic-s-new-epicenter-has-lessons-for-the-world/ar-BB11vMrO?ocid=msedgdhp|title=Italy, Pandemic's New Epicenter, Has Lessons for the World|accessdate=22 March 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200322110135/https://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/italy-pandemic-s-new-epicenter-has-lessons-for-the-world/ar-BB11vMrO%3Focid%3Dmsedgdhp|archive-date=22 March 2020|url-status=dead}}</ref> The following day, [[List of presidents of Piedmont|President of Piedmont]] [[Alberto Cirio]] also tested positive.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, anche il governatore del Piemonte positivo – La Stampa |url=https://www.lastampa.it/cronaca/2020/03/08/news/anche-il-governatore-del-piemonte-alberto-cirio-positivo-al-coronavirus-1.38566278 |accessdate=8 March 2020 |work=[[La Stampa]] |date=8 March 2020 |language=it-IT}}</ref>

A US Navy sailor stationed in [[Naples]] tested positive on 6 March. Health officials in the US military began "a thorough contact investigation" to determine if any other person may have been exposed to the virus.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnn.com/2020/03/07/politics/us-navy-sailor-coronavirus-europe/index.html|title=US Navy sailor in Italy tests positive for coronavirus|publisher=CNN|accessdate=8 March 2020|date=7 March 2020}}</ref>

On 11 March, it was announced that [[Juventus F.C.|Juventus]] and [[Italy national football team|national team]] footballer [[Daniele Rugani]] had tested positive for COVID-19.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.bbc.com/sport/football/51844945|title=Coronavirus: Juventus centre-back Daniele Rugani tests positive for virus|publisher=BBC|accessdate=11 March 2020|date=11 March 2020}}</ref>

GIMBE (Italy's Group for Evidence-based Medicine), in a report from 18 March, analysed data from the [[Istituto Superiore di Sanità]] and found that healthcare workers represented over 8% of all detected coronavirus cases.<ref name="aj-oddone-rising-number">{{cite web |last1=Oddone |first1=Elisa |title=Rising number of medical staff infected with coronavirus in Italy |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2020/03/rising-number-medical-staff-infected-coronavirus-italy-200318183939314.html |publisher=[[Al Jazeera]] |accessdate=19 March 2020 |date=18 March 2020}}</ref>

On 26 March 2020, Italica Grondona became the world's oldest person to recover successfully from the [[coronavirus]] at the age of 102.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://themalaysianreserve.com/2020/03/30/covid-19-102-year-old-italian-woman-survives-the-virus/|title=COVID-19: 102-year-old Italian woman survives the virus|date=30 March 2020|website=The Malaysian Reserve|access-date=31 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite web|url=https://nypost.com/2020/03/29/102-year-old-woman-from-italy-recovers-from-coronavirus/|title=102-year-old woman from Italy recovers from coronavirus|last=Salo|first=Jackie|date=29 March 2020|website=New York Post|access-date=31 March 2020}}</ref> She was successfully recovered from the coronavirus after being tested positive with mild symptoms and was hospitalised in [[Genoa]] on 9 March for 20 days.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://abc7news.com/6063077/|title=102-year-old woman recovers from COVID-19 after 20-day hospitalization in Italy|date=30 March 2020|website=ABC7 San Francisco|access-date=31 March 2020}}</ref>

On 22 March, it was announced that Juventus forward [[Paulo Dybala]] and former [[Italy national football team|Italy national team]] captain [[Paolo Maldini]] had tested positive for COVID-19.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.bbc.com/sport/football/51991426|title=Coronavirus: Paulo Dybala and Paolo Maldini test positive|publisher=BBC|accessdate=22 March 2020|date=22 March 2020}}</ref>

=== March–May 2020: Under national lockdown ===
{{See also|#Nationwide measures}}
[[File:Covid-19 San Salvatore 09.jpg|thumb|right|250px|An exhausted [[Anesthesiology|anesthesiologist physician]], in [[Pesaro]]'s hospital, March 2020]]
Starting on 8 March, the region of Lombardy together with 14 additional northern and central provinces in Piedmont, Emilia-Romagna, Veneto, and Marche, were put under lockdown.<ref name="bbc_lombardy_lockdown" /> Two days later, the government [[2020 Italy coronavirus lockdown|extended the lockdown measures to the whole country]].<ref name="cnn_italy_lockdown" />

Two weeks later, the number of new cases per day started to show signs of slowing down, while the number of new deaths rose slightly.<ref>{{cite news |title=Italy's coronavirus deaths rise slightly, but new cases continue to slow |url=https://www.thelocal.it/20200330/latest-coronavirus-deaths-italy |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=The Local.it |date=30 March 2020}}</ref>
On 31 March, the president of the Italian National Institute of Health, Silvio Brusaferro, announced that the pandemic had reached its peak in the country.<ref>{{cite news |title="L'Italia ha raggiunto il picco", dice l'Istituto Superiore di Sanità |url=https://www.agi.it/cronaca/news/2020-03-31/coronavirus-istituto-superiore-sanit-picco-8038210/ |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=Agi |date=31 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref> The news was confirmed also by the head of the Civil Protection, Angelo Borrelli.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, Borrelli: Raggiunto il picco ma non abbassare la guardia - Salute & Benessere |url=https://www.ansa.it/canale_saluteebenessere/notizie/sanita/2020/03/30/coronavirus-curva-contagi-italia-lombardia-guariti-bandiere-lutto_947f659c-647e-4242-ac48-e2b793e46846.html |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=ANSA |date=30 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

Three weeks into the lockdown, its effects began to show. Italy reported declines in the number of new cases and of new deaths per day. The country also saw a steady decrease in the occupancy of intensive care units.<ref>{{cite news |title=LATEST: Pressure on Italy's intensive care wards eases as new coronavirus cases slow again |url=https://www.thelocal.it/20200406/latest-coronavirus-numbers-italy |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=The Local.it |date=6 April 2020}}</ref> On 5 April, Italy had the lowest number of new daily deaths in two and a half weeks,<ref>{{cite news |last1=Colten |first1=Jerrold |last2=Orihuela |first2=Rodrigo |title=Europe's Slowing Virus Deaths Bolster Leaders on Lockdowns |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-04-05/italy-reports-lowest-daily-coronavirus-fatalities-since-march-19 |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=Bloomberg |date=5 April 2020}}</ref> and one day later the lowest number of new daily cases in three weeks.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Follain |first1=John |title=Italy Reports Lowest New Virus Infections in Almost Three Weeks |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-04-06/italy-reports-lowest-new-virus-infections-in-almost-three-weeks |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=Bloomberg |date=6 April 2020}}</ref>
On 20 April 2020, Italy saw the first fall in the number of active cases.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Mayberry |first1=Kate |last2=Stepansky |first2=Joseph |last3=Varshalomidze |first3=Tamila |title=Italy sees first fall of active coronavirus cases: Live updates |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2020/04/coronavirus-deaths-exceed-40000-live-updates-200419233722851.html |accessdate=21 April 2020 |work=www.aljazeera.com |date=20 April 2020}}</ref>

=== May–September 2020: Reduction of cases and loosening of restrictions===
COVID-19 cases started to decline in May 2020, thanks to the two-months lockdown. Freedom of movements was re-established on 4 May and other not essential activities re-opened later in the month.

=== September 2020–October 2020: Arrival of the second wave ===
{{Update section |date=October 2020}}
Since the end of September 2020, the virus regained strength and grew its prevalence in the regions of Campania and Lazio. This corresponded to a rise in new cases experienced also in other major European countries.

On 14 October, cases of COVID-19 positives exceeded the peak of the March infections.<ref>{{cite news |title=Covid, nuovo record contagi: oltre 8 mila. Morti raddoppiano |url=https://www.ansa.it/sito/notizie/topnews/2020/10/15/covid-nuovo-record-contagi-oltre-8-mila.-morti-raddoppiano_f9b6b817-5cd6-47f3-8be8-0ff937833203.html |accessdate=15 October 2020 |agency=ansa.it |publisher=ansa.it |date=15 October 2020}}</ref>

On October 15, the governor of [[Campania]] closed schools and universities until 30 October 2020.<ref name="tgcom24">{{cite news |title=Covid, picco di casi in Campania: chiuse scuole e università fino al 30/10 |url=https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/campania/covid-impennata-di-casi-in-campania-de-luca-chiude-le-scuole-fino-al-30-ottobre_24252326-202002a.shtml |accessdate=15 October 2020 |agency=tgcom24 |publisher=tgcom24 |date=15 October 2020}}</ref>

=== November 2020–ongoing: A new lockdown ===
On 4 November 2020, Prime Minister Conte announced a new lockdown, dividing the country into three zones depending on the severity of the pandemic. Lombardy, Piedmont, Aosta Valley and Calabria, known as "Red Zones", were put under a strict lockdown, similar to the one which was implement from March to May 2020.<ref>[https://www.repubblica.it/politica/2020/11/04/news/dpcm_scontro_governo_regioni_fasce_rischio_coronavirus-273109038/ Il Dpcm slitta a venerdì. Conte: "In fascia arancione Puglia e Sicilia. Zona rossa per Calabria, Lombardia, Piemonte, Valle d'Aosta"], ''la Repubblica''</ref> A lesser strict lockdown was implement in the "Orange Zones" of Apulia and Sicily, while the rest of the country was declared "Yellow Zone", with a few restrictions. Conte described the situation as "particularly critical", asserting that the virus was moving at a "strong and even violent" pace.<ref>[https://www.nytimes.com/live/2020/11/04/world/covid-19-coronavirus-updates/italy-will-lock-down-six-regions-and-prevent-many-people-from-crossing-between-them Italy will lock down six regions and prevent many people from crossing between them.], ''The New York Times''</ref> In the following week, Campania and Tuscany were declared "Red Zones", while other seven regions, Emilia-Romagna, Friuli-Venezia Giulia, Liguria, Umbria, Marche, Abruzzo and Basilicata, became "Orange Zones".<ref>[https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/11/13/news/coronavirus_campania_e_toscana_diventano_rosse_salgono_a_nove_le_regioni_arancioni-274236701/?ref=RHTP-BH-I273902727-P3-S1-T1 Coronavirus, Campania e Toscana diventano zona rosse, salgono a nove le regioni arancioni], ''la Repubblica''</ref>

==Management==

===First measures===
On 31 January 2020, the [[Council of Ministers of Italy|Italian Council of Ministers]] appointed [[Angelo Borrelli]], head of the [[Protezione Civile|Civil Protection]], as Special Commissioner for the COVID-19 emergency.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://tg24.sky.it/politica/approfondimenti/angelo-borrelli-chi-e.html|title=Chi è Angelo Borrelli, capo della protezione civile nominato commissario per l'emergenza coronavirus &#124; Sky TG24|website=tg24.sky.it}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.fanpage.it/politica/coronavirus-angelo-borrelli-nominato-commissario-straordinario-ecco-chi-e/|title=Coronavirus, Angelo Borrelli commissario straordinario: potrà anche requisire gli hotel|website=Fanpage}}</ref>

[[File:2020 coronavirus task force.jpg|thumb|upright=1.13|[[Conte II Cabinet|Italian government]] task force to face the COVID-19 outbreak in the [[Protezione Civile|Civil Protection]] situation room on 23 February. Prime Minister [[Giuseppe Conte]] and Health Minister [[Roberto Speranza]] are in the foreground, from behind]]

On 22 February, [[Conte II Cabinet|the government]] announced a new decree imposing the quarantine of more than 50,000 people from 11 municipalities in [[Northern Italy]]. The quarantine zones are called the Red Zones and the areas in Lombardy and Veneto outside of them are called the Yellow Zones.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/21/news/coronavirus_codogno_castiglione_d_adda_contagiati_misure_sicurezza-249154447/|title=Coronavirus, in dieci comuni lombardi: 50 mila persone costrette a restare in casa. Quarantena all'ospedale milanese di Baggio|date=21 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref> Penalties for violations range from a €206 fine to three months of imprisonment.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ilsole24ore.com/art/coronavirus-chi-viola-quarantena-rischia-l-arresto-fino-tre-mesi-ACrcnLLB|title=Coronavirus, come funziona la quarantena e cosa rischia chi la viola (l'arresto)|website=Il Sole 24 Ore}}</ref> The [[Italian army|Italian military]] and law enforcement agencies were instructed to secure and implement the lockdown.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-51602007|title=Venice Carnival closes amid coronavirus outbreak|date=23 February 2020|publisher=BBC}}</ref>

Schools were closed in ten municipalities in Lombardy, one in Veneto and one in Emilia Romagna. All public events were cancelled and some commercial activities{{which|date=February 2020}} were halted or were allowed to resume only until 6&nbsp;pm.<ref name="Facebook_Pavia">{{cite web|url=https://www.facebook.com/comunePV/posts/2439843176121889|title=Comune di Pavia|website=facebook.com|access-date=23 February 2020}}{{Primary source inline|date=February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_21/scuole-chiuse-il-coronavirus-lombardia-lodi-piacenza-codogno-a190ccee-54bd-11ea-9196-da7d305401b7.shtml|title=Quali sono i Comuni che hanno chiuso le scuole per il Coronavirus|last=online|first=Redazione|date=21 February 2020|website=Corriere della Sera|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref> All religious services were cancelled.<ref name="Repubblica_23Feb_Carnival">{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/23/news/coronavirus_scuole_chiuse_e_niente_carnevale_tutti_i_provvedimenti-249355737/|title=Coronavirus, scuole chiuse e niente Carnevale di Venezia. I provvedimenti Regione per Regione|date=23 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Regional train services to the most affected areas were suspended, with trains skipping stops at Codogno, [[Maleo, Lombardy|Maleo]] and Casalpusterlengo stations.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_22/coronavirus-treni-fermi-ore-lecce-milano-nessuno-stop-comuni-rischio-lodigiano-431e997c-553d-11ea-8418-2150c9ca483e.shtml|title=Coronavirus, treni fermi per ore a Lecce e Milano. I convogli non-fermano nei Comuni a rischio del Lodigiano|last=online|first=Redazione|date=22 February 2020|website=Corriere della Sera|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/22/news/coronavirus_il_comune_di_milano_sospende_dal_lavoro_i_dipendenti_che_abitano_delle_zone_coinvolte-249252812/|title=Coronavirus, per una settimana didattica sospesa nelle università lombarde. Comune di Milano e grandi aziende: i lavoratori a rischio restano a casa|date=22 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref>

People with symptoms were advised to call the [[112 (emergency telephone number)|112]] emergency number, instead of going directly to hospitals, in an effort to limit the disease's spread.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.sanmatteo.org/site/home/area-comunicazione/in-primo-piano.html|title=Coronavirus, aggiornamenti ed avvisi – Policlinico San Matteo Pavia Fondazione IRCCS|website=sanmatteo.org|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref> The [[Ministry of Health (Italy)|Ministry of Health]] provided a website and a direct line (1500) from which people could obtain the latest updates and information, as well as report suspected cases.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.salute.gov.it/nuovocoronavirus|title=Nuovo coronavirus|last=Salute|first=Ministero della|website=salute.gov.it|language=IT|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref>

Educational trips to destinations in Italy and abroad were suspended. Universities in Lombardy, Veneto, [[Trentino Alto-Adige]], Piedmont and [[Emilia-Romagna]] suspended all activities from 23 February until 1 March.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://news.unipv.it/?p=46130|title=news.unipv – Coronavirus: Sospensione delle attività didattiche dal 24/2 all'1/03|website=news.unipv|language=it-IT|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.unimi.it/it/coronavirus-misure-urgenti-la-comunita-universitaria|title=Coronavirus: misure urgenti per la comunità universitaria {{!}} Università degli Studi di Milano Statale|website=unimi.it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.unibg.it/node/9238|title=Sospensione precauzionale delle attività didattiche |publisher=Università degli studi di Bergamo |access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.unive.it/pag/14024/?tx_news_pi1%5Bnews%5D=8621&cHash=aa65321bb25bdccbf08c0c18299d48de|title=Coronavirus: lezioni ed esami sospesi dal 24/02 al 29/02|website=Università Ca' Foscari Venezia|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.unito.it/avvisi/coronavirus-aggiornamenti-sulla-gestione-della-situazione|title=Coronavirus: aggiornamenti sulla gestione della situazione|date=23 February 2020|website=Università di Torino|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://magazine.unibo.it/archivio/2020/coronavirus-sospensione-attivita-didattica-e-misure-precauzionali-contro-la-diffusione-dell2019infezione|title=Coronavirus: Sospensione Attività Didattica e misure precauzionali contro la diffusione dell'infezione|website=magazine.unibo.it|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref>{{citation overkill|date=April 2020}}

On 22 February 2020, Prime Minister [[Giuseppe Conte]] suspended all sporting events in the regions of Lombardy and Veneto, which included three [[Serie A]] football matches in those regions, as well as one in [[Piedmont]], that were to be played the following day.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.football-italia.net/150398/serie-games-suspended-coronavirus|title=Serie A games suspended for Coronavirus|publisher=Football Italia|date=22 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.football-italia.net/150407/coronavirus-also-cancels-torino-parma|title=Coronavirus also cancels Torino-Parma|publisher=Football Italia|date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.theguardian.com/football/2020/feb/23/three-serie-a-matches-coronavirus-outbreak-inter-milan|title=Four Serie A matches called off due to coronavirus outbreak|date=23 February 2020 |work=The Guardian}}</ref> The following week, six Serie A matches were initially to be played behind closed doors, but all were later suspended,<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.bbc.com/sport/football/51637700|title=Coronavirus: Five Serie A matches to be played behind closed doors|publisher=bbc.com|date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url= https://www.football-italia.net/150647/official-juventus-inter-and-others-moved|title=Official: Juventus-Inter called off and others|publisher=Football Italia|date=29 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.football-italia.net/150715/official-sampdoria-verona|title=Official: Sampdoria-Verona is off|publisher=Football Italia|date=1 March 2020}}</ref> as were two [[Coppa Italia]] matches.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.football-italia.net/150787/official-juventus-milan-postponed|title=Official: Juventus-Milan postponed|publisher=Football Italia|date=3 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.football-italia.net/150804/official-napoli-inter-postponed|title=Official: Napoli-Inter postponed|publisher=Football Italia|date=4 March 2020}}</ref>

Authorities in Veneto cancelled the last two days of the [[Carnival of Venice]] on 23 February.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-51602007|title=Venice Carnival closes amid coronavirus outbreak|date=23 February 2020|work=BBC News|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref> Authorities in Piedmont cancelled the last three days of the Carnival of [[Ivrea]].<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.lastampa.it/cronaca/2020/02/24/news/ivrea-addio-guerra-delle-arance-e-la-quarta-volta-nella-storia-1.38507893|title=Ivrea, addio guerra delle arance. È la quarta volta nella storia|date=23 February 2020|website=la Stampa|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

[[La Scala]], [[Duomo di Milano]] and [[Piccolo Teatro (Milan)|Piccolo Teatro]] in Milan, as well as [[Basilica Di San Marco]] in Venice, were closed until further notice.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/23/news/coronavirus_scala_milano_chiusure_nella_storia-249380233/|title=La Scala chiusa per il coronavirus: in più di due secoli era accaduto soltanto sei volte|date=23 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.corriere.it/notizie/cronaca/20_febbraio_23/coronavirus-chiuse-scuole-palestre-locali-guida-coprifuoco-nord-00193c74-568a-11ea-b447-d9646dbdb12a.shtml|title=Cosa è aperto, cosa no? Guida al "coprifuoco" da Coronavirus|last=Giannattasio|first=Maurizio|date=23 February 2020|website=Corriere della Sera|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.avvenire.it/chiesa/pagine/milano-l-arcivescovo-delpini-un-pensiero-di-benedizione|title=Coronavirus. Chiese aperte ma Messe sospese. La preghiera dell'arcivescovo Delpini|date=24 February 2020|website=Avvenire|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref> A [[Giorgio Armani]] fashion show, which was scheduled on Sunday, the last day of [[Milan Fashion Week]] 2020, went ahead without any media or buyers present; it was instead streamed live online.<ref>{{Cite news|last=Luke Leitch|url=https://www.vogue.com/article/giorgio-armani-to-hold-empty-show-following-italian-coronavirus-outbreak|title=Giorgio Armani to Hold Empty Show Following Italian Coronavirus Outbreak|work=Vogue|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|agency=Associated Press|url=https://www.telegraph.co.uk/news/2020/02/23/giorgio-armani-cancels-milan-fashion-week-show-virus-fears/|title=Giorgio Armani cancels Milan Fashion Week show over coronavirus fears|date=23 February 2020|work=The Telegraph|access-date=23 February 2020|issn=0307-1235}}</ref>

In addition to the emergency phone numbers 112 and 118, new dedicated numbers were added for the different regions – Lombardy 800894545, [[Campania]] 800909699, Veneto 800462340, Piedmont 800333444 and Emilia-Romagna 800033033.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.fanpage.it/attualita/coronavirus-quali-sono-i-numeri-di-telefono-di-ministero-e-regione-da-chiamare-in-caso-di-sintomi/|title=Coronavirus, quali sono i numeri di telefono di Ministero e Regione da chiamare in caso di sintomi|website=Fanpage|language=it|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.regione.emilia-romagna.it/notizie/attualita/come-prevenire-il-rischio-di-contagio|title=Nuovo coronavirus, come prevenire il rischio di contagio|website=Regione Emilia-Romagna|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref name=autogenerated1>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/23/news/coronavirus_scuole_chiuse_e_niente_carnevale_tutti_i_provvedimenti-249355737/|title=Coronavirus, scuole chiuse e niente Carnevale di Venezia. Supermarkets in Lombardy and Emilia-Romagna were emptied by customers as residents stockpiled food and supplies.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ilrestodelcarlino.it/bologna/cronaca/coronavirus-supermercati-vuoti-1.5045265|title=Coronavirus Bologna, razzia ai supermercati. On 24 February 500 additional police officers were assigned to patrol the quarantined areas in [[Lodi, Lombardy|Lodi]] and Veneto.<ref name="Repubblica_24Feb" /> Additional toll-free numbers were added for other regions — [[Valle D'Aosta]] 800122121, [[Trentino-Alto Adige/Südtirol|Trentino Alto Adige]] 800751751, [[Friuli Venezia Giulia]] 800500300, [[Tuscany|Toscana]] 800556060, [[Umbria]] 800636363, [[Marche]] 800936677 and [[Lazio]] 800118800.<ref name="TollFree" />

The governor of [[Basilicata]], [[Vito Bardi]], instituted a mandatory 14-day quarantine for people arriving from areas in Northern Italy affected by the outbreak.<ref name="Repubblica_24Feb">{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/24/news/coronavirus_149_i_casi_confermati_conte_i_contagi_possono_crescere_-249427098/|title=Coronavirus, quarto morto, è un 84enne di Bergamo. Sette regioni coinvolte per 30 milioni di italiani|date=24 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref> The Ministry of Health announced that it had engaged 31 laboratories in Italy to carry out the analysis of swabs from suspected COVID-19 cases.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/coronavirus-il-ministero-della-salute-ha-aggiornato-la-circolare-con-le-nuove-disposizioni-analisi-in-31-laboratori_15196699-202002a.shtml|title=Coronavirus, il ministero della Salute ha aggiornato la circolare con le nuove disposizioni: analisi in 31 laboratori|website=Tgcom24|language=IT|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref> Minister [[Roberto Speranza]] appointed Walter Ricciardi, a member of [[World Health Organization]]'s executive committee and former president of [[Istituto Superiore di Sanità|Italian National Institute of Health]], as a special adviser for relations between Italy and international health organisations.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/24/news/coronavirus_speranza_nomina_walter_ricciardi_come_consigliere_e_alle_regioni_dice_no_a_scelte_unilaterali_-249447649/|title=Coronavirus, Speranza nomina Walter Ricciardi come consigliere e alle Regioni dice: "No a scelte unilaterali"|date=24 February 2020|website=la Repubblica}}</ref> Filming of ''[[Mission: Impossible 7]]'' starring [[Tom Cruise]] in Venice was halted.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.thewrap.com/mission-impossible-vii-halts-production-in-italy-due-to-coronavirus-outbreak/|title='Mission: Impossible VII' Halts Production in Italy Due to Coronavirus Outbreak|date=24 February 2020|website=TheWrap|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

Major companies such as [[IBM]], [[Enel]], [[Luxottica]], [[PwC]] and [[Vodafone]] continued to allow employees to work from home. [[Generali Tower]] in Milan and [[Palazzo Madama]] in Rome installed thermal scanners to measure temperatures of visitors and employees.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.finanza.com/Finanza/Notizie_Italia/Italia/notizia/Coronavirus_Italia_Enel_ricorre_allo_smart_working_General-516928|title=Coronavirus Italia: Enel ricorre allo smart working. Multiple regions in Italy such as [[Liguria]], Trentino Alto Adige, Friuli Venezia Giulia, [[Abruzzo]] and Marche decided to close all schools and universities for two days to a week. Court proceedings were postponed until further notice.<ref name=autogenerated1 />

The [[FTSE MIB]] Index fell by 6% and other stock market indices across Europe were also affected.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.marketwatch.com/story/italian-stocks-set-to-lead-sharp-decline-for-european-equities-as-coronavirus-spreads-2020-02-24|title=Italian stocks slump nearly 6% as European equities crumble on spreading coronavirus|last=Goldstein|first=Barbara Kollmeyer, Steve|website=MarketWatch|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Over 300,000 calls per day were logged on Lombardy's toll-free line as well as the emergency number 112.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/25/news/coronavirus_milano_codogno_lombardia_contagi_morti_chiamate_numeri_emergenza-249521977/|title=L'assalto ai centralini per la paura coronavirus: 300mila chiamate in un giorno al numero di emergenza della Lombardia|date=25 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Some of the residents inside the Red Zone managed to leave the quarantined areas daily, bypassing the checkpoints by going through back roads.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/25/news/la_zona_rossa_i_ribelli_di_codogno_violiamo_i_blocchi_per_sopravvivere_-249506911/|title=Codogno, i ribelli della zona rossa: "Violiamo i blocchi per sopravvivere"|date=24 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.dw.com/en/coronavirus-life-around-italys-quarantined-red-zone/a-52513830|title=Coronavirus: Life around Italy's quarantined 'red zone' {{!}} DW {{!}} 24 February 2020|website=Deutsche Welle|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

Walters]] issued a travel ban covering the areas of Italy affected by the outbreak for US service members and their families.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.rollcall.com/2020/02/25/coronavirus-threatens-u-s-military-base-operations-in-europe-general-says/|title=Coronavirus threatens U.S. military base operations in Europe, general says|website=Roll Call|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Driver's licence exams were suspended in Lombardy and Veneto.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.ansa.it/lombardia/notizie/2020/02/25/coronavirus-sospesi-gli-esami-patente_82f235e4-e57a-42c7-ad4d-4e297fb259b8.html|title=Coronavirus: sospesi gli esami per la patente – Lombardia|date=25 February 2020|website=Agenzia ANSA|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> The number of checkpoints in the Red Zones was increased from 15 to 35, and army personnel were sent to help staff the checkpoints.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.ansa.it/sito/notizie/cronaca/2020/02/25/check-point-zona-rossaarriva-lesercito_651efc33-6cb3-48ff-ac84-aec43486a570.html|title=Check-point zona rossa,arriva l'Esercito – Cronaca|date=25 February 2020|website=Agenzia ANSA|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

The [[Italian Basketball Federation]] suspended all of its championship games, including [[Lega Basket Serie A]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.raisport.rai.it/articoli/2020/02/basket-A-A2-maschile-femminile-6592d551-065e-4245-931a-488e53809874.html|title=Basket: la Fip sospende la serie A, A2, B maschile, A1 e A2 donne – Rai Sport|website=RaiSport}}</ref>
