[[Morgan Stanley]], [[Barclays]], [[Mediobanca]] and [[UniCredit]] requested their Milan staff to work from home.<ref name="Reuters_banks" />

Multiple fairs and exhibitions were rescheduled. [[Milan Furniture Fair|Salone del Mobile]] was postponed to 16 to 21 June.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ilsole24ore.com/art/coronavirus-salone-mobile-rinviato-giugno-AClPZvLB|title=Coronavirus, Salone del Mobile rinviato a giugno|website=Il Sole 24 Ore|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Bologna Children's Book Fair was rescheduled to 4 to 7 May.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.bookfair.bolognafiere.it/|title=Bologna Children's Book Fair|last=Fiere|first=Bologna|website=Bologna Children bookfair|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Cosmoprof Worldwide Bologna, a cosmetic fair, was rescheduled to 11 to 15 June.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.cosmoprof.com/en/official-updates/|title=Official updates|last=COSMOPROF|website=COSMOPROF|access-date=25 February 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200225201203/https://www.cosmoprof.com/en/official-updates/|archive-date=25 February 2020|url-status=dead}}</ref> Expocasa, a furniture fair in Turin, was rescheduled initially to 28 March to 5 April but later to future date to be announced later.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://torino.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/25/news/coronavirus_expocasa_rinviata_la_fiera_dell_arredamento_si_terra_dal_28_marzo_al_5_aprile-249565043/|title=Coronavirus, Expocasa rinviata, la fiera dell'arredamento si terrà dal 28 marzo al 5 aprile|date=25 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web |title=Aggiornamenti Corona Virus – Rinvio Manifestazione |url=https://www.expocasa.it/3796/aggiornamenti-corona-virus |website=Expocasa |accessdate=20 March 2020}}</ref> Roma Motodays was postponed to 17 to 19 April.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/motori/sezioni/moto/2020/02/25/news/motodays_coronavirus_rinvio-249562967/|title=Effetto Coronavirus: rinviato a Roma il Motodays|date=25 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

Italy opened a probe into skyrocketing online prices for masks and sanitising gels. Police issued warnings that criminals were using false identities and posing as health inspectors to gain access to people's homes to steal money, jewellery and other valuables.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/china-health-italy-probe-idUSL5N2AP37X|title=Italy probes "insane" prices for coronavirus masks, sanitizers|date=25 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

On 26 February, Director of the Italian National Institute of Health Franco Locatelli announced that swabbing would only be performed on symptomatic patients, as 95% of the swabs previously tested were negative.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://tg24.sky.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/coronavirus-tamponi-solo-su-sintomatici.html|title=Coronavirus, Consiglio superiore sanità: tamponi solo su sintomatici {{!}} Sky TG24|website=tg24.sky.it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

The [[Italian Minister of University and Research]], [[Gaetano Manfredi]], announced that online lessons would be delivered to students in areas affected by the outbreak starting on 2 March.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.miur.gov.it/web/guest/-/coronavirus-manfredi-universita-da-lunedi-lezioni-on-line-per-gli-studenti-delle-aree-colpite-primo-passo-verso-la-normalita-|title=Coronavirus, Manfredi, Università: "Da lunedì lezioni on line per gli studenti delle aree colpite, primo passo verso la normalità" – Coronavirus, Manfredi, Università: "Da lunedì lezioni on line per gli studenti delle aree colpite, primo passo verso la normalità"|website=Miur – Ministero dell'istruzione – Ministero dell'università e della ricerca|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> [[Palermo]] and [[Naples]] closed all schools until 29 February.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://napoli.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/coronavirus_a_napoli_scuole_chiuse_fino_a_sabato-249615433/|title=Coronavirus: a Napoli scuole chiuse fino a sabato 29 febbraio|date=26 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.blogsicilia.it/palermo/coronavirus-scuole-chiuse-palermo-ordinanza-regione/520347/|title=Scuole chiuse fino a lunedì a Palermo e Provincia, arriva l'ordinanza regionale|date=25 February 2020|website=BlogSicilia – Ultime notizie dalla Sicilia|language=it-IT|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> The [[University of Basilicata]] installed a thermal scanner and continued all teaching activities as per normal.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.ansa.it/basilicata/notizie/2020/02/26/coronavirus-scanner-termico-allunibas_1147963f-0e34-4dbe-96a9-4e76a15b5264.html|title=Coronavirus: scanner termico all'Unibas – Basilicata|date=26 February 2020|website=Agenzia ANSA|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> The [[University of Bari]] suspended all medical- and health-related internships for medical and healthcare students.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://bari.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/coronavirus_sospesi_i_tirocini_per_gli_studenti_di_medicina_di_bari-249627906/|title=Coronavirus, sospesi i tirocini di Medicina a Bari. Gli studenti: "Spiegateci il perché"|date=26 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> [[Polytechnic University of Milan|Politecnico di Milano]] conducted thesis mentoring for more than one thousand students graduating the following week using [[Skype]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/coronavirus_in_lombardia_al_politecnico_di_milano_la_tesi_di_laurea_si_discute_via_skype-249628719/|title=Coronavirus in Lombardia, al Politecnico di Milano la tesi di laurea si discute via Skype|date=26 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

The [[Italian Winter Sports Federation]] decided to proceed with the Women's World Cup alpine skiing races at [[La Thuile, Aosta Valley]] on 29 February.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://torino.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/coronavirus_confermate_le_gare_della_coppa_del_mondo_di_sci_femminile_a_la_thuile-249617192/|title=Coronavirus, confermate le gare della coppa del mondo di sci femminile a La Thuile|date=26 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> The MIDO Milan Eyewear Show was rescheduled to 5 to 7 July.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.wmido.com/ita-la-50a-edizione-di-mido-si-terra-dal-5-al-7-luglio/|title=MIDO 2020 will take place from July 5 to the 7 at Rho Fiera Milano – WMido|website=wmido.com|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

On 27 February, [[Taranto]], Apulia closed all schools until 29 February.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.primocircolotaranto.gov.it/wordpress/ordinanza-n-13-comune-di-taranto-chiusura-scuole-per-le-giornate-del-27-28-e-29-febbraio-2020/|title=Ordinanza n. 13 -Comune di Taranto chiusura scuole per le giornate del 27 28 e 29 febbraio 2020 – Istituto Comprensivo Renato Moro|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> Multiple schools were closed in Roseto degli Abruzzi.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.abruzzolive.it/coronavirus-turista-positivo-chiuse-scuole-a-roseto-in-ricostruzione-movimenti-del-paziente-brianzolo/|title=Coronavirus, turista positivo: chiuse scuole a Roseto. In ricostruzione movimenti del paziente brianzolo|website=AbruzzoLive|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> [[D'Annunzio University of Chieti–Pescara|D'Annunzio University]] suspended all activities until 29 February.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.scuolainforma.it/2020/02/26/aggiornamento-coronavirus-al-26-2-per-ogni-regione-altre-scuole-chiuse-nuovo-decreto.html|title=Aggiornamento Coronavirus al 26/2 per ogni regione: altre scuole chiuse, decreto con nuove misure|date=26 February 2020|website=ScuolaInforma|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> Cartoocomics Fair in Milan was rescheduled to 2 to 4 October.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://it.finance.yahoo.com/notizie/coronavirus-fiera-milano-posticipa-cartoomics-al-2-4-104522157.html|title=Coronavirus, Fiera Milano posticipa Cartoomics al 2–4 ottobre|publisher=Yahoo! Finance|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> The Winter Rescue Race in [[Piedmont]] was cancelled.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.unionemonregalese.it/2020/02/27/annullata-coronavirus-winter-rescue-race-artesina/|title=Artesina: le gare di Soccorso alpino annullate per l'emergenza coronavirus|last=Monregalese|first=Redazione Unione|date=27 February 2020|website=L'Unione Monregalese|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> [[University of Bologna]] planned to set up a remote teaching project in which exams and lessons would be delivered to students online, to be partially completed on 2 March.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://bologna.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/27/news/coronavirus_universita_di_bologna_lezioni_esami_e_lauree_on_line-249716958/|title=Coronavirus, Università di Bologna: lezioni, esami e lauree on line|date=27 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> [[Messina]] closed all schools from 29 February to 3 March.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.strettoweb.com/2020/02/coronavirus-messina-scuole/976298/|title=Messina, scuole chiuse per il Coronavirus: ecco l'ordinanza del sindaco|date=27 February 2020|website=Stretto Web|language=it-IT|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref>

On 28 February, during an interview with [[Rai News24]], Professor Massimo Galli from the Luigi Sacco Hospital in Milan suggested that the majority of newly recorded cases were pre-existing cases that were finally detected during the extensive tests performed on people (and their relatives) who had come in contact with confirmed patients.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.rainews.it/dl/rainews/media/ContentItem-81824682-be63-4c83-a220-ae2b5630732b.html|title=Massimo Galli: il virus circolava già prima dei casi conclamati|website=Rainews|language=it|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref> The rapid increase of positive cases was the result of the blanket testing approach that was deployed following the first confirmed case in Codogno.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/28/news/_polmoniti_anomale_a_meta_gennaio_cosi_e_nato_il_focolaio_di_codogno_-249759796/|title=Coronavirus, polmoniti anomale a metà gennaio: "Così è nato il focolaio di Codogno"|date=27 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

The Ministry of Health announced new guidelines for reporting cases. It would no longer report asymptomatic cases (positive swabs taken from patients who were not showing symptoms), which had counted as 40 to 50% of all reported cases at the time. These people would undergo isolation at home and would be followed up with new tests until they were negative.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/28/news/cambia_il_metodo_di_conteggio_esclusi_i_positivi_asintomatici-249765660/|title=Cambia il metodo di conteggio: esclusi i positivi asintomatici|date=27 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://abcnews.go.com/Health/wireStory/italy-virus-count-methods-agencys-urging-69254949|title=Italy blasts virus panic as it eyes new testing criteria|website=ABC News|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref> Universities in Lombardy extended their closure until 7 March.<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" />

===Nationwide measures===
On 1 March, the Council of Ministers approved a decree to organise the containment of the outbreak. In the decree, the Italian national territory was divided into three areas:<ref>{{cite news |title=Il governo firma il decreto coronavirus: l'Italia divisa in 3 zone |url=https://www.repubblica.it/politica/2020/03/01/news/coronavirus_misure_governo-249980561/ |accessdate=2 March 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=1 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref>
[[File:Covid-19 pandemic in Italy lockdown and lifting.png|thumb|350px|The number of new cases and deaths per day in Italy from COVID-19 showing the effects of lockdown and lifting]]
* A red zone (composed of the municipalities of Bertonico, Casalpusterlengo, Castelgerundo, Castiglione D'Adda, Codogno, Fombio, Maleo, San Fiorano, Somaglia and Terranova dei Passerini in Lombardy, and the municipality of [[Vo']] in Veneto), where the whole population is in quarantine.
* A yellow zone (composed of the regions of Lombardy, Veneto and Emilia-Romagna), where social and sports events are suspended and schools, theatres, clubs, and cinemas are closed.
* The rest of the national territory, where safety and prevention measures are advertised in public places and special sanitisations are performed on means of public transport.

On 4 March, the Italian government imposed the shutdown of all schools and universities nationwide for two weeks as the country reached 100 deaths from the outbreak.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Guerzoni |first1=Monica |title=Scuole e università di tutta Italia chiuse fino a metà marzo per il coronavirus |url=https://www.corriere.it/scuola/20_marzo_04/coronavirus-scuole-chiuse-tutta-italia-decisione-governo-entro-stasera-e7ba0614-5e12-11ea-8e26-25d9a5210d01.shtml |accessdate=4 March 2020 |work=Corriere della Sera |date=3 April 2020 |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|last1=Palermo|first1=Angela Giuffrida Lorenzo Tondo in|url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/04/italy-orders-closure-of-schools-and-universities-due-to-coronavirus|title=Italy orders closure of all schools and universities due to coronavirus|date=4 March 2020|work=The Guardian|access-date=5 March 2020|last2=Beaumont|first2=Peter|issn=0261-3077}}</ref> The same day, the government ruled that all sporting events in Italy would be played behind closed doors until 3 April.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.football-italia.net/150823/official-behind-closed-doors-until-april-3|title=Official: Behind closed doors until April 3|publisher=Football Italia|date=4 March 2020}}</ref>

On 5 March, when the newly appointed [[Emilia-Romagna]] regional minister of health, Raffale Donini, tested positive for COVID-19, Governor [[Stefano Bonaccini]] appointed Sergio Venturi as commissioner for the emergency. Venturi was the regional minister of health until February 2020.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://gazzettadireggio.gelocal.it/reggio/cronaca/2020/03/05/news/coronavirus-positivo-l-assessore-donini-torna-in-campo-l-ex-venturi-1.38553828|title=Coronavirus, positivo l'assessore Donini: torna in campo l'ex Venturi &#124; A Reggio Emilia undici casi in più: adesso sono 31|date=5 March 2020|website=Gazzetta di Reggio|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref>

[[File:COVID19 avvisi a Bologna.jpg|left|thumb|Montage of notices on shops in Bologna declaring their temporary closure, or requiring people to stay at least one metre apart]]
In the night between 7 and 8 March, the government approved a decree to lock down Lombardy and 14 other provinces in Veneto, Emilia-Romagna, Piedmont and Marche, involving more than 16&nbsp; million people.<ref name="bbc_lombardy_lockdown">{{cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-middle-east-51787238|title=Northern Italy quarantines 16 million people|work=BBC News|date=8 March 2020|accessdate=8 March 2020|via=bbc.com}}</ref> The decree "absolutely avoided any movement into and out of the areas" and, like the previous one, it provided sanctions of up to three months in prison for those who violated the lockdown.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.wsj.com/articles/italy-plans-large-scale-lockdown-in-countrys-north-to-fight-coronavirus-11583613874|title=Italy Locks Down the Country's North to Fight Coronavirus|first=Eric Sylvers and Giovanni|last=Legorano|date=8 March 2020|accessdate=8 March 2020|work=The Wall Street Journal}}</ref> It was possible to move into and out of the areas only for emergencies or "proven working needs", which must be authorised by the [[prefect]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/08/news/coronavirus_i_decreti_del_governo-250617415/|title=Coronavirus, il decreto del governo: tutte le misure per la zona arancione e quelle per il resto d'Italia|date=8 March 2020|website=la Repubblica|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref> The decree also established the closure of all gyms, swimming pools, spas and wellness centres. Shopping centres had to be closed on weekends, while other commercial activities could remain open if a distance of one metre between customers could be guaranteed.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.romatoday.it/attualita/coronavirus-pub-cinema-teatri-locali-chiusi-nuovo-decreto.html|title=Coronavirus: stop a pub, cinema, teatro e discoteche anche a Roma. Ecco cosa prevede il nuovo decreto|website=RomaToday|language=it|access-date=8 March 2020}}</ref> The decree imposed the closure of museums, cultural centres and ski resorts in the lockdown areas and the closure of cinemas, theatres, pubs, dance schools, game rooms, betting rooms and [[Bingo (American version)|bingo]] halls, [[disco]]s and similar places in the entire country.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.romatoday.it/attualita/coronavirus-pub-cinema-teatri-locali-chiusi-nuovo-decreto.html|title=Coronavirus: stop a pub, cinema, teatro e discoteche anche a Roma. Ecco cosa prevede il nuovo decreto|website=RomaToday|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref> Civil and religious ceremonies, including funeral ceremonies, were suspended. All organised events were also suspended, as well as events in public or private places, including those of a cultural, recreational, sporting and religious nature, even if held in closed places.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://corrieredellumbria.corr.it/news/coronavirus/1516428/emergenza-coronavirus-bozza-decreto-sospesi-anche--funerali-in-lombardia-e-11-province-covi19-epidemia-contagio.html|title=Emergenza Coronavirus, bozza decreto: sospesi anche i funerali in Lombardia e 11 province|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref> This measure was described as the largest lockdown in the history of Europe,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/03/08/world/europe/italy-coronavirus-quarantine.html|title=On Day 1 of Lockdown, Italian Officials Urge Citizens to Abide by Rules|first1=Jason|last1=Horowitz|first2=Emma|last2=Bubola|date=8 March 2020|accessdate=10 March 2020|work=The New York Times}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.theverge.com/2020/3/7/21169637/italy-lockdown-lombardy-coronavirus-outbreak|title=Italy locks down northern region in response to coronavirus outbreak|first=Kim|last=Lyons|date=7 March 2020|website=The Verge|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref> as well as the most aggressive response taken in any region beyond China, and paralysed the wealthiest parts of the country as Italy attempted to constrain the rapid spread of the disease.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Horowitz |first1=Jason |title=Italy Locks Down Much of the Country's North Over the Coronavirus |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/03/07/world/europe/coronavirus-italy.html|accessdate=8 March 2020 |work=The New York Times |date=7 March 2020}}</ref><ref name=Italia>[https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/europe/italy-coronavirus-milan-lombardy-lockdowns/2020/03/07/403fcea2-60b3-11ea-ac50-18701e14e06d_story.html To contain coronavirus, Italy will restrict movement across much of its northern region, including the city of Milan], ''[[The Washington Post]]'', Chico Harlan and Stefano Pitrelli, 7 March 2020. Retrieved 8 March 2020.</ref>

Riots broke out in many penitentiaries throughout Italy after restrictions on [[conjugal visit]]s were imposed by the government in the 8 March decree.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/italian-prisoners-riot-over-coronavirus-restrictions/|title=Italian prisoners riot over coronavirus restrictions|website=The Times of Israel|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref> Nine prisoners died in [[Modena]] and three in [[Rieti]],<ref>{{cite web|url=https://bologna.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/09/news/modena_sei_morti_nella_rivolta_in_carcere-250719903/|title=Modena, sette detenuti morti nella rivolta in carcere e sei in prognosi riservata|date=9 March 2020|website=la Repubblica|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/10/news/coronavirus_carceri_ancora_proteste_tre_detenuti_morti_a_rieti-250829816/|title=Coronavirus, carceri, ancora proteste. Tre detenuti morti a Rieti, le vittime salgono a dodici|date=10 March 2020|website=la Repubblica|accessdate=11 March 2020}}</ref> while 76 detainees escaped from [[Foggia]]'s penitentiary.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.ansa.it/sito/notizie/cronaca/2020/03/09/rivolta-in-carcere-foggiaalcuni-evadono_1e2d031d-d354-4076-8129-bdccaed5fa23.html|title=Rivolta in carcere Foggia,alcuni evadono – Cronaca|date=9 March 2020|website=Agenzia ANSA|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://bari.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/09/news/coronavirus_detenuti_evadono_dal_carcere_di_foggia_e_vengono_bloccati_all_esterno-250720580/|title=Coronavirus, rivolta nelle carceri: a Foggia evasione di massa. A Trani e Bari strade bloccate|date=9 March 2020|website=la Repubblica|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://abcnews.go.com/Health/wireStory/italian-inmates-die-protest-virus-measures-69482325|title=Prison riots hit Italy amid virus; 6 die in overdose|date=9 March 2020|work=ABC News|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref> Two prison agents were assaulted and kidnapped in [[Pavia]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/03/08/coronavirus-rivolta-nelle-carceri-a-pavia-sequestrati-2-agenti-modena-morto-un-detenuto-proteste-pure-a-frosinone-napoli-e-palermo/5729730/|title=Coronavirus, rivolta nelle carceri: a Pavia sequestrati 2 agenti. Modena, morti tre detenuti. Proteste pure a Frosinone, Napoli e Palermo|date=8 March 2020|website=Il Fatto Quotidiano|accessdate=10 March 2020}}</ref> On 9 March in [[Bologna]], detainees took control of the Dozza penitentiary, forcing personnel to exit the building.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.facebook.com/search/top/?q=ètv&epa=SEARCH_BOX|title=Rivolta anche al carcere di Bologna|accessdate=10 March 2020}}{{Primary source inline|date=April 2020}}</ref> On 11 March, two prisoners were found dead in Bologna's penitentiary.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://bologna.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/11/news/detenuto_morto_dozza-250944868/|title=Rivolta nel carcere di Bologna: morto un detenuto|date=11 March 2020|website=la Repubblica|accessdate=12 March 2020}}</ref> In total, fourteen prisoners died in the whole country.<ref>[https://ilmanifesto.it/carceri-14-i-detenuti-morti-ma-bonafede-si-autoassolve/ Carceri, 14 i detenuti morti. Ma Bonafede si autoassolve], ''il manifesto''</ref>

On 9 March, the government announced that all sporting events in Italy would be cancelled until at least 3 April, but the ban does not include Italian clubs or national teams participating in international competitions.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/sport/51808683|title=Coronavirus: All sport in Italy to be suspended because of outbreak|date=9 March 2020|work=BBC Sport|access-date=9 March 2020}}</ref> In the evening, Conte announced in a press conference that all measures previously applied only in the so-called "red zones" had been extended to the whole country, putting approximately 60 million people in lockdown. Conte later proceeded to officially sign the new executive decree.<ref name="cnn_italy_lockdown">{{cite news |last1=Reynolds |first1=Emma |last2=Picheta |first2=Rob |title=All of Italy is in lockdown as coronavirus cases rise |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2020/03/09/europe/coronavirus-italy-lockdown-intl/index.html |accessdate=9 March 2020 |publisher=CNN |date=9 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Tondo |first1=Lorenzo |title=Coronavirus: Italian PM extends lockdown to entire country |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/09/coronavirus-italy-prime-minister-country-lockdown?utm_term=Autofeed&CMP=twt_gu&utm_medium&utm_source=Twitter#Echobox=1583793579 |accessdate=9 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=9 March 2020}}</ref>

[[File:Ian Art Photography - Italy 100 people queuing at a supermarket during coronavirus outbreak mar-2020.jpg|thumb|upright=1.13|Queue in front of a supermarket after the introduction of [[social distancing]] rules]]
On 11 March, the government allocated 25&nbsp;billion euros for the emergency.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/economia/2020/03/11/news/emergenza_coronavirus_conferenza_stampa_conte_misure_economiche-250924846/|title=Emergenza coronavirus, il piano del governo sale a 25 miliardi. Gualtieri alla Ue: 'Servono stimoli'|date=11 March 2020|website=la Repubblica|accessdate=12 March 2020}}</ref> In the evening, Conte announced a tightening of the lockdown, with all commercial and retail businesses except those providing essential services, like grocery shops and pharmacies, closed down.<ref name=":13" /><ref name=":12" /><ref>{{cite web |title=Coronavirus Measures |url=https://www.repubblica.it/politica/2020/03/11/news/coronavirus_conte_italia_governo_misure-250988471/?ref=RHPPTP-BL-I250988111-C12-P1-S1.12-T1 |website=La Repubblica |date = 11 March 2020|accessdate=11 March 2020}}</ref> He also appointed Domenico Arcuri as Delegated Commissioner for the Emergency. Arcuri will cooperate with Commissioner [[Angelo Borrelli]] with the aim of strengthening the distribution of [[intensive care unit|intensive care]] equipment.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.fanpage.it/attualita/coronavirus-il-governo-nominera-domenico-arcuri-commissario-delegato-per-lemergenza/|title=Coronavirus: chi è Domenico Arcuri, il commissario delegato per l'emergenza scelto da Conte|website=Fanpage|accessdate=12 March 2020}}</ref>

On 19 March, the [[Italian Army|Army]] was deployed to the city of [[Bergamo]], the worst hit Italian city by the coronavirus, as the local authorities can no longer process the number of dead residents. The city's mayor [[Giorgio Gori]] said the true number of dead could be much higher than reported.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.adnkronos.com/fatti/cronaca/2020/03/18/coronavirus-gori-tanti-muoiono-casa-non-vengono-contati_tLagSTNm9fczG1a59ZhosI.html|title=Coronavirus, Gori: "Tanti muoiono in casa, non vengono contati"|website=Adnkronos}}</ref> Army trucks transported bodies to [[crematorium]]s in several other cities, as cemeteries in the city were full.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://news.sky.com/story/coronavirus-italian-army-called-in-to-carry-away-corpses-as-citys-crematorium-is-overwhelmed-11959994|title=Coronavirus: Italian army called in as crematorium struggles to cope with deaths|publisher=Sky News}}</ref> On the following day, the Army was called in to assist the police forces in enforcing the lockdown.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Di Donato |first1=Valentina |last2=Ruotolo |first2=Nicola |last3=Smith-Spark |first3=Laura |title=Italy calls in military to enforce lockdown as 627 people die in 24 hours |url=https://edition.cnn.com/2020/03/20/europe/italy-military-coronavirus-intl/index.html |accessdate=21 March 2020 |publisher=CNN |date=20 March 2020}}</ref>

On 20 March, the Ministry of Health ordered tighter regulations on free movement. The new measures banned open-air sports and running, except individually and in close proximity of one's residence. Parks, playgrounds, and public green were closed down. Furthermore, movement across the country was further restricted, by banning "any movement towards a residence different from the main one", including holiday homes, during weekends and holidays.<ref>{{cite news |title=Le nuove restrizioni decise dal governo |url=https://www.ilpost.it/2020/03/20/ordinanza-coronavirus-attivita-sportiva-correre/ |accessdate=21 March 2020 |work=Il Post |date=20 March 2020 |language=it-IT}}</ref>

On 21 March, Conte announced further restrictions within the nationwide lockdown, by halting all non-essential production, industries and businesses in Italy, following the rise in the number of new cases and deaths in the previous days.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Farrer |first1=Martin |title=Italy: PM warns of worst crisis since WW2 as coronavirus deaths leap by almost 800 |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/22/italian-pm-warns-of-worst-crisis-since-ww2-as-coronavirus-deaths-leap-by-almost-800 |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=22 March 2020}}</ref> This measure had also been strongly asked for by multiple institutions, including trade unions, mayors, and regional presidents, as well as medical professionals, but was initially opposed by the industrialists.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, i sindaci toscani scrivono a Conte: "Chiudere tutto ciò che non è essenziale" |url=https://www.lanazione.it/cronaca/coronavirus-sindaci-toscana-chiudere-tutto-1.5076824 |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=La Nazione |date=21 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title='Chiudere fabbriche', 41 sindaci a Conte – Abruzzo |url=http://www.ansa.it/abruzzo/notizie/2020/03/17/chiudere-fabbriche-41-sindaci-a-conte_2b8aaf8a-15de-46a2-ae61-5baa6389fb36.html |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=Agenzia ANSA |date=17 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Chiudere le fabbriche? La lettera dei sindacati |url=https://www.repubblica.it/economia/2020/03/21/news/chiudere_le_fabbriche_la_lettera_dei_sindacati-251916540/ |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=21 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=I medici della Lombardia: "Chiudere tutte le attività non essenziali". Il no degli industriali |url=https://www.huffingtonpost.it/entry/gli-industriali-dicono-no-alla-chiusura-delle-fabbriche_it_5e68d0eec5b60557280e9304 |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=L'HuffPost |date=11 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, Milano trema: 634 casi in un giorno. Fontana chiama Conte: chiudere tutto, Esercito per strada |url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/italia/coronavirus_milano_casi_contagi_lombardia_ultime_notizie-5121166.html |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=Il Messaggero |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=De Angelis |first1=Alessandro |title="Chiudete tutto, anche le fabbriche" (di A. De Angelis) |url=https://www.huffingtonpost.it/entry/giorgio-gori-chiudete-tutto-anche-le-fabbriche_it_5e74ad81c5b63c3b648e6263 |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=L'HuffPost |date=20 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref>{{citation overkill|date=April 2020}}

On 24 March, in a live-streamed press conference, Conte announced a new decree approved by the Council of Ministers. The decree imposed higher fines for the violation of the restrictive measures, and regulation of the relationship between government and Parliament during the emergency. It included also the possibility of reducing or suspending public and private transport, and gave the regional governments power to impose additional restrictive regulations in their Regions for a maximum of seven days before being confirmed by national decree.<ref>{{cite news |title=Italy announces fines of up to €3,000 for breaking quarantine rules |url=https://www.thelocal.it/20200324/italy-announces-fines-of-up-to-3000-for-breaking-quarantine-rules |accessdate=25 March 2020 |work=thelocal.it |date=24 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Cosa ha detto Giuseppe Conte |url=https://www.ilpost.it/2020/03/24/decreto-restrizioni-sanzioni-coronavirus/ |accessdate=25 March 2020 |work=Il Post |date=24 March 2020 |language=it-IT}}</ref>

On 1 April, the government extended the period of lockdown until 13 April, with health minister Speranza saying that the restrictive measures had begun to yield the first positive results.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Henley |first1=Jon |title=Italy extends lockdown amid signs coronavirus infection rate is easing |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/apr/01/italy-extends-lockdown-amid-signs-coronavirus-infection-rate-is-easing |accessdate=1 April 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=1 April 2020}}</ref>
[[File:Pavia, Italia (49937550568).jpg|thumb|240px|People in [[Pavia]] wearing protective masks]]
On 6 April, the government announced a new economic stimulus plan, consisting of €200 billion of state-guaranteed loans to companies and additional €200 billion of guarantees to support exports.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Leali |first1=Giorgio |title=Italy adopts €400B liquidity plan amid coronavirus crisis |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/italy-adopts-e400b-liquidity-plan-amid-coronavirus-crisis/ |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=Politico |date=6 April 2020}}</ref>

On 7 April, after more than a month of suspension, the [[Italian Basketball Federation]] officially ended the 2019–20 [[Lega Basket Serie A|LBA]] season, without assigning the title.<ref>[https://sportando.basketball/en/italian-basketball-federation-officially-ends-lba-2019-20-season/ Italian Basketball Federation officially ends LBA 2019-20 season], Sportando</ref>

On 8 April, a government's decree closed all Italian ports until 31 July, stating that they do not ensure the necessary requirements for the classification and definition of "safe place", established by the [[Hamburg Rules]] on maritime search and rescue."<ref>[https://www.huffingtonpost.it/entry/litalia-chiude-i-porti_it_5e8d89f2c5b6e1d10a6c2671?yhj&utm_hp_ref=it-homepage L'Italia chiude i porti], ''Huffington Post''</ref>

On 10 April, Conte announced the prolongation of the lockdown until 3 May, as well as the reopening of some businesses like bookshops and forestry.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/04/10/news/coronavirus_giuseppe_conte_riaperture-253677426/|title=Coronavirus, il premier Conte: "Chiusura fino al 3 maggio, non possiamo cedere adesso"|date=10 April 2020|website=la Repubblica}}</ref>

On 26 April, the Prime Minister announced a starter plan for the so-called "phase 2", that would start from 4 May. Movements across regions would still be forbidden, while the ones between municipalities would be allowed only for work and health reasons, as well as for visits to relatives. The plan allowed the re-opening of manufacturing industries and construction sites, however schools, bars, restaurants and hairdressers would stay closed.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus: Italy's PM outlines lockdown easing measures |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/amp/world-europe-52435273 |accessdate=27 April 2020 |work=BBC News |date=26 April 2020 |language=en-gb}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Giuffrida |first1=Angela |title=Italy unveils plans for easing of coronavirus lockdown restrictions |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/apr/27/italy-unveils-plans-for-easing-of-coronavirus-lockdown-restrictions-conte |accessdate=27 April 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=27 April 2020}}</ref>

On 13 May, Education Minister Lucia Azzolina announced schools would remain closed until September.<ref>[https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-italy-education-idUSKBN22P1PK Italian schools to reopen in September: Education minister], ''Reuters'', 13 May 2020.</ref>

On 16 May, Conte announced the government plan for the easing of restrictions. Starting from 18 May most businesses could reopen, and free movement was granted to all citizens within their Region; movement across Regions was still banned for non-essential motives. Furthermore, on 25 May swimming pools and gyms could also reopen, and on 15 June theatres and cinemas.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Severgnini |first1=Chiara |title=La conferenza stampa di Conte: "Dati incoraggianti, corriamo un rischio calcolato" |url=https://www.corriere.it/politica/20_maggio_16/discorso-conte-conferenza-stampa-oggi-decreto-18-maggio-1e810142-9785-11ea-ba09-20ae073bed63.shtml |accessdate=26 May 2020 |work=Corriere della Sera |date=16 May 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

On 3 June, free movement within the whole national territory was restored, ''de facto'' ending the lockdown started in March.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus: Italy's Conte offers hope as travel restrictions end |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-52914089 |accessdate=7 October 2020 |work=BBC News |date=3 June 2020}}</ref>

Penalties for breaching isolation were increased with fines from €500 to €5,000 and imprisonment of up to 18 months.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20201127-france-weighs-forcing-coronavirus-infected-patients-to-isolate |title=France weighs forcing coronavirus-infected patients to isolate |publisher=France24 |date=27 November 2020}}</ref>

===Containment measures on the second wave===
Starting from July 2020, many countries in Europe, including Italy, witnessed a new rise in detected coronavirus cases.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus in Europe: Infections surge in France, Germany and Spain |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-53747852 |accessdate=7 October 2020 |work=BBC News |date=12 August 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=As Covid cases rise again, how are countries in Europe reacting? |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/sep/23/as-covid-cases-rise-again-how-are-countries-in-europe-reacting |accessdate=7 October 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=23 September 2020}}</ref> On 7 October, the Parliament postponed the end of the state of emergency to 31 January 2021, and Prime Minister Conte imposed the use of protection mask outdoors.<ref>{{cite news |title=Il cdm proroga lo stato d'emergenza al 31 gennaio. Mascherine subito obbligatorie. Sì della Camera alla risoluzione di maggioranza |url=https://www.repubblica.it/politica/2020/10/07/news/camera_covid_voto_risoluzione_maggioranza-269726919/?ref=RHPPTP-BH-I269167158-C12-P1-S1.8-T1 |accessdate=7 October 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=7 October 2020 |language=it}}</ref>
On 13 October 2020, the Italian government reintroduced stricter rules to limit the spread of COVID-19.<ref>{{cite news |title=Conte: 'Non manderemo la polizia a casa, ma serve responsabilità' |url=https://www.ansa.it/sito/notizie/politica/2020/10/13/conte-curva-sta-risalendo-consaiglio-europeo-recovery_49c33d56-2cd2-41e6-b31e-86a3a0b1c173.html |accessdate=13 October 2020 |agency=ansa.it |publisher=ansa.it |date=13 October 2020}}</ref> Demonstrations and gatherings of people were strictly forbidden.<ref>{{cite news |title=Covid, in Campania vietati tutti i cortei, anche quelli funebri |url=https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/campania/covid-in-campania-vietati-tutti-i-cortei-anche-quelli-funebri_24258602-202002a.shtml |accessdate=15 October 2020 |agency=tgcom24 |publisher=tgcom24 |date=15 October 2020}}</ref> Regions and municipalities were given the power to only tighten, but not release, containment measures.<ref>{{cite news |title=Covid, Conte: "Lockdown? Possibili misure restrittive per le Regioni" |url=https://www.tgcom24.mediaset.it/cronaca/covid-conte-lockdown-possibili-misure-restrittive-per-le-regioni_24214166-202002a.shtml |accessdate=15 October 2020 |agency=tgcom24 |publisher=tgcom24 |date=15 October 2020}}</ref>

Italian regions and the central government began reinforcing hospitals to accommodate more sick and infected with COVID-19.{{Citation needed |date=October 2020}}
All hospital facilities were upgraded and expanded with a larger capacity for beds and intensive units than in March 2020.{{Citation needed |date=October 2020}} 
The Italian government also purchased about 19 million doses of [[flu vaccine]], to be distributed to the population.{{Citation needed |date=October 2020}}
Tracking applications, monitoring systems with the help of [[surveillance]] [[Miniature UAV|drones]] and [[Predictive analytics|predictive systems]] are used to understand the progress of the epidemic.{{Citation needed |date=October 2020}}
If containment fails, the possible cases of infections will rise to about one million people and about 80,000 will died before the end of the pandemic, but the release of the [[COVID-19 vaccine]] is imminent and can change this dramatic projection.{{Citation needed |date=October 2020}}

On 25 October, Conte introduced new restrictions, imposing the closing of gyms, swimming pools, theatres and cinemas, as well as the closing of bars and restaurants by 6pm.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, Conte firma il nuovo Dpcm: in semi-lockdown per un mese. Stop a bar e ristoranti alle 18 ma aperti la domenica |url=https://www.repubblica.it/politica/2020/10/25/news/coronavirus_nuovo_dpcm_conte_firma_ristoranti_aperti_domenica-271793108/?ref=RHTP-BH-I271771521-P2-S1-T1 |accessdate=25 October 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=25 October 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

===Local measures===
On 15 March, President of Campania [[Vincenzo De Luca]] imposed a strict quarantine on [[Ariano Irpino]], in the province of Avellino, and four other municipalities in the province of Salerno, [[Atena Lucana]], [[Caggiano]], [[Polla, Italy|Polla]], and [[Sala Consilina]].<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, De Luca "chiude" altri quattro Comuni |url=https://napoli.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/15/news/de_luca_chiude_altri_4_comuni-251388474/ |accessdate=16 March 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=15 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

On 16 March, President of Emilia-Romagna [[Stefano Bonaccini]] imposed a strengthened quarantine on the municipality of [[Medicina]], near Bologna, since it had developed an intense outbreak. People were not allowed to enter or exit the town for any reason.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://bologna.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/16/news/coronavirus_medicina_e_zona_rossa_vietato_entrare_e_uscire-251412467/ |title=Coronavirus, Medicina è zona rossa, vietato entrare e uscire|date=16 March 2020|website=la Repubblica}}</ref>

In early April, Lombardy and Tuscany made it compulsory for all residents to wear a face mask when leaving their home.<ref name="it20200406">{{cite news |url=https://www.ansa.it/english/news/2020/04/06/coronavirus-lombardy-makes-face-masks-compulsory_a852ffdb-a0dd-4c55-a725-e852c5a2fc43.html |title=Coronavirus: Lombardy, Tuscany make face masks compulsory |date=6 April 2020 |work=ANSA }}</ref>

Due to the spike in [[Coronavirus disease 2019|COVID-19]] cases in August, Italy's health minister, [[Roberto Speranza]] announced the closure of nightclubs in some parts of the country and made masks mandatory between 6 pm and 6 am, in crowded areas and at social gatherings. The restrictions came into effect from 17 August 2020.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/coronavirus-italy-nightclubs-face-masks-cases-young-people-roberto-speranza-a9673391.html|title=Coronavirus: Italy to shut nightclubs and make masks compulsory after spike in cases|accessdate=17 August 2020|website=The Independent}}</ref>

On 15 October 2020, the president of Campania De Luca, closed all schools and universities until 30 October 2020.<ref name="tgcom24"/> On 23 October, De Luca announced a regional lockdown, imposing restrictions to all not essential movements as well as a [[curfew]].<ref>[https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/10/23/de-luca-annuncia-campania-verso-il-lockdown-totale-per-30-40-giorni-chiedero-al-governo-di-estenderlo-a-livello-nazionale-record-di-oltre-2mila-contagi-in-un-giorno-diretta/5977246/ De Luca annuncia: “Campania verso il lockdown per 30-40 giorni. Al governo chiederò di estenderlo a tutti”. Record di oltre 2mila casi in un giorno], ''Il Fatto Quotidiano''</ref> In the night, riots and clashes happened in the streets of [[Naples]] to protest against the lockdown.<ref>[https://www.france24.com/en/europe/20201024-hundreds-protest-clash-with-police-in-naples-over-new-coronavirus-curfew Hundreds protest, clash with police in Naples over new coronavirus curfew], ''France 24''</ref>

===Screening and testing policies===
{{Expand section |date=March 2020}}
The strategy of mass-testing [[asymptomatic carriers]] was proven to be successful in stopping the spread of the virus in one Italian town.<ref name=Horowitz2020-03-21>{{cite web |last1=Horowitz |first1=Jason |last2=Bubola |first2=Emma |last3=Povoledo |first3=Elisabetta |title=Italy, Pandemic's New Epicenter, Has Lessons for the World |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/03/21/world/europe/italy-coronavirus-center-lessons.html |website=[[The New York Times]] |archive-url= https://web.archive.org/web/20200322023527/https://www.nytimes.com/2020/03/21/world/europe/italy-coronavirus-center-lessons.html |archive-date=23 March 2020 |date=21 March 2020 |url-status=live |quote=steps to isolate the coronavirus and limit people's movement need to be put in place early, with absolute clarity, then strictly enforced}}</ref><ref name=McCall2020-03-19>{{cite web |last1=McCall |first1=Rosie |title=Coronavirus mass testing experiment in Italian town appears to have halted COVID-19 outbreak |url=https://www.newsweek.com/coronavirus-mass-testing-experiment-italian-town-covid-19-outbreak-1493183 |website=[[Newsweek]] |archive-url= https://web.archive.org/web/20200321131113/https://www.newsweek.com/coronavirus-mass-testing-experiment-italian-town-covid-19-outbreak-1493183 |archive-date=21 March 2020  |date=19 March 2020 |url-status=live}}</ref><ref name=Crisanti2020-03-20>{{cite web |last1=Crisanti |first1=Andrea |author-link=Andrea Crisanti (scientist) |last2=Cassone |first2=Antonio |title=In one Italian town, we showed mass testing could eradicate the coronavirus |url=https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2020/mar/20/eradicated-coronavirus-mass-testing-covid-19-italy-vo |website=[[The Guardian]] / [[University of Padua]] |archive-url= https://web.archive.org/web/20200323203803/https://www.theguardian.com/commentisfree/2020/mar/20/eradicated-coronavirus-mass-testing-covid-19-italy-vo |archive-date=23 March 2020 |date=20 March 2020 |url-status=live |quote=asymptomatic or quasi-symptomatic subjects represent a good 70% of all virus-infected people and, still worse, an unknown, yet impossible to ignore portion of them can transmit the virus to others}}</ref> This strategy in Italy was supported by the region of [[Veneto]].<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/03/18/coronavirus-zaia-vanno-chiusi-supermercati-nel-weekend-e-vietate-passeggiate-si-al-controllo-su-celle-telefoniche-ma-ci-vuole-norma/5740615/|title=Coronavirus, Zaia: "Vanno chiusi supermercati nel weekend e vietate passeggiate. Sì al controllo su celle telefoniche ma ci vuole norma"|language=it|work=[[Il Fatto Quotidiano]]|first= Gisella|last=Ruccia|date=18 March 2020|access-date=23 March 2020|quote=L’esperienza insegna che ogni asintomatico positivo può contagiare fino a 10 altre persone. Quindi, la caccia all’asintomatico positivo è fondamentale, tanto è vero che oggi abbiamo 8500 persone in isolamento, letteralmente trovate con questa modalità}}</ref>

==Lockdown areas==
{{main|COVID-19 pandemic lockdown in Italy}}
On 22 February, the government established a lockdown for eleven municipalities in [[Lombardy]] and [[Veneto]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.la7.it/nonelarena/video/lelenco-dei-comuni-in-quarantena-a-causa-del-coronavirus-23-02-2020-308963|title=L'elenco dei comuni in quarantena a causa del coronavirus|accessdate=8 March 2020|via=la7.it}}</ref>

On 7 March, the government prepared to extend until 3 April the restricted zone to all of Lombardy, plus fourteen other provinces in Veneto (3), [[Emilia-Romagna]] (5), [[Marche]] (1) and [[Piedmont]] (5).<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/politica/20_marzo_07/coronavirusin-lombardia-si-potra-entrare-uscire-solo-gravi-motivi-chiuse-discoteche-palestre-impianti-sci-0478cd9c-609a-11ea-8d61-438e0a276fc4.shtml|title=Coronavirus, il governo isola la Lombardia e 14 province|first=Fiorenza|last=Sarzanini|website=Corriere della Sera|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref> The lockdown affects over 16 million people, roughly a quarter of Italy's total population, and prevents people from entering or leaving the zone, except "for proven occupational needs or situations of need or for health reasons",<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, treni, aeroporti, blocchi stradali: ecco come funzionano le nuove regole del decreto del 7 marzo
 |url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_marzo_08/coronavirus-ecco-come-funzionano-nuove-regole-rispettare-d657e654-611c-11ea-8f33-90c941af0f23.shtml|accessdate=8 March 2020 |work=Corriere della Sera |date=8 March 2020|language=it}}</ref> under threat of fines.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Davidson |first1=Helen |last2=Tondo |first2=Lorenzo |last3=Yu |first3=Verna |title=Coronavirus: quarter of Italy's population put in quarantine as virus reaches Washington DC |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/08/coronavirus-italy-quarantine-virus-reaches-washington-dc |accessdate=8 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=8 March 2020}}</ref> The [[enclave]] nation of San Marino, which is nestled between two of the provinces, has been effectively locked down as well.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.romagnauno.it/san-marino/san-marino-isolato-dal-decreto-italiano-diventa-automaticamente-zona-rossa/?fbclid=IwAR3qu4hqUMBCXoaqtV-2OPtGRBN3ggIHA68_MhfHkP1FQy9Xkre82Rgog98|title=San Marino isolato dal decreto italiano diventa automaticamente Zona rossa|website=Romagna Uno|date=7 March 2020|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref>

On 9 March, Prime Minister Conte announced that the lockdown would be extended to the entire country.<ref name="auto"/>

==Reactions abroad==
===Travel restrictions===
{{See|Travel restrictions related to the COVID-19 pandemic}}
{{Update section |date=March 2020}}
[[File:Restrizioni per gli Italiani COVID19.png|thumb|upright=2.27|
Restrictions to travel from Italy, as of 31 March 2020
{{legend|#008000|Italy}}
{{legend|#AA0000|Entrance refused to people from Italy}}
{{legend|#003380|Enforced quarantine for people arriving from Italy}}]]
On 23 February 2020, Austria suspended all trains to and from Italy for a few hours because of suspected cases.<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" /><ref>{{cite web|url=https://news.sky.com/story/coronavirus-towns-in-lockdown-as-italy-races-to-contain-europes-biggest-outbreak-11941438|title=Coronavirus: Austria stops all trains to and from Italy amid Europe's biggest coronavirus outbreak|publisher=Sky News|access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref> Romania instituted a quarantine for people arriving from Lombardy and Veneto.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.news1.news/2020/02/coronavirus-romania-quarantine-for-those-returning-from-lombardy-and-veneto-ischia-northern-tourists-stop-landing.html|title=Coronavirus, Romania: quarantine for those returning from Lombardy and Veneto {{!}} Ischia, Northern tourists stop landing |work=News1 English |access-date=23 February 2020}}</ref>

On 24 February, an [[Alitalia]] flight from Rome to Mauritius was blocked at the [[Sir Seewoosagur Ramgoolam International Airport]] by the local authorities, who imposed quarantine or repatriation for 212 Italian passengers.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_febbraio_24/coronavirus-volo-alitalia-fermo-mauritius-quarantena-o-rimpatrio-aa38bc60-56e5-11ea-b89d-a5ca249e9e1e.shtml|title=Coronavirus, volo Alitalia con 300 persone a bordo fermo a Mauritius|last=Salvia|first=Flavio Haver e Lorenzo|date=24 February 2020|website=Corriere della Sera}}</ref> Of the 212 passengers, 172 were allowed to disembark while 40 passengers from Lombardy and Veneto decided to go back to Italy.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/china-health-italy-flight-idUSL5N2AO35K|title=Update 1-Mauritius blocks some Italian visitors over coronavirus concerns -Alitalia|date=24 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> An intercity bus operated by [[Flixbus]] from Milan to [[Lyon]] was quarantined at [[Gare de Lyon-Perrache]] station so that its passengers could undergo health checks.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.askanews.it/esteri/2020/02/24/coronavirus-flixbus-arrivato-da-milano-confinato-a-stazione-lione-pn_20200224_00123|title=Coronavirus, Flixbus arrivato da Milano confinato a stazione Lione|date=24 February 2020|website=Askanews|language=it-IT|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref>

Brazil added Italy to its COVID-19 alert list, meaning that passengers entering Brazil from Italy showing flu symptoms would undergo medical checkups.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.usnews.com/news/world/articles/2020-02-24/brazil-to-check-arrivals-from-italy-france-germany-for-coronavirus-symptoms|title=Brazil to Check Arrivals From Italy, France, Germany for Coronavirus Symptoms|date=n.d.|website=Usnews}}</ref> Argentina, France, Croatia, Egypt, Greece, Ireland, Israel, Latvia, Lithuania, Ukraine, Serbia and South Africa issued multiple recommendations that included postponement of school trips to Italy, a 14-day quarantine for people arriving from Lombardy and Veneto and a warning for all citizens to not to travel to regions of Italy affected by the outbreak.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.srbija.gov.rs/vest/en/150543/foreign-ministry-advises-serbian-citizens-against-travelling-to-italy.php|title=Foreign Ministry advises Serbian citizens against travelling to Italy|last=srbija.gov.rs|website=srbija.gov.rs|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.lemonde.fr/planete/article/2020/02/24/coronavirus-mesures-de-precaution-hausse-de-la-mobilisation-comment-la-france-se-prepare-a-une-possible-epidemie_6030677_3244.html|title=Coronavirus : la France prend des mesures de précaution pour les personnes revenant d'Italie|date=24 February 2020|work=Le Monde.fr|access-date=24 February 2020|language=fr}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.euronews.com/2020/02/24/covid-19-outbreak-in-italy-what-are-other-eu-countries-doing|title=COVID-19 outbreak in Italy: What are other EU countries doing?|last=Montalto Monella|first=Lillo|date=24 February 2020|website=euronews|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/24/news/coronavirus_viaggi_turismo_italia-249495072/|title=Coronavirus, sempre più paesi sconsigliano i viaggi in Italia: "Una mazzata per il turismo e il pil"|date=24 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.lrt.lt/en/news-in-english/19/1145534/coronavirus-lithuania-may-declare-state-emergency|title=Coronavirus: Lithuania may declare state emergency|date=24 February 2020|website=lrt.lt|language=lt|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.corriere.it/esteri/20_febbraio_25/coronavirus-stati-che-impongono-restrizioni-all-italia-404a91e6-57e6-11ea-a2d7-f1bec9902bd3.shtml|title=Ingressi vietati, quarantena e invito all'isolamento: le restrizioni imposte agli italiani all'estero|last=Frate|first=Claudio Del|date=25 February 2020|website=Corriere della Sera|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> A joint [[World Health Organization|WHO]] and [[European Centre for Disease Prevention and Control|ECDC]] mission arrived in Italy to support COVID-19 control and prevention efforts.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.euro.who.int/en/countries/italy/news/news/2020/2/joint-who-and-ecdc-mission-in-italy-to-support-covid-19-control-and-prevention-efforts|title=Joint WHO and ECDC mission in Italy to support COVID-19 control and prevention efforts|date=24 February 2020|website=euro.who.int|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Following the discovery of a case involving an Italian citizen, the H10 Costa Adeje Palace in Tenerife was put on lockdown.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnn.com/2020/02/25/europe/tenerife-coronavirus-hotel-intl/index.html|title=Tenerife hotel on partial lockdown as Italian tests positive for coronavirus|author1=Laura Perez Maestro |first2=Niamh |last2=Kennedy |first3=Amy|last3=Woodyatt|publisher=CNN|access-date=29 February 2020}}</ref>

The [[European Parliament]]'s Director General for Personnel, Kristian Knudsen, requested that staff who had travelled to areas affected by the COVID-19 outbreak, including parts of Italy, China, Singapore, and South Korea, to self-quarantine and work from home for 14 days.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.politico.eu/article/parliament-tells-staff-to-stay-home-if-they-visited-places-hit-by-coronavirus/|title=Parliament tells staff to stay home if they visited places hit by coronavirus|last=Deutsch|first=Jillian|date=24 February 2020|website=Politico|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/26/news/conoravirus_bruxelles_bartolo-249655095/|title=Coronavirus, il racconto in prima persona di Bartolo: "Io, deputato europeo in quarantena, fuori dal Parlamento"|date=26 February 2020|website=la Repubblica}}</ref>

On 25 February, the United Kingdom and Malta recommended that travellers coming from Italy self-quarantine for 14 days and for all citizens not to travel to regions of Italy affected by the outbreak.<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" /><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.maltatoday.com.mt/news/national/100587/corona_virus_health_ministry|title=No coronavirus cases in Malta, Health Ministry says|website=MaltaToday.com.mt|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/uk-51625733|title=New coronavirus advice for Britons back from Italy|date=25 February 2020|work=BBC News|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> Malta installed thermal-scanning devices to monitor passengers arriving via [[Malta International Airport]], as well as passengers disembarking from vessels at the [[Grand Harbour]] and the [[Virtu Ferries]] catamaran terminal in [[Marsa, Malta|Marsa]], which had direct connections to [[Pozzallo|Pozzalo]] and [[Catania]] in Sicily.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://timesofmalta.com/articles/view/no-covid-19-cases-in-malta-at-this-point-health-ministry.773582|title=No coronavirus cases in Malta but country is well prepared, say authorities|website=The Times|location=Malta|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref> [[Prague International Airport]] introduced special arrival gates for selective screening of passengers arriving on flights from Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.radio.cz/en/section/news/coronavirus-prague-airport-designates-special-gates-for-arrivals-from-italy|title=Coronavirus: Prague Airport designates special gates for arrivals from Italy|website=Radio Prague International|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ceskenoviny.cz/zpravy/letiste-praha-ma-specialni-brany-pro-prilety-z-italie/1858394|title=Letiště Praha má speciální brány pro přílety z Itálie {{!}} ČeskéNoviny.cz|website=www.ceskenoviny.cz|language=cs|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> Kuwait, Iraq, Jordan and Seychelles suspended all flights to and from Italy.<ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Europe">{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/25/news/coronavirus_cina_trump-249513033/|title=Coronavirus, dall'Italia si spande in Europa. Conte: "Inaccettabili limitazioni agli italiani". Ma molti Paesi prendono misure|date=25 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-kuwait-idUSKCN20I2F9|title=Kuwait suspends flights to and from South Korea, Thailand, Italy over coronavirus fears|date=24 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/esteri/2020/02/27/news/coronavirus_stati_restrizioni_viaggio_italia_12_divieti_ingresso-249720846/|title=Coronavirus, ecco gli Stati dove gli italiani non-possono viaggiare o hanno restrizioni|date=27 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref> Bulgaria suspended all flights to and from Milan until 27 March. Australia, Saudi Arabia, Netherlands and the United States issued a travel advisory for all citizens not to travel to parts of Italy affected by the outbreak.<ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Europe" /><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.businessinsider.com/cdc-issues-travel-warning-italy-covid-19-concerns-2020-2|title=The US is telling Americans with preexisting conditions to avoid trips to Italy|last=Al-Arshani|first=Sarah|website=Business Insider|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

Two intercity buses operated by Flixbus, one travelling from Lyon to [[Rijeka]] via [[Turin]], the other travelling from Turin to [[Zagreb]], were stopped at the Croatian border for a few hours as the passengers underwent health checks.<ref name="Repubblica_liveupdate" />

[[Goldman Sachs]], [[Deloitte]], [[Citigroup]] Inc, [[Credit Suisse]], [[Lazard Capital Markets|Lazard]], [[Crédit Agricole|Credit Agricole]], [[Nomura Holdings|Nomura]], [[Banque Populaire]] and [[BNP Paribas]] requested that staff who had recently returned from Italy to work from home for at least 14 days and deferred non-essential travel to Italy.<ref name="Reuters_banks">{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-banks-idUSKCN20I2LW|title=Goldman, Citi among banks curbing Italy trips over coronavirus fears – sources|date=25 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://timesofmalta.com/articles/view/deloitte-malta-asks-staff-returning-from-italy-to-work-from-home.773615|title=Coronavirus: Deloitte Malta asks staff returning from Italy to work from home|website=The Times|location=Malta|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

On 26 February, the European Parliament postponed internships until 1 October for 35 trainees who declared residence addresses in areas affected by the COVID-19 outbreak, including Lombardy, Piedmont, Emilia-Romagna and Veneto.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://edition.cnn.com/asia/live-news/coronavirus-outbreak-02-26-20-intl-hnk/h_5964fbd1f32ef875b399c3461de9c200|title=European Parliament cancels internships for people from coronavirus affected areas|first1=Jessie |last1=Yeung |first2=Adam |last2=Renton |first3=Meg |last3=Wagne |first4=Mike |last4=Hayes |first5=Rachel|last5=Bowman|date=26 February 2020|publisher=CNN|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> Six American universities — [[Elon University]], [[Fairfield University]], [[Florida International University]], [[New York University]], [[Stanford University]] and [[Syracuse University]] — postponed or cancelled their study-abroad programmes in Italy, mainly in Florence.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnn.com/2020/02/26/us/colleges-canceling-study-abroad-coronavirus-trnd/index.html|title=A growing list of US colleges are canceling study abroad programs because of the coronavirus|last=Sutton|first=Francisco Guzman and Joe|publisher=CNN|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.lanazione.it/firenze/cronaca/coronavirus-toscana-1.5046897|title=Coronavirus in Toscana: quattro positivi, altri due casi di contagio a Firenze / Diretta|last=Nazione|first=La|date=26 February 2020|website=La Nazione|language=it|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

Russia, Spain and Turkey issued a recommendation for all citizens not to travel to regions of Italy affected by the outbreak.<ref name=":2" /><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.theolivepress.es/spain-news/2020/02/25/spain-issues-travel-warning-for-italy-over-coronavirus-outbreak-as-it-steps-up-protocols/|title=Spain issues travel warning for Italy over coronavirus outbreak as it steps up protocols|last=Dollimore|first=Laurence|date=25 February 2020|website=Olive Press News Spain|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> El Salvador barred the entry of travellers arriving from Italy.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-el-salvador-idUSKBN20J2UB|title=El Salvador bars visitors from Italy and South Korea, citing coronavirus|date=25 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

The chief executive of the [[Irish Rugby Football Union]], Philip Browne, cancelled [[Six Nations Championship]] rugby matches between Ireland and Italy from 6 to 8 March in [[Dublin]].<ref>{{Cite news|last=Carroll|first=Rory|url=https://www.theguardian.com/sport/2020/feb/26/ireland-v-italy-six-nations-match-postponed-due-to-coronavirus|title=Ireland v Italy in Six Nations postponed and may be cancelled due to coronavirus|date=26 February 2020|work=The Guardian|access-date=26 February 2020|issn=0261-3077}}</ref>

On 27 February, Israel barred entry to foreign nationals travelling from Italy. Officials at [[Ramon Airport]] refused to let 25 foreign nationals arriving on a Ryanair flight from Bergamo to disembark. Israeli passengers were allowed to enter the country and were quarantined at home for 14 days.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.timesofisrael.com/israeli-returning-from-italy-has-coronavirus-visitors-from-there-to-be-barred/|title=Israeli diagnosed with virus after Italy trip; visitors from there to be barred |website=The Times of Israel|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ynetnews.com/article/ryXHlBB4I|title=Dozens of travelers from Italy refused entry to Israel|date=27 February 2020|website=ynetnews|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.jpost.com/Breaking-News/Israeli-who-came-back-from-Italy-diagnosed-with-coronavirus-619053|title=Coronavirus confirmed in Israeli who returned from Italy|website=The Jerusalem Post {{!}} JPost.com|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> After being denied permission to dock in [[Ocho Rios]], Jamaica and [[George Town, Cayman Islands|George Town]], Cayman Islands on 26 February, the ''[[MSC Meraviglia]]'', operated by [[MSC Cruises]], was finally able to dock in [[Cozumel]], Mexico. The cruise liner was carrying 4,500 passengers and 1,600 crew members, one of whom was reportedly showing flu-like symptoms.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.foxnews.com/travel/cruise-ship-msc-meraviglia-coronavirus-concerns|title=Cruise ship MSC Meraviglia turned away from two Caribbean ports amid coronavirus concerns|last=Puhak|first=Janine|date=26 February 2020|publisher=Fox News Channel|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-mexico-port-idUSKCN20K33F|title=Mexican port denies cruise ship permission to dock over coronavirus fears|date=26 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.foxnews.com/travel/coronavirus-concerns-cruise-ship-msc-meraviglia-mexico|title=MSC cruise ship docks in Mexico following coronavirus scare; company says ill crew member diagnosed with flu|last=Puhak|first=Janine|date=27 February 2020|publisher=Fox News Channel|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://apnews.com/5dd186d96385f7621182cbe5466901a8|title=Cruise ship docks at Mexico's Cozumel amid virus fears|date=27 February 2020|website=AP NEWS|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> Another Italian cruise liner, the [[Costa Favolosa]], which was denied permission to dock at [[Tortola]], [[British Virgin Islands]] on 26 February, was finally able to berth in [[Sint Maarten]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.cruisehive.com/cruise-ship-with-sick-passengers-denied-to-dock-in-the-british-virgin-islands/38014|title=Cruise Ship With Sick Passengers Denied to Dock in the British Virgin Islands|date=26 February 2020|website=Cruise Hive|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.loopcayman.com/content/italian-cruise-ship-blocked-tortola-berths-st-maarten-1|title=Italian cruise ship blocked from Tortola berths in St Maarten|website=loopcayman.com|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> The final two stages of the [[UAE Tour]] were cancelled after two Italian staff members of one of the teams tested positive for SARS-CoV-2. Following this discovery, the W Abu Dhabi and the Crowne Plaza Abu Dhabi, both on [[Yas Island]], were put on lockdown.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.cyclingnews.com/news/final-uae-tour-stages-called-off-over-coronavirus-fears/|title=Final UAE Tour stages called off after two coronavirus cases confirmed|date=February 2020 |website=Cyclingnews.com|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

On 28 February, Germany enacted new health security measures to include regulations for air and sea travel, requiring passengers from multiple countries, including Italy, to report their health status before entry. Train railway companies must report passengers with symptoms to authorities and the federal police would step up checks within 30 kilometres of the border.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-germany-idUSKCN20M34J|title=Germany enacts new health security measures against coronavirus infections|date=28 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=29 February 2020}}</ref>

On 29 February, the United States [[Centers for Disease Control and Prevention]] upgraded the status of Italy to Level 3 (guidance to avoid non-essential travel because of widespread community transmission).<ref>{{cite web|url=https://wwwnc.cdc.gov/travel/notices/warning/coronavirus-italy|title=Coronavirus in Italy – Warning – Level 3, Avoid Nonessential Travel – Travel Health Notices {{!}} Travelers' Health {{!}} CDC|website=wwwnc.cdc.gov|access-date=29 February 2020}}</ref> Multiple companies such as [[Amazon (company)|Amazon]], Google, [[Toronto-Dominion Bank|TD Bank Group]], [[Bank of Nova Scotia]], [[London Stock Exchange Group]] and [[Cargill]], Inc. deferred all non-essential travel to countries affected by major virus outbreak, including Italy.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-amazon-com-idUSKCN20M2TZ|title=Amazon defers 'non-essential' moves even in U.S. as corporate travel bans spread|date=28 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=29 February 2020}}</ref> The [[University of Notre Dame]] ended its Rome Global Gateway programme and evacuated 106 students from Rome.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://emergency.nd.edu/|title=Emergency Information |website=University of Notre Dame Emergency Information|access-date=29 February 2020}}</ref>

On 3 March, India suspended all visas to nationals of Italy, as well as visa to foreign nationals who have travelled to Italy on or after 1 February 2020. Passengers arriving directly or indirectly from Italy must undergo medical screening at the port of entry.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://boi.gov.in/content/advisory-travel-and-visa-restrictions-related-covid-19|title=Advisory: Travel and Visa restrictions related to COVID-19|date=3 March 2020}}</ref>

On 4 March, Thailand declared that people travelling from Italy must be quarantined for 14 days after arriving, with no exceptions.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://mgronline.com/qol/detail/9630000021535|title="อนุทิน" เซ็นประกาศ สธ.กำหนด 9 ประเทศเป็นเขตติดโรคติดต่ออันตราย ทุกคนที่เดินทางมาต้องกักตัว 14 วัน สกัดโควิด-19|date=4 March 2020}}</ref>

On 8 March, Romania declared that people travelling from Italy must be quarantined for 14 days after arriving on a connecting flight or by road, with no exceptions, and suspended flights from Italy from 9 to 23 March.<ref>{{cite news |title=Update – Coronavirus: Romania suspends flights, buses, and trains to Italy, additional measures in place |url=https://www.romania-insider.com/italy-flights-suspended-march-23-coronavirus |accessdate=10 March 2020 |publisher=Romania-Insider |date=9 March 2020}}</ref>

On 10 March, Slovenia barred entry to foreign nationals travelling from Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Slowenien kündigt Schließung der Grenze zu Italien an |url=https://orf.at/stories/3157329/ |accessdate=5 April 2020 |work=news.ORF.at |date=10 March 2020 |language=de}}</ref> On same day also Austria barred entry to foreign nationals travelling from Italy with exception for people with medical documents and people who travel only through Austria to Germany without stop in Austria.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.br.de/nachrichten/deutschland-welt/oesterreich-will-einreisen-aus-italien-weitgehend-stoppen,RspR1PZ|title=Österreich will Einreisen aus Italien weitgehend stoppen|date=10 March 2020|website=BR24|accessdate=11 March 2020}}</ref>

On 18 March, Nigeria placed an indefinite suspension on all flights coming from Italy with immediate effect.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://punchng.com/breaking-fg-places-travel-ban-on-china-italy-us-uk-others|title=Updated: FG places travel ban on China, Italy, US, UK, nine others|last=Ogundele|first=Kamarudeen|date=18 March 2020|accessdate=26 March 2020|publisher=[[The Punch]] Newspaper}}</ref>

===Export restrictions and aid received===
[[File:Samaritan's Purse in Verona airport - Scarico materiale.jpg|thumb|left|upright=1.13|[[Samaritan's Purse]] aeroplane with medical aids at the [[Verona Villafranca Airport]]]]
The Italian government asked for medical equipment from the European Union mechanism of civil protection, and on 11 March complained about the slow response of the other European countries.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Daniel Boffey |title=Italy criticises EU for being slow to help over coronavirus epidemic |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/11/italy-criticises-eu-being-slow-help-coronavirus-epidemic |accessdate=14 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=11 March 2020 |quote=Italy has already asked to activate the European Union mechanism of civil protection for the supply of medical equipment for individual protection. But unfortunately not a single EU country responded}}</ref> The [[List of Permanent Representatives of Italy to the European Union|Italian Permanent Representative to the European Union]], Maurizio Massari, wrote: "unfortunately, not a single EU country responded to the Commission's call."<ref>{{cite news |title=Italian ambassador to the EU: Italy needs Europe's help |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/coronavirus-italy-needs-europe-help/ |accessdate=14 March 2020 |work=[[Politico]] |date=11 March 2020 |quote="unfortunately, not a single EU country responded to the Commission's call."}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Miles Johnson |title=Italy shuts all retailers except food stores and pharmacies |url=https://www.ft.com/content/b25470c0-63e6-11ea-a6cd-df28cc3c6a68 |accessdate=14 March 2020 |work=[[Financial Times]] |date=11 March 2020 |quote=Maurizio Massari, Italian permanent representative to the EU, saying that no EU member had responded to a request for medical equipment. "Only China responded bilaterally. Certainly, this is not a good sign of European solidarity," he wrote}}</ref>  Eventually, Germany, France and Austria donated millions of protective masks to Italy, however aid arrived from non-EU countries like China, Russia and Cuba before it arrived from any other EU country.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Naomi O'Leary |title=Covid-19: Economic downturn worsens old EU splits |url=https://www.irishtimes.com/business/economy/covid-19-economic-downturn-worsens-old-eu-splits-1.4214059 |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=[[The Irish Times]] |date=27 March 2020 }}</ref><ref name="npr_aid">{{cite news |last1=Poggioli |first1=Sylvia |title=For Help On Coronavirus, Italy Turns To China, Russia And Cuba |url=https://www.npr.org/sections/coronavirus-live-updates/2020/03/25/821345465/for-help-on-coronavirus-italy-turns-to-china-russia-and-cuba?t=1585572391993 |accessdate=30 March 2020 |publisher=NPR |date=25 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title='Health Silk Road:' China showers Europe with coronavirus aid as both spar with Trump |url=https://fortune.com/2020/03/19/china-europe-coronavirus-aid-trump/ |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=Fortune }}</ref>

The lack of masks became an issue during the peak of the emergency, partly because of the requisitions of imported goods bought by Italy in transport hubs in other countries such as Poland<ref>{{cite news|url=https://roma.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/21/news/coronavirus_lazio_mascherine_dogana_polonia_scontro_diplomatico-251900742/|date=21 March 2020 |title= Coronavirus, le mascherine destinate a Roma e al Lazio bloccate in Polonia|publisher=[[La Repubblica]]|access-date=22 March 2020|language=it}}</ref> and Turkey.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://roma.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/21/news/coronavirus_lazio_mascherine_dogana_polonia_scontro_diplomatico-251900742/|date=19 March 2020 |title= Coronavirus: Cisl, 1 mln mascherine per Trentino bloccate|publisher=[[Agenzia Nazionale Stampa Associata|ANSA]]|access-date=19 March 2020|language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|last=Gabanelli|first=Milena|url=https://www.corriere.it/dataroom-milena-gabanelli/20_marzo_19/coronavirus-200-mila-mascherine-gli-ospedali-italiani-bloccate-ad-ankara-15-giorni-2b0ea5be-695d-11ea-913c-55c2df06d574_preview.shtml?reason=unauthenticated&cat=1&cid=cYfmThlo&pids=FR&credits=1&origin=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.corriere.it%2Fdataroom-milena-gabanelli%2F20_marzo_19%2Fcoronavirus-200-mila-mascherine-gli-ospedali-italiani-bloccate-ad-ankara-15-giorni-2b0ea5be-695d-11ea-913c-55c2df06d574.shtml|title=Coronarivus, 200 mila mascherine per gli ospedali italiani bloccate ad Ankara da 15 giorni|work=[[Corriere della Sera]]|access-date=19 March 2020|language=it}}</ref> Masks were confiscated by mistake in Czechia. It was happen during a raid against Chinese reseller Zhou Lingjian.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://zpravy.aktualne.cz/domaci/confiscated-face-masks-imported-by-an-influential-representa/r~560650326f6611ea842f0cc47ab5f122/|access-date=26 March 2020 |title= Confiscated face masks imported by an influential Chinese representative in Czechia|first=Lukáš|last=Valášek}}</ref>

Since early March, the German government restricted the export of products essential to its national health service. Italian distributors were advised they could not be supplied with surgical gowns, protective masks, glasses, particulate respirators, nor visors.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, stop export of masks: Germany "suffocates" Italy |url=https://www.liberoquotidiano.it/news/italia/21145392/coronavirus_germania_mascherine_italia.html |accessdate=15 March 2020 |work=[[Libero (newspaper)|Libero]] |date=13 March 2020 |language=it |quote="which confirms that the company will not be able to meet the demand for new surgical gowns, protective masks, glasses, and visors because Germany, with a letter in early March, confirmed the restrictions on the export of essential products for the system national health service".}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, Germany asphyxiates Italy on masks? The case of the "export limits" |url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/italia/coronavirus_mascherine_germania_italia_esportazioni_3m_lettera-5108989.html |accessdate=15 March 2020 |work=[[Il Messaggero]] |date=13 March 2020 |language=it |quote=explains to Italian customers that they cannot meet their demand for masks and the like due to export restrictions imposed by the German government. The US multinational received the letter in the first week of March.
