The restrictions concern: surgical gowns (sterile and non-sterile), particulate respirators (FFP2 / FFP3), surgical masks, protective goggles, visors, protective clothing.}}</ref> France also imposed similar export restrictions and the German health minister [[Jens Spahn]] defended Germany's decision.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Caizzi |first1=Ivo |title=Masks divide the EU as Germany and France block exports |url=https://www.corriere.it/esteri/20_marzo_06/mascherine-dividono-ue-germania-francia-bloccano-l-export-30087c42-5fd6-11ea-96d2-d1c7db9c0ec3.shtml |accessdate=15 March 2020 |work=[[Corriere della Sera]] |date=6 March 2020 |language=it |quote=But the German health minister, Jens Spahn, defended his government's decision to impose "to ask the authorities for an authorization" to export masks}}</ref> On 12 March, the German ministry issued a decree suspending the export restriction in particular emergency cases, and promised to send one million protective masks to Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, la Germania invierà un milione di mascherine all'Italia |url=https://www.repubblica.it/esteri/2020/03/13/news/coronavirus_la_germania_invia_un_milione_di_mascherine_all_italia-251219227/ |accessdate=15 March 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=13 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

On 13 March, a team of nine Chinese experts, among whom there was the manager of the 40,000 Chinese doctors who had been sent to Wuhan and a leading cardio-pulmonary reanimation doctor, arrived in Rome to share their expertise. The Chinese Red Cross brought 31 tons of respiratory devices, electrocardiographs, 40 ventilators, tens of thousands of masks, and other medical equipment supplied by the hospital of the School of Medicine of Shanghai Jiaotong University.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, medici cinesi a Roma: anche erbe medicinali fra le 31 tonnellate di materiali |url=https://roma.corriere.it/notizie/cronaca/20_marzo_13/coronavirus-aiuti-cinesi-anche-erbe-medicinali-le-31-tonnellate-materiali-04e4543c-6512-11ea-ac89-181bb7c2e00e.shtml |work=Il Corriere della Sera |date=13 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Pelosi |first1=Gerardo |title=Coronavirus, attese per oggi un milione di mascherine |url=https://www.ilsole24ore.com/art/coronavirus-attese-oggi-milione-mascherine-ADTgUWC?refresh_ce=1 |accessdate=14 March 2020 |work=[[Il Sole 24 Ore]] |date=11 March 2020 |language=it |quote=Only China has responded bilaterally. This is not a good sign of EU solidarity}}</ref><ref name=aljazeera-china-italy>{{cite news |title=China sends essential coronavirus supplies to Italy |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2020/03/china-sends-essential-coronavirus-supplies-italy-200313195241031.html |accessdate=14 March 2020 |publisher=[[Al Jazeera]] |date=14 March 2020 }}</ref> While the head of the Italian Red Cross, Francesco Rocca said these medical supplies were donated by the Chinese Red Cross, other sources claimed that these were paid products and services.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Balmer |first1=Crispian |title=China sends medical supplies, experts to help Italy battle coronavirus |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-italy-respirators/china-sends-medical-supplies-experts-to-help-italy-battle-coronavirus-idUSKBN2101IM |accessdate=24 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=13 March 2020 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Giulia Pompili |title=But what help from China against the virus, it's all stuff we purchase |url=https://www.ilfoglio.it/cronache/2020/03/12/news/ma-quali-aiuti-della-cina-contro-il-virus-e-tutta-roba-che-compriamo-306324/ |accessdate=16 March 2020 |work=[[Il Foglio]] |date=12 March 2020 |language=it |quote=confermano al Foglio fonti della Farnesina e la Protezione civile, non c’è nessuna donazione, niente di gratis}}</ref> Chinese billionaire and [[Alibaba Group|Alibaba]] co-founder [[Jack Ma]] also donated 500,000 masks and other medical supplies, which landed at Liege Airport in Belgium on 13 March and were then sent to Italy.<ref name=aljazeera-china-italy /><ref>{{cite news |last1=Blenkinsop |first1=Philip |title=Jack Ma donates two million masks for coronavirus crisis in Europe |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-jack-ma-idUSKBN2110KA |accessdate=24 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=14 March 2020 }}</ref>

On 17 March, Undersecretary at the [[Ministry of Health (Italy)|Ministry of Health]], [[Sandra Zampa]] announced the purchase of many new [[ventilator]]s as well as the importing of one and a half million masks from South Africa.<ref name="la7.it">{{Citation|title=Sandra Zampa: "È arrivata una partita di un milione e mezzo di mascherine dal Sud Africa"|url=https://www.la7.it/laria-che-tira/video/sandra-zampa-e-arrivata-una-partita-di-un-milione-e-mezzo-di-mascherine-dal-sud-africa-17-03-2020-313803|language=it|access-date=17 March 2020}}</ref>

The [[Agnelli family]] donated €10&nbsp;million to the Government's coronavirus funds. The family's companies Fiat and Ferrari also brought 150 ventilators and offered to help make new ventilator units, in addition to providing a fleet of vehicles to be used to distribute food and medical supplies to the elderly.<ref>{{Cite news |url=https://www.formula1.com/en/latest/article.family-behind-ferrari-donates-eur10m-and-150-ventilators-to-help-fight.49I36GCiU2RZgz5i1mONJN.html |title=Family behind Ferrari donates €10m and 150 ventilators to help fight coronavirus in Italy |date=18 March 2020 |publisher=Formula One |access-date=20 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news |last1=Pollina |first1=Elvira |url=https://uk.reuters.com/article/uk-health-coronavirus-ventilators-italy/exclusive-ferrari-and-fiat-look-at-helping-italy-make-ventilators-in-coronavirus-crisis-idUKKBN2162YR |title=Exclusive: Ferrari and Fiat look at helping Italy make ventilators in coronavirus crisis |date=19 March 2020 |access-date=20 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |last2=Piovaccari |first2=Giulio}}</ref>

On 21 March, the Cuban government sent 52 medical staff (35 doctors and 17 nurses) specialised in infectious diseases who had dealt with the Ebola outbreak. They arrived in Milan on 22 March and entered service in [[Cremona]] on 24 March.<ref>{{cite news |title=Cuban doctors head to Italy battle coronavirus |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-cuba/cuban-doctors-head-to-italy-battle-coronavirus-idUSKBN219051 |agency=Reuters |date=23 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Emergenza Coronavirus, numeri e medici cubani infondono speranz |url=https://www.ilgiorno.it/cremona/cronaca/coronavirus-medici-cubani-1.5078589 |work=Il Giorno Cremona|date=24 March 2020}}</ref>

[[File:Medici Albanesi Covid-19.jpg|thumb|right|250px|Albanian physicians arrived in [[Fiumicino Airport]], April 2020]]
On 21 March, US Secretary of State [[Mike Pompeo]] said that the United States Air Force "sent a C-130 filled with medical supplies to Italy".<ref name="npr_aid"/> On 30 March, US President [[Donald Trump]] said that the US was to send $100&nbsp;million worth of medical and hospital supplies to Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Trump says US to send medical supplies to Italy, France, Spain |url=https://www.france24.com/en/20200330-trump-says-us-to-send-medical-supplies-to-italy-france-spain |accessdate=31 March 2020 |publisher=France 24 |date=30 March 2020 }}</ref>

After a phone call with Conte, Russian president [[Vladimir Putin]] arranged the Russian army to send medical help to Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Russian army to send coronavirus help to Italy after Putin phone call |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-russia-italy/russian-army-to-send-coronavirus-help-to-italy-after-putin-phone-call-idUSKBN219081 |accessdate=22 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=22 March 2020 }}</ref> On 22 March 2020, Russia sent nine [[Military aircraft|military transport planes]] with eight mobile brigades of military medics, a team of about one hundred military virologists and epidemiologists, special disinfection vehicles, and other medical equipment and pharmaceuticals to Italy. The [[fuselage]] of the plane also carried a message for the nation, which read: "From Russia with Love".<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ft.com/content/b1c5681e-6cf9-11ea-89df-41bea055720b|title=Russia sends Italy coronavirus aid to underline historic ties|accessdate=23 March 2020|website=Financial Times}}</ref> President of Lombardy [[Attilio Fontana]] and Italian Foreign Minister [[Luigi Di Maio]] expressed their gratitude for the aid.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Vivaldelli |first1=Roberto | name-list-style = vanc |title=Quelle polemiche infondate sugli aiuti russi all'Italia |url=https://it.insideover.com/politica/quelle-polemiche-infondate-sugli-aiuti-russi-allitalia.html |work=[[Il Giornale]] |date=2020-03-28}}</ref>

The US-based evangelical group [[Samaritan's Purse]] opened a coronavirus field hospital in the parking lot of Cremona hospital.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Sorace |first1=Stephen |title=Samaritan's Purse opens coronavirus field hospital in Italy, receives first patients |url=https://www.foxnews.com/world/italy-evangelical-coronavirus-field-hospital |accessdate=23 March 2020 |publisher=Fox News Channel |date=22 March 2020}}</ref>

On 24 March, Germany took in six coronavirus patients from the Bergamo hospital to be treated in Saxony.<ref>{{cite news |title=Germany treats first Italians as coronavirus care crosses borders |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-germany-italy-idUSKBN21B2GL |accessdate=29 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=24 March 2020 }}</ref> Later the same week, the German health minister said that Germany would take in a total of at least 47 Italian patients.<ref>{{cite news |title=Germany Takes in 47 Coronavirus Patients From Italy |url=https://www.usnews.com/news/world/articles/2020-03-26/germany-takes-in-47-coronavirus-patients-from-italy |accessdate=29 March 2020 |work=US News |agency=Reuters |date=26 March 2020}}</ref>
On 25 March, a C-130 from Ramstein Air Base in Germany delivered humanitarian supplies to Aviano Air Base.<ref>{{Cite web | url=https://www.joint-forces.com/world-news/30519-us-humanitarian-assistance-support-to-italy |title = US Humanitarian Assistance Support to Italy|date = 25 March 2020}}</ref>

Somalia sent twenty volunteer doctors to Italy to help fight COVID-19.<ref>{{cite news |title=Somalia sending 20 doctors to help Italy fight virus |url=https://www.aa.com.tr/en/africa/somalia-sending-20-doctors-to-help-italy-fight-virus/1782154 |accessdate=27 March 2020 |work=aa.com.tr}}</ref> Albania also sent a group of thirty medical staff members to Lombardy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, l'Albania invia medici e infermieri: "Non dimentichiamo l'Italia che ci ha aiutato" |url=https://www.repubblica.it/esteri/2020/03/29/news/coronavirus_medici_albania_italia-252593099/?ref=RHPPTP-BH-I252538519-C12-P4-S4.4-T1 |accessdate=29 March 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=28 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref> Serbia sent four planes carrying medical equipment to Italy.<ref>[https://www.usnews.com/news/world/articles/2020-04-25/serbia-sends-four-planes-carrying-medical-equipment-to-italy Serbia Sends Four Planes Carrying Medical Equipment to Italy] 25 April 2020 ''www.usnews.com'', accessed 30 May 2020</ref>

==Impact==
===Healthcare===
The pandemic outbreak heightened the pressure on the Italian healthcare system.<ref>{{cite news|work=[[The New York Times]]|url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/03/12/world/europe/12italy-coronavirus-health-care.html |title=Italy's Health Care System Groans Under Coronavirus – a Warning to the World|access-date=3 April 2020|date=12 March 2020|first=Jason|last=Horowitz}}</ref>

On 9 March, Alessia Bonari, a nurse from Grosseto who worked at a hospital in Milan, posted on Instagram stating that she was physically strained from being overworked and was scared to work after treating over 10,000 patients who have tested positive. Bonari and her co-workers had been extremely exhausted due to the pressures of work, and according to her, health caretakers had been working in uncomfortable conditions. The post, which reached global notoriety, contained a photo of her bruised face from wearing unfit masks and hazmat goggles, and stated that "the protective devices are bad." She concluded her post persuading others "to be selfless, to stay at home and thus protect those who are most fragile."<ref>{{cite web|url=https://7news.com.au/lifestyle/health-wellbeing/coronavirus-italy-instagram-post-from-milan-nurse-shows-bruised-face-from-hazmat-gear-c-739675|title=Coronavirus Italy: Instagram post from Milan nurse shows bruised face from hazmat gear|website=7news|last=Burke|first=Kelly|date=10 March 2020|accessdate=26 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://news.sky.com/story/coronavirus-bruised-by-face-masks-nurses-show-the-impact-of-fighting-the-pandemic-11955457|title=Coronavirus: Italian nurses share the startling reality of fighting the pandemic|date=13 March 2020|accessdate=26 April 2020|website=Sky News}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://nypost.com/2020/03/11/im-afraid-too-coronavirus-nurse-posts-photo-of-face-bruised-from-mask/|title='I'm afraid, too': Coronavirus nurse posts photo of face bruised from mask|website=New York Post|last=Salo|first=Jackie|date=11 March 2020|accessdate=26 April 2020}}</ref>

[[File:Covid-19 San Salvatore 08.jpg|left|thumb|An intensive care nurse, showing her bruised face during the peak of the pandemic, in [[Pesaro]]]]
On 17 March, undersecretary at the [[Ministry of Health (Italy)|Ministry of Health]] [[Sandra Zampa]] announced the purchase of many new [[ventilator]]s as well as the importing of one and a half million masks from [[South Africa]].<ref name="la7.it"/>

In order to deal with the numbers of COVID-19 patients, [[intensive care unit]]s were expanded, and new hospitals were created, especially in Lombardy.<ref>{{cite news|language=it |work=[[La Stampa]]|date=1 April 2020|access-date=1 April 2020 |title=Coronavirus, l'uomo che ha moltiplicato i letti di terapia intensiva in Lombardia: "Ora la situazione è stabile"|url= https://www.lastampa.it/topnews/primo-piano/2020/04/01/news/coronavirus-il-primario-chi-esce-di-casa-deve-indossare-sempre-la-mascherina-1.38664361}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|work=[[The Independent]]|access-date=1 April 2020|url=https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/coroanvirus-italy-hospital-milan-lombardy-cases-deaths-a9438761.html |title=Coronavirus: Italy's worst-hit region builds new hospital in 10 days|first= Federica |last=Marsi}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it |publisher=[[La Repubblica]]|url= https://video.repubblica.it/dossier/coronavirus-wuhan-2020/coronavirus-ospedale-da-campo-in-tempi-record-a-bergamo-la-gioia-dei-volontari/357254/357814?ref=RHPPTP-BS-I252667351-C12-P8-S6.4-F1 |format=video|date=1 April 2020|access-date=1 April 2020|title= Coronavirus, ospedale da campo in tempi record a Bergamo: la gioia dei volontari}}</ref> In Emilia-Romagna, professor Marco Ranieri developed a method to double the efficiency of ventilators in ICUs.<ref>{{cite web|language=it |publisher=[[Il Riformista]]|title=Un ventilatore per due pazienti, la scoperta italiana che raddoppia i posti in terapia intensiva  |date= 26 March 2020 |access-date=26 March 2020 |url=https://www.ilriformista.it/un-ventilatore-per-due-pazienti-la-scoperta-italiana-che-raddoppia-i-posti-in-terapia-intensiva-65657/}}</ref> The lack of a single protocol for hospitals was considered to be a problem.<ref>{{cite web|language=it |work=[[La Stampa]]|title=Un protocollo nazionale dagli ospedali più virtuosi|url=https://www.lastampa.it/topnews/lettere-e-idee/2020/03/30/news/un-protocollo-nazionale-dagli-ospedali-piu-virtuosi-1.38653841 |date=30 March 2020|access-date=1 April 2020 |first=Nicola|last=Bedin}}</ref>

Due to hospitals overcrowding with coronavirus patients, thousands of cancer patients experienced difficulties in getting access to treatment and transplants, with their lives put at even higher risk. Dozens of cancer hospital sections were indeed either dedicated to host coronavirus wards, or closed after personnel got infected.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tondo |first1=Lorenzo |title=Life 'hanging by a thread' for Italian cancer patients in coronavirus crisis |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/apr/07/life-hanging-by-a-thread-for-italian-cancer-patients-in-coronavirus-crisis |accessdate=7 April 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=7 April 2020}}</ref> According to a study, cancer patients represented 17% of coronavirus fatalities in Italy.<ref>{{cite web |title=Caratteristiche dei pazienti deceduti positivi a COVID-19 in Italia |url=https://www.epicentro.iss.it/coronavirus/sars-cov-2-decessi-italia#3 |website=epicentro.iss.it |publisher=Istituto Superiore di Sanità |accessdate=7 April 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

A letter published on the ''NEJM Catalyst Innovations in Care Delivery'' claimed that one of the reasons for the high death count in the area of Bergamo was hospital contamination.<ref>{{cite journal |last1=Nacoti |first1=Mirco |last2=Ciocca |first2=Andrea |last3=Giupponi |first3=Angelo |last4=Brambillasca |first4=Pietro |last5=Lussana |first5=Federico |last6=Pisano |first6=Michele |last7=Goisis |first7=Giuseppe |last8=Bonacina |first8=Daniele |last9=Fazzi |first9=Francesco |last10=Naspro |first10=Richard |last11=Longhi |first11=Luca |last12=Cereda |first12=Maurizio |last13=Montaguti |first13=Carlo |title=At the Epicenter of the Covid-19 Pandemic and Humanitarian Crises in Italy: Changing Perspectives on Preparation and Mitigation |journal=NEJM Catalyst Innovations in Care Delivery |year=2020 |volume=1 |issue=2 |doi=10.1056/CAT.20.0080 |url=https://catalyst.nejm.org/doi/full/10.1056/CAT.20.0080 |accessdate=5 April 2020 |publisher=Massachusetts Medical Society|doi-broken-date=18 October 2020 }}</ref> Progressively, different hospitals became dedicated to COVID-19 patients only, and more rigid separations were set up between hospital sections and [[triage]] structures.<ref>{{cite web|title= Coronavirus, Piemonte: riorganizzazione degli ospedali|url=https://www.askanews.it/cronaca/2020/03/07/coronavirus-piemonte-riorganizzazione-degli-ospedali-pn_20200307_00163/  |date=21 March 2020|agency= askanews|language=it|access-date=1 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|title= Vittorio Veneto è "ospedale COVID": chiusi tutti i reparti|language=it |publisher=[[Il Gazzettino]]|url=https://www.ilgazzettino.it/nordest/treviso/vittorio_veneto_ospedale_covid_reparti_chiusura-5123239.html |access-date=1 April 2020|date=21 March 2020|first=Claudia|last=Borsoi}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it |url=https://qds.it/asp-trapani-cambia-piano-organizzativo-ospedale-marsala-diventa-covid-hospital/|access-date=1 April 2020|first=Gabriele|last=d'Amico |publisher=[[Quotidiano di Sicilia]]|title=Asp Tp, ospedale Marsala diventa Covid-hospital}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it|access-date=2 April 2020 |url=https://www.ilrestodelcarlino.it/modena/cronaca/con-il-nostro-pre-triage-aiutiamo-gli-ospedali-1.5089778 |title=Con il nostro pre-triage aiutiamo gli ospedali |first=Roberto|last=Grimaldi|work=[[Il Resto del Carlino]]}}</ref> In some regions, hotels were used to host healthcare workers or patients,<ref>{{cite news|language=it |date=30 March 2020 |url=https://bari.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/30/news/coronavirus_hotel_a_4_stelle_bari_per_medici_e_personale_policlinico-252731747/ |title=Coronavirus, hotel a 4 stelle a Bari ospita medici e personale dei reparti Covid del Policlinico: "Fino a fine emergenza"|work=[[La Repubblica]]|access-date=2 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it |url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/04/01/coronavirus-a-roma-alberghi-requisiti-per-ospitare-i-pazienti-in-via-di-guarigione-il-piano-della-regione-lazio-per-affrontare-lemergenza/5756431/ |access-date=1 April 2020|title=Coronavirus, a Roma alberghi requisiti per ospitare i pazienti in via di guarigione: il piano della Regione Lazio per affrontare l'emergenza|first=Vincenzo|last=Bisbiglia |work=[[Il Fatto Quotidiano]]|date=1 April 2020}}</ref> and in Liguria a ship was adapted to host people in quarantine.<ref>{{cite web|language=it |title=Pronta Splendid, la prima nave ospedale per degenti post-Covid-19 |url=https://www.ilsole24ore.com/art/pronta-splendid-prima-nave-ospedale-degenti-post-covid-19-AD6NHJE |access-date=1 April 2020|first=Raoul |last=de Forcade|publisher=[[Il Sole 24 Ore]]}}</ref> On 1 April, the first Italian drive-through testing facilities opened in [[Alessandria]]<ref>{{cite news |language=it |url=https://torino.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/04/01/news/alessandria_tampone_in_auto_come_al_drive_in_ne_faremo_300_al_giorno_-252867384/?ref=RHPPLF-BH-I252756236-C8-P8-S5.2-T1 |title= Alessandria, tampone in auto come al drive in: "Ne faremo 300 al giorno" |first=Federica |last=Cravero |publisher=[[La Repubblica]]}}</ref> and in north-western Tuscany.<ref>{{cite news |language=it |url=https://www.lanazione.it/pisa/cronaca/coronavirus-test-1.5088065|publisher=[[La Nazione]]|date=30 March 2020|access-date=7 April 2020|title=Covid -19: via ai tamponi in auto nell'Asl Nord Ovest}}</ref>

At least ten different [[clinical trial]]s were ongoing in Italian hospitals at the beginning of April.<ref name=PortaaPorta>{{cite AV media |date=n.d.|title=I 10 farmaci in sperimentazione in Italia per frenare il Coronavirus  |medium=Television production|language=it |url= https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=N-CljlaL844|access-date= 5 April 2020 |publisher= [[Porta a Porta]]-[[RAI]]}}</ref> The [[supercomputer]] of [[ENEA (Italy)|ENEA]] in Portici was used to run advanced simulations related to other possible drugs.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date=30 March 2020|url=https://it.notizie.yahoo.com/covid-19-supercomputer-enea-per-la-ricerca-su-095327433.html |agency= askanews|title=Covid-19, supercomputer Enea per la ricerca su farmaci e vaccini}}</ref> Some of the treatments employed for COVID-19 patients involved the administration of antiviral drugs. [[Remdesivir]] was tested with promising initial results in Naples.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|title=Coronavirus, il professor Paolo Maggi: "39enne guarito con il farmaco Remdesivir, primo caso al Sud"|first=Anna Laura|last=De Rosa|date=31 March 2020|access-date=2 April 2020|publisher=[[La Repubblica]]|url= https://napoli.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/31/news/coronavirus_il_professor_paolo_maggi_paziente_guarito_con_il_farmaco_remdesivir_-252738358/?ref=RHPPLF-BH-I252750617-C8-P7-S2.5-T1}}</ref> Despite doubts from the scientific community, [[Avigan]] (favipiravir) was also included in testing protocols by [[Italian Medicines Agency]] (AIFA) even though it was not authorised in Europe.<ref name=PortaaPorta/><ref>{{cite news|language=it|date=23 March 2020|url=https://www.rainews.it/tgr/veneto/video/2020/03/ven-Sperimentazione-farmaci-avigan-aifa-scienziati-effetti-collaterali-Enrico-Bucci-Philadelphia-temple-university-8d5c442d-f847-4c4e-b84b-ee9dce01f0d1.html |title= Sperimentazione Avigan, le perplessità della comunità scientifica  |first=Maurizio|last=Menicucci |publisher=[[TGR]]|format=video}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it|date=23 March 2020|url=https://www.corriere.it/salute/malattie_infettive/20_marzo_23/avigan-via-sperimentazione-17ada1f4-6d19-11ea-ba71-0c6303b9bf2d.shtml |title=Avigan, c'è il via libera dell'Aifa alla sperimentazione per Covid-19 |first=Laura |last=Cuppini}}</ref> Similarly to France, [[hydroxychloroquine]] (the less toxic version of the malaria drug chloroquine) was also tested:<ref name=PortaaPorta/><ref>{{cite news|language=it|first=Sarah|last= Boseley|work=[[The Guardian]]|date=27 March 2020|title=Vital drug for people with lupus running out after unproven Covid-19 link|access-date=3 April 2020|url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/27/vital-drug-people-lupus-coronavirus-covid-19-link-hydroxychloroquine}}</ref> in Lazio, its use was reported by the second week of April on a significant fraction of the roughly a thousand COVID-19 patients confined at home.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|first=Mauro|last= Evangelisti|work=[[Il Messaggero]]|date=12 April 2020|title=COVID19, vicepresidente ordine medici di Roma: "Cure a casa con la clorochina, la terapia sta funzionando "|access-date=12 April 2020|url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/salute/medicina/coronavirus_clorochina_cura_farmaco_12_aprile_2020-5166720.html|archive-date=12 April 2020 |archive-url=https://www.dagospia.com/rubrica-39/salute/non-dite-anti-trumpiani-che-clorochina-sta-funzionando-roma-233175.htm}}</ref> Plasma treatment already tried in China (transfer of antibodies from recovered COVID-19 patients to sick people) was tested at the hospital of Pavia (and later in Mantua) under the supervision of professor Cesare Perotti;<ref name=Repubblica20200204Plasma>{{cite news|language=it|date= 2 April 2020 |url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/04/02/news/coronavirus_lombardia_a_mantova_e_pavia_studiano_l_uso_del_plasmia_dei_guariti_per_curare_gli_aammalati-252947630/|title=Coronavirus, a Mantova e Pavia si studia l'uso del plasma dei guariti per curare gli ammalati|work=[[La Repubblica]]|access-date= 4 April 2020}}</ref> the first two donors involved in the research programme were a married couple, both doctors and among the first COVID-19 patients reported in the province.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 2 April 2020 |url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/salute/ricerca/coronavirus_plasma_cure_pavia_ultime_notizie_oggi_2_aprile_2020-5148595.html |title=Coronavirus, malati curati con il plasma dei guariti: a Pavia la sperimentazione|work=[[Il Messaggero]]|access-date= 3 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 2 April 2020 |url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/04/02/coronavirus-plasmaterapia-per-i-pazienti-al-san-matteo-di-pavia-tecnica-ereditata-da-epidemia-di-ebola-e-sars-e-poi-usata-in-cina/5757985/ |title=Coronavirus, plasmaterapia per i pazienti al San Matteo di Pavia. Tecnica "ereditata" da epidemia di Ebola e Sars e poi usata in Cina|work=[[Il Fatto Quotidiano]]|access-date= 2 April 2020}}</ref> The final results published in May showed a reduction in mortality.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 11 May 2020 |url=https://milano.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/05/11/news/con_cura_plasma_mortalita_ridotta_dal_15_al_6_risultati_sperimentazione_san_matteo_pavia_e_asst_mantova-256327648/?ref=RHPPLF-BH-I256321920-C8-P2-S3.4-T1|work=[[La Repubblica]]|access-date= 23 May 2020  |title= Coronavirus, cura con il plasma: mortalità ridotta dal 15% al 6%, la sperimentazione del San Matteo di Pavia e dell'Azienda di Mantova}}</ref> In the beginning of April, based on the results of autopsies showing the presence of micro-[[thrombosis]] in the lungs of COVID-19 patients, doctors in Tuscany and other areas of northern Italy started to use [[heparin]] to reduce the risk of blood clotting;<ref name=Campanella2020>{{cite news|first=G. Flavio|last=Campanella|language=it|date= 11 April 2020 |url=https://www.lagazzettadelmezzogiorno.it/news/bari/1218599/bari-molecola-di-dio-contro-la-covid-19-l-eparina-e-efficace-forse-ci-siamo.html|title=Coronavirus: dai medici in prima linea e dalle prime autopsie una ipotesi nuova sulle cause dei decessi, ma anche sulle cure|work=[[La Gazzetta del Mezzogiorno]]|access-date= 14 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|first=Fabio|last=Martini|language=it|date= 12 April 2020 |url=https://www.lanazione.it/pontedera/cronaca/coronavirus-cure-1.5101478|title=Coronavirus: dai medici in prima linea e dalle prime autopsie una ipotesi nuova sulle cause dei decessi, ma anche sulle cure|work=[[La Stampa]]|access-date= 13 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|first=Ilenia |last=Pistolesi|language=it|date= 10 April 2020 |url=https://www.lanazione.it/pontedera/cronaca/coronavirus-cure-1.5101478|title=Coronavirus, "La cura sperimentale con l'eparina funziona"|work=[[La Nazione]]|access-date= 13 April 2020}}</ref> the news was originally circulating on social media from internal chats of healthcare workers and considered a hoax by virologist [[Roberto Burioni]],<ref>{{cite news|first=Marco|last=Benedetto|language=it|date= 11 April 2020 |url=https://www.blitzquotidiano.it/cronaca-italia/coronavirus-e-trombosi-massimo-boldi-gira-il-post-ai-medicidibattito-su-fb-3173693/|title=Coronavirus e trombosi. Massimo Boldi gira il post ai medici: dibattito su Fb|work=[[Blitz Quotidiano]]|access-date= 13 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 11 April 2020 |url=https://www.iltempo.it/cronache/2020/04/11/news/roberto-burioni-bufala-medico-pavia-cardiologo-polmonite-trombosi-antinfiuammatori-antibiotici-1313456/|title=Polmonite o trombosi? Roberto Burioni fa a pezzi la bufala del medico di Pavia|work=[[Il Tempo]]|access-date= 13 April 2020}}</ref> but protocols including [[low-molecular-weight heparin]] were formally submitted as a treatment proposal to AIFA.<ref name=Campanella2020/> A programme involving 14 research centres was approved on 13 April.<ref>{{cite news|title=Coronavirus, Aifa autorizza uno studio sull' eparina|work=[[La Stampa]]|language=it|date= 14 April 2020 |url=https://www.lastampa.it/cronaca/2020/04/14/news/coronavirus-aifa-autorizza-uno-studio-sull-eparina-1.38716259}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|title=Eparina, arma contro il coronavirus. Ma la sua efficacia è in dubbio|work=[[Il Giornale]]|language=it|date= 13 April 2020 |url=https://www.ilgiornale.it/news/cronache/eparina-arma-contro-coronavirus-sua-efficacia-dubbio-1853385.html}}</ref>

[[File:Coronavirus Italy.jpg|thumb|upright=1.13|Nurses of the coronavirus task force to support health structures in [[Northern Italy]]]]

The workforce of the healthcare system underwent massive reorganisation. Pediatricians were assigned to adult patients and as a result, their insurance coverage had to be adapted.<ref>{{cite magazine |page= 16|date=March 2020 |title=Estensione Polizza RC SiP |url=https://docs.sip.it/2020/sito_sip/Pediatria3_web.pdf |language=it |magazine= Pediatria|publisher=SIP – Società Italiana di Pediatria |access-date=2 April 2020}}</ref> Retired professionals were asked to go back to work to fill the vacancies, despite the high risk for their age group.<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.ilgazzettino.it/nordest/belluno/coronavirus_emergenza_medici_pensionati-5107073.html |access-date=2 April 2020|title=Coronavirus, emergenza medici. Erano già in pensione: tornano quattro dottori, hanno tra i 65 e i 71 anni|publisher=[[Il Gazzettino]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=16 March 2020  |title= Coronavirus, arrivano i medici pensionati |language=it |work=[[Il Messaggero]] |url=https://www.ilmessaggero.it/umbria/coronavirus_sale_164_numero_contagiati-5114409.html |access-date=2 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |language=it |url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/03/05/sono-le-venti-nove-un-medico-pensionato-richiamato-in-servizio-per-il-coronavirus-letica-viene-prima-ma-colleghi-over-65-sono-a-rischio/5727237/ |access-date=2 April 2020|title=Sono le Venti (Nove), un medico pensionato richiamato in servizio per il coronavirus: "L'etica viene prima. Ma colleghi over 65 sono a rischio"|date= 5 March 2020}}</ref> At the peak of the pandemics volunteers from the rest of the country were sent to hospitals in critical areas of northern and central Italy.<ref>{{cite news |date=3 April 2020  |title=In Piemonte oltre mille morti. Arrivano i medici volontari contro il coronavirus |language=it |work=[[La Stampa]] |url=https://www.lastampa.it/torino/2020/04/03/news/in-piemonte-oltre-mille-morti-arrivano-i-medici-volontari-contro-il-coronavirus-1.38673210 |access-date=15 April 2020|first=Alessandro|last=Mondo}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |date=24 March 2020 |title=Corse dei treni gratuite per tutti i medici volontari diretti negli ospedali del Nord Italia |language=it|work=[[Il Secolo XIX]] |url=https://www.ilsecoloxix.it/italia/2020/03/24/news/corse-dei-treni-gratuite-per-tutti-i-medici-volontari-diretti-negli-ospedali-del-nord-italia-1.38632210 |access-date=15 April 2020}}</ref>

Healthcare workers were also affected by coronavirus infections, with a higher percentage of the infected healthcare workers being women because of their predominance among nurses.<ref name=Capocci2020>{{cite news|language=it|work=[[Il Manifesto]]|url=https://ilmanifesto.it/la-strage-dei-medici-di-base-sono-piu-della-meta-dei-dottori-morti/ |title=La strage dei medici di base, sono più della metà dei dottori morti|date=26 March 2020|access-date=2 April 2020 |first=Andrea|last=Capocci}}</ref> This resulted in death in a considerable number of cases, especially amongst general practitioners.<ref name=Capocci2020/><ref>{{cite news|language=it|title=Elenco dei Medici caduti nel corso dell'epidemia di Covid-19|url=https://portale.fnomceo.it/elenco-dei-medici-caduti-nel-corso-dellepidemia-di-covid-19/ |publisher=Federazione nazionale degli ordini dei medici chirurghi e degli odontoiatri|access-date=2 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it |url=https://www.quotidianodelsud.it/laltravocedellitalia/due-italie/saluteeassistenza/2020/03/21/coronavirus-emergenza-medici-richiamati-i-pensionati |title=Coronavirus: emergenza medici, richiamati i pensionati|publisher=[[Il Quotidiano del Sud]]|first=Francesco|last=Specchia |date= 21 March 2020|access-date=2 April 2020}}</ref> By the end of March, more than 60 doctors in Italy had died with COVID-19,<ref>{{cite web |title=More Than 60 Doctors in Italy Have Died in COVID-19 Pandemic |url=https://www.medscape.com/viewarticle/927753 |website=[[Medscape]]|date=30 March 2020}}</ref> and the figure increased to 80 by 4 April<ref>{{cite web |title=Coronavirus, salgono a 80 i medici morti in Italia|url=https://www.adnkronos.com/fatti/cronaca/2020/04/04/coronavirus-salgono-medici-morti-italia_n2cEQuHSyTnreuqhOKDjiN.html?refresh_ce|agency=[[Adnkronos]]|date=4 April 2020|access-date=4 April 2020}}</ref> and later 145 by 22 April.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 22 April 2020 |title=Coronavirus in Italia, muore un anestesista: 145 medici uccisi dal virus|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/04/22/news/coronavirus_in_italia_contagi_morti_e_tutte_le_news_sulla_situazione-254661588/?ref=RHPPTP-BH-I254721612-C8-P1-S4.3-T1 |access-date=22 April 2020|publisher=[[La Repubblica]]}}</ref> Healthcare personnel were also subject to high levels of stress,<ref>{{cite news|language=it |url=https://www.internazionale.it/reportage/annalisa-camilli/2020/04/01/coronavirus-psicologi-medici-infermieri |title=Il dolore invisibile dei medici in corsia contro il coronavirus |first=Annalisa |last=Camilli|access-date=1 April 2020|date=1 April 2020}}</ref> and the risk of professional burn-out was considered high, particularly across nurses and in more affected areas.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 30 March 2020 |url=https://www.ansa.it/canale_saluteebenessere/notizie/sanita/2020/03/29/coronavirus-ordini-degli-infermieri-4-mila-i-contagiati_e5d63b67-193d-42e9-8dff-933c7ecb0785.html |access-date=3 April 2020|agency=ANSA|title=Coronavirus: Ordini degli infermieri, 4 mila i contagiati}}</ref> Two suicides, one of a nurse in Jesolo and one of a nurse in Monza, were assumed to be related to psychological pressure.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 18 March 2020 |title=Jesolo, si suicida infermiera che lavorava nel reparto di terapia intensiva con i pazienti malati di coronavirus  |url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/18/news/jesolo_si_suicida_infermiera_che_lavorava_nel_reparto_di_terapia_intensiva_con_i_pazienti_malati_di_coronavirus-251635576/ |access-date=2 April 2020|publisher=[[La Repubblica]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 24 March 2020 |title=Suicida a Monza un'infermiera di terapia intensiva|url=https://www.agi.it/cronaca/news/2020-03-24/infermiera-suicida-monza-positiva-coronavirus-7815160/ |access-date=31 March 2020 }}</ref>

The emergency was an occasion to test or develop new protocols based on digital technologies. With the aim of reducing consumption of protective equipment, robots were introduced in hospitals in Varese,<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 3 April 2020 |title=Arrivano i robot-medici che dialogano con i pazienti: "Come si sente?"|url= https://video.repubblica.it/dossier/coronavirus-wuhan-2020/coronavirus-in-trincea-arrivano-i-robot-medici-che-dialogano-con-i-pazienti-come-si-sente/357390/357950?ref=RHPPRB-BS-I0-C4-P5-S1.4-T1 |access-date=3 April 2020|work=[[La Repubblica]]|first=Daniele|last=Alberti}}</ref> and remote diagnostics were introduced to monitor home care patients in Lodi.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 24 March 2020 |url=https://www.agi.it/cronaca/news/2020-03-28/coronavirus-telemedicina-lodi-zucchetti-7958552/ |title=L'ospedale di Lodi sperimenta la telemedicina sviluppata da un'azienda locale|access-date=2 April 2020|agency=[[Agenzia Giornalistica Italia]]|first=Alessio|last=Nisi}}</ref> To facilitate home calls from patients, ''[[Istituto Italiano di Tecnologia]]'' in Genoa (IIT) and ''Istituto di robotica e macchine intelligenti'' (I-RIM) designed a robot for video calls that could be assembled by hospital personnel<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 30 March 2020 |title=Coronavirus, robot in ospedale per le videochiamate tra pazienti e famiglie|url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_marzo_30/coronavirus-robot-ospedale-le-videochiamate-pazienti-famiglie-37420a12-7289-11ea-bc49-338bb9c7b205.shtml |access-date=1 April 2020|first=Giovanni|last=Viafora |work=[[Corriere della Sera]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 30 March 2020 |title=Le soluzioni Zucchetti e Bitdefender per il Covid-19|url=https://www.tomshw.it/business/le-soluzioni-zucchetti-e-bitdefender-per-il-covid-19/ |publisher=[[Tom's Hardware]]|first=Antonino|last=Caffo|access-date=2 April 2020}}</ref> and that was tested at the end of April in Pisa, Massa-Carrara and Induno Olona.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 24 April 2020 |title=Coronavirus, negli ospedali i primi robot teleguidati che consentono ai pazienti di video-chiamare a casa |url=https://www.corriere.it/video-articoli/2020/04/24/coronavirus-ospedali-primi-robot-teleguidati-che-consentono-pazienti-video-chiamare-casa/fc014fc4-8581-11ea-b71d-7609e1287c32.shtml|publisher=[[Corriere della Sera]]|format=video|first=Giovanni|last=Viafora|access-date=24 April 2020}}</ref> The ''Policlinico Universitario'' in Rome tested AI software for fast analysis of chest X-rays.<ref>{{cite news|language=it|date= 30 March 2020 |url=https://innovazione.tiscali.it/intelligenza-artificiale/articoli/Diagnosi-del-coronavirus-Italia-ha-acquistato-intelligenza-artificiale-cinese/ |publisher=[[Tiscali]]|access-date=1 April 2020 |first=Michael |last=Pontrelli |title= Diagnosi del coronavirus, l'Italia ha acquistato l'intelligenza artificiale cinese}}</ref>

===Economy===
{{See also|Financial market impact of the COVID-19 pandemic}}
[[File:Emergenza coronavirus (49651209716).jpg|thumb|right|upright=1.13|Sets of [[personal protective equipment]] in a Civil Protection hub, ready to be distributed to the regions]]
The pandemic provoked large economic damage to the Italian economy. The sectors of tourism, accommodation and food services were among the hardest hit by foreign countries' limitations to travel to Italy, and by the nationwide lockdown imposed by the government on 8 March.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Brunton |first1=John |title='Nothing less than a catastrophe': Venice left high and dry by coronavirus |url=https://www.theguardian.com/travel/2020/mar/17/nothing-less-than-a-catastrophe-venice-left-high-and-dry-by-coronavirus |accessdate=19 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=17 March 2020}}</ref> By April, finance minister [[Roberto Gualtieri]] predicted a 6% GDP decline for 2020.<ref name=FT6April/>

On 12 March, the Italian stock market was among the worst hit during [[2020 stock market crash#Black Thursday (12 March)|Black Thursday]], when the FTSE MIB index lost 17% of its value in one day.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Za |first1=Valentina |last2=Allen |first2=Nathan |title=Italy, Spain curb trading to stem coronavirus market crash |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-europe-stocks-short-selling/italy-spain-curb-trading-to-stem-coronavirus-market-crash-idUSKBN2101LN |accessdate=19 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=13 March 2020 }}</ref>

Multiple factories, like [[Fiat Chrysler Automobiles|Fiat Chrysler]], halted production in some of their plants.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Ghiglione |first1=Davide |last2=Romei |first2=Valentina |last3=Hall |first3=Ben |title=Italy faces mounting economic damage from coronavirus |url=https://www.ft.com/content/d0565f72-5fcf-11ea-b0ab-339c2307bcd4 |accessdate=19 March 2020 |work=Financial Times |date=12 March 2020}}</ref> On 21 March, the government issued the shutdown of all non-essential businesses, industries, and economic activities.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Bertacche |first1=Marco |last2=Orihuela |first2=Rodrigo |last3=Colten |first3=Jerrold |title=Italy Struck by Deadliest Day as Virus Prompts Industry Shutdown |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2020-03-21/germany-plans-extra-spending-of-eu150-billion-scholz-says |accessdate=2 April 2020 |work=Bloomberg |date=21 March 2020}}</ref>

''[[The Economist]]'' predicts a 7% GDP decline for Italy in 2020.<ref name="France24">{{cite news |title=Mafia primed to feast on Italy's virus devastation |url=https://www.france24.com/en/20200329-mafia-primed-to-feast-on-italy-s-virus-devastation |accessdate=11 April 2020 |work=France 24 |date=29 March 2020 |language=en}}</ref> Economist Alberto Bisin forecast that Italy's [[debt-to-GDP ratio]] would rise from 130% to 180% by the end of the year, due to borrowing and losses.<ref name="future">{{cite news |title=Italy's future is in German hands |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/coronavirus-italy-future-germany/ |accessdate=2 April 2020 |work=Politico |date=2 April 2020}}</ref> Multiple economists believe that Italy will struggle to pay back its debt.<ref name="future" /><ref name=FT6April/>

Although the virus has hit northern Italy hardest, economically deprived areas of southern Italy are suffering the most from the lockdown. Many residents of those areas work in the [[grey economy]] and are therefore not eligible for unemployment benefits.<ref>{{cite news |last1=CNN |first1=Barbie Latza Nadeau and Valentina Di Donato |title=As northern Italy is ravaged by coronavirus, there's trouble brewing down south |url=https://www.cnn.com/2020/04/04/europe/southern-italy-coronavirus-black-economy-intl/index.html |accessdate=11 April 2020 |work=CNN}}</ref> In some places the [[Italian mafia]] was reported to be delivering groceries to needy residents. Prosecutors warned that the mafia was not acting out of altruism and was instead seeking control over residents.<ref>{{cite news |title=Mafia distributes food to Italy's struggling residents |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/apr/10/mafia-distributes-food-to-italys-struggling-residents |accessdate=11 April 2020 |work=the Guardian |date=10 April 2020 |language=en}}</ref><ref name="France24" />

====Conversion of production to medical supplies====
{{See also|Shortages related to the COVID-19 pandemic}}
Some Italian small and medium-sized enterprises partially or totally converted their production to supply personal protective equipment at a local scale. Many of these items could not be approved for hospital use, but they were considered useful to supply demand for the general population.<ref name=DeStefaniLaStampa>{{cite news|url=https://www.lastampa.it/economia/2020/03/18/news/la-grande-corsa-alla-riconversione-chi-creava-vestiti-ora-fa-mascherine-1.38605102|date=18 March 2020 |title= La grande corsa alla riconversione: chi creava vestiti ora fa mascherine|first1=Gabriele|last1=De Stefani|work=[[La Stampa]]|access-date=22 March 2020|language=it}}</ref>

[[File:Mascherine regalate dalla Grafica Veneta alla Regione Veneto.jpg|thumb|left|300px|The protective masks donated by Grafica Veneta to the Region of Veneto]]

In Veneto, Grafica Veneta – the printing company of the ''Harry Potter'' books in Italian – started to mass-produce protective masks.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.repubblica.it/economia/2020/03/22/news/coronavirus_mascherine-252001308/?ref=RHPPTP-BH-I252011244-C12-P1-S3.4-T1|first=Marco |last=Patucchi|date=22 March 2020|access-date=23 March 2020|title=Coronavirus, lo stampatore di libri che dona mascherine: "Ho conosciuto la morte, non potevo sottrarmi"|publisher=[[La Repubblica]]}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/03/18/coronavirus-grafica-veneta-riconverte-produzione-4-milioni-di-mascherine-al-giorno-gratis-alla-popolazione/5740755/|title=Coronavirus, Grafica Veneta riconverte produzione: 4 milioni di mascherine al giorno "gratis alla popolazione"|language=it|work=[[Il Fatto Quotidiano]]|first= Giuseppe |last=Pietrobelli |date=18 March 2020|access-date=22 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.ilgazzettino.it/nordest/padova/coronavirus_grafica_veneta_produzione_mascherine-5114284.html|title=Grafica Veneta pronta a produrre "mascherine", Zaia: "Saranno le prime "made in Veneto""|language=it|publisher=[[Il Gazzettino]]|date=16 March 2020|access-date=18 March 2020}}</ref>
In Piedmont, Ci.Ti.Elle, a company from [[Castiglione Torinese]] specialising in textiles for hotels, put its twelve employers to assembling surgical masks for the regional ''Protezione Civile'', and the hospitals of San Maurizio Canavese, Alessandria and Chivasso, with the support the Filmar company from Caselle for the elastics.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.lastampa.it/torino/2020/03/20/news/coronavirus-l-azienda-si-converte-dai-tessuti-per-gli-hotel-alle-mascherine-distribuite-gratis-1.38617334|date=21 March 2020 |title= Coronavirus, l'azienda si converte: dai tessuti per gli hotel alle mascherine distribuite gratis|first1=Nadia |last1=Bergamini|first2=Andrea |last2=Bucci |work=[[La Stampa]]|access-date=22 March 2020|language=it}}</ref>
In Lombardy Cifra, a manufacturer from [[Verano Brianza]] specialising in sportswear, also converted its production line.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://rep.repubblica.it/pwa/generale/2020/03/23/news/dai_body_sportivi_alle_mascherine_la_fabbrica_che_reagisce_all_emergenza-252117447/?ref=RHPPTP-BH-I252124970-C12-P1-S4.4-T1|date=23 March 2020 |title= Dai body sportivi alle mascherine la fabbrica che reagisce all'emergenza|publisher=[[La Repubblica]]|access-date=24 March 2020|language=it|first=Marco|last=Patucchi}}</ref>
In the textile district of the [[province of Prato]], the Machattie company started production of polypropylene masks in March, and the Dreoni company in [[Vaiano]] switched its production from car upholstery to protective masks with certified standard, with the help of the local population (its owner later died of COVID-19).<ref name=DeStefaniLaStampa/><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2020/05/17/sergio-dreoni-il-primo-imprenditore-toscano-a-riconvertire-la-sua-produzione-per-donare-mascherine-onesto-e-appassionato/5803797/|title=Sergio Dreoni, il primo imprenditore toscano a riconvertire la sua produzione per donare mascherine: "Onesto e appassionato"|first=Giacomo|last=Salvini|publisher=[[Il Fatto Quotidiano]]|access-date=17 May 2020|language=it|date=17 May 2020}}</ref>

Companies producing alcoholic beverages also underwent reconversion to produce alcohol-based hand sanitiser. In Piedmont this occurred in [[Canelli]] at the [[Ramazzotti (liqueur)|Ramazzotti]] factory (part of the [[Pernod Ricard]] group)<ref>{{cite news|url= https://torino.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/03/28/news/canelli_la_fabbrica_dell_amaro_ramazzotti_si_mette_a_produrre_igienizzanti_per_le_mani-252550031/?ref=RHPPBT-BH-I252189793-C12-P2-S3.4-T1|title= Canelli, la fabbrica dell'amaro Ramazzotti si mette a produrre l'igienizzante per le mani|language=it|first=Camilla|last=Capulli|access-date=28 March 2020|date=28 March 2020|work=[[La Stampa]]}}</ref> and in [[Chieri]] at the Martini plant.<ref>{{cite news|url= https://www.lastampa.it/topnews/edizioni-locali/torino/2020/03/27/news/coronavirus-la-fabbrica-dei-cocktail-ora-fa-i-disinfettanti-1.38644037|title= Coronavirus, la fabbrica dei cocktail ora fa i disinfettanti|language=it|first1=Gianni |last1=Giacomino |first2=Sarah |last2=Scaparone|access-date=28 March 2020|date=27 March 2020|work=[[La Stampa]]}}</ref>

Isinnova, a local engineering startup from Brescia, provided emergency solutions to local hospitals to compensate the shortages of spare parts for the machines. Firstly, they produced venturi valves for respirators using [[3D printer]]s,<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.forbes.com/sites/amyfeldman/2020/03/19/talking-with-the-italian-engineers-who-3d-printed-respirator-parts-for-hospitals-with-coronavirus-patients-for-free/ |language=it|work=[[Forbes]]|first=Amy |last=Feldman |date=19 March 2020|access-date=22 March 2020 |title=Meet The Italian Engineers 3D-Printing Respirator Parts For Free To Help Keep Coronavirus Patients Alive}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.giornaledibrescia.it/brescia-e-hinterland/le-valvole-per-la-rianimazione-scarseggiano-si-stampano-in-3d-1.3466921|title=Le valvole per la rianimazione scarseggiano: si stampano in 3D|language=it|publisher=[[Giornale di Brescia]]|date=14 March 2020|access-date=22 March 2020}}</ref> and later (in collaboration with [[Decathlon (retailer)|Decathlon]]) they adapted a snorkelling mask into a non-invasive ventilator.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.giornaledibrescia.it/brescia-e-hinterland/easy-covid-19-la-maschera-da-sub-si-trasforma-in-respiratore-1.3468476|title=Easy Covid 19, la maschera da sub si trasforma in respiratore|language=it|publisher=[[Giornale di Brescia]]|date=21 March 2020|access-date=22 March 2020}}</ref> Using 3D-printer technology as well, Elmec Informatica started to produce for the hospital of Busto Arsizio, sterilisable protective masks in [[thermoplastic polyurethanes]] that could adapt to [[Continuous positive airway pressure]] (CPAP) antiviral filters.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.ilgiorno.it/varese/cronaca/coronavirus-mascherine-3d-1.5083431|last=Formenti|first=Rosella|title=  Busto Arsizio, in ospedale mascherine con la stampante 3D|access-date=31 March 2020|date=27 March 2020|work=[[Il Giorno (newspaper)|Il Giorno]]}}</ref> The [[Istituto Poligrafico e Zecca dello Stato|Italian National Mint and Printing House]] used the plastic film applied to [[identity card]]s to produce face shields.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://video.repubblica.it/dossier/covid-19-i-grandi-marchi-rispondono/l-istituto-poligrafico-contro-il-coronavirus--con-la-plastica-delle-carte-di-identita-creiamo-visiere-sanitarie/358767/359323?ref=RHPPTP-BS-I253430426-C12-P9-S1.4-T1|title= L'Istituto Poligrafico contro il Coronavirus: ''Con la plastica delle carte di identità creiamo visiere sanitarie''|access-date=22 April 2020|date=22 April 2020|work=[[La Repubblica]]|first= Antonio|last= Nasso}}</ref>

====Cross-talks with the EU====
On 25 March, Italy, together with Belgium, France, Greece, Ireland, Luxembourg, Portugal, Slovenia, and Spain, sent a joint letter to the Council of the EU, calling for the issuing of a new common debt instrument, nicknamed in the media as "[[Eurobond (eurozone)|eurobond]]" or "corona bond", to help funding the measures taken against the coronavirus pandemic and the expected economic downturn to follow.<ref name=Dombey>{{cite news |last1=Dombey |first1=Daniel |last2=Chazan |first2=Guy |last3=Brundsen |first3=Jim |title=Nine eurozone countries issue call for 'coronabonds' |url=https://www.ft.com/content/258308f6-6e94-11ea-89df-41bea055720b |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=Financial Times |date=25 March 2020}}</ref> In subsequent conference calls between the leaders of the EU member states, the proposal saw the opposition of the Netherlands and Germany.<ref>{{cite news |title=Germans and Dutch set to block EU 'corona bonds' at video summit |url=https://www.euractiv.com/section/economy-jobs/news/germans-and-dutch-set-to-block-eu-corona-bonds-at-video-summit/ |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=euractiv.com |date=26 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Hornig |first1=Frank |last2=Mahler |first2=Armin |last3=Müller |first3=Peter |last4=Rainer |first4=Anton |last5=Reiermann |first5=Christian |title=Calls for Coronabonds Met with Familiar "Nein"  |url=https://www.spiegel.de/international/europe/calls-for-corona-bonds-met-with-familiar-nein-a-6eb0e5ce-fddd-4909-95bb-ae8421ef3d2e |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=Der Spiegel |date=27 March 2020 }}</ref>

On 9 April, after two meetings of the [[Eurogroup]], the ministers of Finances of the Eurozone countries agreed to €500 billion aid, including the possibility of using the [[European Stability Mechanism|ESM]], but without common debt instruments.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Smith-Meyer |first1=Bjarke |title=EU agrees on €500B of economic aid but no 'corona bonds' |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/corona-bonds-fade-in-midst-of-eurogroups-e500b-economic-strategy/ |accessdate=10 April 2020 |work=Politico |date=10 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Stevis-Gridneff |first1=Matina |title=E.U. Backs Half-Trillion Euro Stimulus, but Balks at Pooling Debt |url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/04/09/world/europe/coronavirus-european-union-bailout.html |accessdate=10 April 2020 |work=The New York Times |date=9 April 2020}}</ref>

===Society===
[[File:Italian flag coronavirus.jpg|thumb|right|upright=1.13|An [[Italian flag]] with the slogan "''Andrà tutto bene''" ("Everything will be all right")]]
Subsequent to the imposing of the national lockdown, there were protests in some Italian prisons, with fourteen deaths among Modena, Bologna and Foggia's penitentiary.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Gostoli |first1=Ylenia |title=Six inmates die as prison riots over coronavirus rules grip Italy |url=https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2020/03/inmates-die-prison-riots-coronavirus-rules-italy-200309125813658.html |accessdate=19 March 2020 |publisher=Al Jazeera |date=9 March 2020}}</ref>

With all of Italy ordered to remain indoors, Italians took to their balconies to sing together, play music, and applaud the country's health care providers.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://time.com/5802700/lockdown-song/|title=People Quarantined in Italy Join Together in Song From Balconies During Coronavirus Lockdown|last1=Locker|first1=Melissa|last2=Hoffman|first2=Ashley|date=15 March 2020|work=Time|accessdate=21 March 2020}}</ref> Some of the demonstrations were spontaneous, others were organised by social media and radio.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.cnn.com/2020/03/20/europe/italian-radio-national-anthem-intl-scli/index.html|title=Italians sing together as radio stations unite to broadcast the national anthem|last=Spary|first=Sara|date=20 March 2020|publisher=CNN|accessdate=21 March 2020}}</ref> On 13 March at 6&nbsp;pm, Italians throughout the country joined to sing the national anthem. At noon on 14 March, they stood on their balconies clapping to salute the nation's health care workers.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.nytimes.com/2020/03/14/world/europe/italians-find-a-moment-of-joy-in-this-moment-of-anxiety.html|title=Italians Find 'a Moment of Joy in This Moment of Anxiety': Under lockdown to prevent the spread of the coronavirus, the song breaks out from rooftops, balconies and windows.|last=Horowitz|first=Jason|date=14 March 2020|work=The New York Times|accessdate=21 March 2020}}</ref> A video of opera singer Maurizio Marchini performing the aria "[[Nessun dorma]]" from his balcony in Florence went viral.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.independent.co.uk/arts-entertainment/music/news/coronavirus-italy-tenor-nessun-dorma-video-maurizio-marchini-sing-balcony-florence-a9402761.html|title=Coronavirus: Italian tenor stuns quarantined neighbours with 'Nessun Dorma' performance from balcony|last=Stolworthy|first=Jacob|date=14 March 2020|work=The Independent|accessdate=21 March 2020}}</ref>

Some Italians have adapted the local custom of paying in advance at a cafe for a customer who can't afford it ("suspended coffee") by paying extra at grocery stores. Shops may double the amount and donate non-perishable foods to local aid groups like the [[Community of Sant'Egidio]].<ref>{{cite news |url=https://www.npr.org/sections/coronavirus-live-updates/2020/04/24/842891052/in-italy-suspended-shopping-helps-those-facing-economic-hardship-during-pandemic |title=In Italy, 'Suspended Shopping' Helps Those Facing Economic Hardship During Pandemic |date=24 April 2020 |work=NPR}}</ref>

Riots erupted on 23 October 2020 at night in Naples as people took to the street following the imposition of a curfew to reduce the spread of coronavirus. This came after Vincenzo De Luca, President of the Campania region, said that he was considering imposing a total lockdown, closing schools, businesses and leaving only essential services open, to prevent further spread of the virus. They were the first such demonstrations in Italy since the start of its coronavirus outbreak eight months ago.<ref>[https://www.mirror.co.uk/news/world-news/riots-erupt-naples-lockdown-protest-22898101]</ref>

===Education===
{{Main|Impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on education}}
After the first outbreak in Lombardy and Veneto, the regional governments of Emilia-Romagna, Friuli Venezia Giulia, Liguria, Lombardy, Piedmont, Trentino, and Veneto closed all schools and universities from 23 February to 1 March.<ref>{{cite news |title=Ufficiale: dopo Lombardia, Veneto, Trentino e Piemonte scuole chiuse anche in tutta l'Emilia-Romagna |url=https://www.open.online/2020/02/23/urgente-sala-scuole-chiuse-a-milano-e-provincia-da-domani/ |accessdate=24 March 2020 |work=Open |date=23 February 2020 |language=it-IT}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, Nord Italia "blindato": scuole chiuse in 7 regioni |url=http://www.today.it/attualita/scuole-chiuse-coronavirus-dove-quando.html |accessdate=24 March 2020 |work=Today |date=23 February 2020 |language=it}}</ref> The suspension was later extended, with the agreement of the national government, up to 8 March in Emilia-Romagna, Lombardy, and Veneto.<ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus, oltre mille contagiati. Scuole chiuse fino all'8 marzo in Veneto, Lombardia, Emilia Romagna |url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/29/news/le_scuole_ancora_otto_giorni_di_stop_in_lombardia_emilia_e_veneto-249848004/ |accessdate=24 March 2020 |work=la Repubblica |date=28 February 2020 |language=it}}</ref>

On 4 March, the government announced the closure of all schools and colleges until 15 March.<ref>{{Cite web|url=http://www.thetelegram.com/news/world/coronavirus-deprives-nearly-300-million-students-of-their-schooling-unesco-419714/|title=Coronavirus deprives nearly 300 million students of their schooling: UNESCO {{!}} The Telegram|last=Inc|first=Reuters|website=thetelegram.com|access-date=15 March 2020}}</ref>

With the enactment of the lockdown of Lombardy and 14 more northern provinces on 8 March, the re-opening of schools in these areas was delayed to 3 April.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Tondo |first1=Lorenzo |title=Italy set to quarantine whole of Lombardy due to coronavirus |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/mar/07/italy-set-to |accessdate=24 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=7 March 2020 }}</ref> On 9 March, the government extended the lockdown to the national territory, closing all schools and universities until 3 April.<ref>{{cite news |title=Italian premier locks down entire country to stop virus |url=https://apnews.com/3ff579e06d07428f0bc993c0a98c001d |accessdate=24 March 2020 |work=AP NEWS |date=9 March 2020}}</ref>

Schools eventually stayed closed until the end of the academic year. Their safe reopening was organized by the Ministry of Education together with the Ministry of Health, and was scheduled on 14 September 2020. However some regional governments opted for delaying the reopening.<ref>{{cite news |title=Ricomincia la scuola, non tutta |url=https://www.ilpost.it/2020/09/13/scuola-ricominciano-lezioni/ |accessdate=14 September 2020 |work=Il Post |date=13 September 2020 |language=it-IT}}</ref>

===Religion===
{{Main|Impact of the COVID-19 pandemic on religion#Christianity}}
In Italy, in-person gatherings for religious worship have been suspended and as a result, many churches broadcast Mass via online live-stream, radio and television.<ref>{{cite web |title=In Italy and beyond, churches grapple with coronavirus |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/coronavirus-church-online-live-stream-congregation/ |work=Politico |accessdate=30 March 2020  |date=17 March 2020}}</ref>

Church funerals cannot be held given the national lockdown.<ref name="Scalzo2020"/> In some northern cities, authorities have had issues in dealing with the storage of the high number of coffins, and churches have offered to care for them.<ref name="Scalzo2020">{{cite news |last1=Scalzo |first1=Flavio Lo |title=Italy small town priest deals with death on industrial scale |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-italy-coffins/italy-small-town-priest-deals-with-death-on-industrial-scale-idUSKBN21F0M6 |agency=[[Reuters]] |accessdate=30 March 2020  |date=29 March 2020}}</ref> In the towns of Seriate and Bergamo, the Italian Army has volunteered to transport some of these coffins from churches and morgues to cemeteries and crematoriums in other provinces.<ref name="Scalzo2020"/><ref>{{cite news |title=Army takes Bergamo coffins away – English |url=https://www.ansa.it/english/news/general_news/2020/03/19/army-takes-bergamo-coffins-away_a6e09e12-ba62-4dc9-834b-c227c6bd1fa3.html |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=ANSA.it |date=19 March 2020 }}</ref>

===Politics===
[[File:Mattarella 25 Aprile 2020.jpg|thumb|right|250px|President [[Sergio Mattarella]] at the [[Victor Emmanuel II Monument|Altar of the Fatherland]] during the [[Liberation Day (Italy)|Liberation Day]], wearing a face mask]]
On 5 March, the Italian government decided to postpone the [[2020 Italian constitutional referendum|constitutional referendum]] that was due on 29 March. The referendum has been delayed until further notice.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Dallison |first1=Paul |title=Italy postpones referendum due to coronavirus |url=https://www.politico.eu/article/italy-postpones-referendum-due-to-coronavirus/ |accessdate=22 March 2020 |work=Politico |date=5 March 2020}}</ref>

According to a few surveys, many Italians feel betrayed by the European Union's response to the crisis. This has led to an increase in [[euroscepticism]], with the number of Italians agreeing that EU membership is a disadvantage jumping from 47% in November 2018 to 67% in March 2020, according to a ''Tecnè'' survey. Former president of the European Commission [[Donald Tusk]] said that the risk for the European Union is greater than the [[European debt crisis]] of 2009, and that despite the fact that EU aid to Italy is greater than from other countries, its perception is crucial.<ref name=FT6April>{{cite news |last1=Johnson |first1=Miles |last2=Fleming |first2=Sam |last3=Chazan |first3=Guy |title=Coronavirus: Is Europe losing Italy? |url=https://www.ft.com/content/f21cf708-759e-11ea-ad98-044200cb277f |accessdate=6 April 2020 |work=[[Financial Times]] |date=6 April 2020}}</ref>

Top Italian figures have condemned an article in a German newspaper suggesting the mafia was waiting for an influx of European Union cash amid the coronavirus outbreak. Foreign Minister [[Luigi Di Maio]] said, “[[Die Welt]], an important German newspaper, urged Europe this morning to not help Italy because ‘the mafia is waiting for money from Brussels’”.<ref>{{Cite web|url=https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/coronavirus-eu-money-die-welt-italy-countries-europecoronavirus-eu-money-die-welt-italy-countries-a9458641.html|title=Italy demands apology after German paper said 'mafia waiting for EU coronavirus money'|date=9 April 2020|website=The Independent}}</ref>

===Sport===
On 13 October 2020, it was announced that [[Juventus F.C.|Juventus]] forward [[Cristiano Ronaldo]] has tested positive for COVID-19.<ref>{{cite news |title=Cristiano Ronaldo positivo al Covid: asintomatico, è in isolamento |url=https://www.ilgiornale.it/news/sport/cristiano-ronaldo-positivo-coronavirus-1896263.html |accessdate=13 October 2020 |agency=ilgiornale.it |publisher=ilgiornale.it |date=13 October 2020}}</ref>
Many Serie A football players have tested positive for the COVID-19 and some matches played in stadiums without a public have been postponed.<ref>{{cite news |title=CR7 e l'allarme virus: la Serie A vada avanti anche nella lotta alla pandemia |url=https://www.gazzetta.it/Calcio/Serie-A/13-10-2020/allarme-covid-serie-avanti-anche-lotta-pandemia-3802790840602_preview.shtml |accessdate=13 October 2020 |agency=gazzetta.it |publisher=gazzetta.it |date=13 October 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Genoa, altri 3 positivi: Brlek, Zajc e un membro dello staff. Il totale è 19 |url=https://www.gazzetta.it/Calcio/Serie-A/Genoa/02-10-2020/genoa-positivi-esito-nuovi-tamponi-3802460323739.shtml |accessdate=13 October 2020 |agency=gazzetta.it |publisher=gazzetta.it |date=2 October 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=l Consiglio straordinario di Lega ha deciso: rinviata Genoa-Torino |url=https://www.gazzetta.it/Calcio/Serie-A/01-10-2020/consiglio-straordinario-lega-si-decide-genoa-torino-3802435102121.shtml |accessdate=13 October 2020 |agency=gazzetta.it |publisher=gazzetta.it |date=1 October 2020}}</ref>

Even at the [[2020 Giro d'Italia|Giro d'italia 2020]] some cyclists were found to be positive at COVID-19 and some withdrew from the race.<ref>{{cite news |title=Giro, positivi Kruijswijk, Matthews e sei membri staff. Si ritirano le squadre Jumbo e Mitchelton |url=https://www.gazzetta.it/Giroditalia/13-10-2020/giro-positivi-due-corridori-sei-membri-squadre-3802773675490.shtml |accessdate=13 October 2020 |agency=gazzetta.it |publisher=gazzetta.it |date=13 October 2020}}</ref>

On 15 October 2020, motorcycle racer [[Valentino Rossi]] confirmed that he was positive for COVID-19.<ref>{{cite news |title=Covid: Valentino Rossi positivo, niente Aragon |url=https://www.ansa.it/sito/notizie/topnews/2020/10/15/covid-valentino-rossi-positivo-niente-aragon_b27f7212-9bca-4e01-b5af-243451d53c2d.html |accessdate=15 October 2020 |agency=ansa.it |publisher=ansa.it |date=15 October 2020}}</ref> 
On the same day, swimmer [[Federica Pellegrini]] confirmed that she was positive at COVID-19.<ref>{{cite news |title=Federica Pellegrini annuncia in lacrime: "Fatto il tampone, sono positiva al Covid" |url=https://www.sportmediaset.mediaset.it/altrisport/nuoto/federica-pellegrini-annunciain-lacrime-sono-positiva-al-covid_24256019-202002a.shtml |accessdate=15 October 2020 |agency=tgcom24 |publisher=tgcom24 |date=15 October 2020}}</ref>

==Statistics==
===Data quality issues===
Deaths statistics for Italy include coronavirus victims who died in hospital, as well as those who died outside of hospitals and were tested before or after dying. Post-mortem tests are routinely carried out, and there is no distinction between people who died "with" or "of" coronavirus, including patients with pre-existing conditions,<ref name="Europa Today">{{cite news |title=Ecco come si calcolano i decessi collegati al coronavirus nei diversi Paesi Ue |url=https://europa.today.it/attualita/coronavirus-contati-decessi-ue.html |publisher=Europa Today |date=30 March 2020}}</ref> which make up 96% of the total death count.<ref>{{cite web |title=Caratteristiche dei pazienti deceduti positivi all'infezione da SARS-CoV-2 in Italia |url=https://www.epicentro.iss.it/coronavirus/sars-cov-2-decessi-italia |website=Istituto Superiore di Sanità}}</ref> However, in regions where the healthcare system has been overwhelmed by the pandemic (e.g. Lombardy), official death statistics likely missed a portion of deaths outside hospitals.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Stancati |first1=Margherita |last2=Sylvers |first2=Eric |title=Italy's Coronavirus Death Toll Is Far Higher Than Reported |url=https://www.wsj.com/articles/italys-coronavirus-death-toll-is-far-higher-than-reported-11585767179 |accessdate=2 April 2020 |work=The Wall Street Journal |date=1 April 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Tracking covid-19 excess deaths across countries |url=https://www.economist.com/graphic-detail/2020/04/16/tracking-covid-19-excess-deaths-across-countries |work=The Economist}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Italy's coronavirus deaths could be underestimated in data: official |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-italy-data/italys-coronavirus-deaths-could-be-underestimated-in-data-official-idUSKBN21I250 |accessdate=28 April 2020 |work=Reuters |date=31 March 2020 |language=en}}</ref> In some areas of northern Italy, a comparison of the average registered deaths over the previous years with the deaths in the first months of 2020 showed a sizeable excess of deaths that were not officially included in the coronavirus toll.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Cancelli |first1=Claudio |last2=Foresti |first2=Luca |title=The real death toll for Covid-19 is at least 4 times the official numbers |url=https://www.corriere.it/politica/20_marzo_26/the-real-death-toll-for-covid-19-is-at-least-4-times-the-official-numbers-b5af0edc-6eeb-11ea-925b-a0c3cdbe1130.shtml |accessdate=28 April 2020 |work=Corriere della Sera |date=26 March 2020 |language=it}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Giugliano |first1=Ferdinando |title=We May Be Underestimating the Coronavirus Death Toll |url=https://www.bloomberg.com/opinion/articles/2020-04-01/coronavirus-italy-shows-we-may-be-underestimating-death-toll |accessdate=28 April 2020 |work=Bloomberg |date=1 April 2020}}</ref> In the month of March, 10,900 excess deaths have been estimated, that have not been reported as COVID-19 deaths.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Wu |first1=Jin |last2=McCann |first2=Allison |last3=Katz |first3=Josh |last4=Peltier |first4=Elian |title=71,000 Missing Deaths: Tracking the True Toll of the Coronavirus Outbreak |url=https://www.nytimes.com/interactive/2020/04/21/world/coronavirus-missing-deaths.html |accessdate=13 May 2020 |work=The New York Times}}</ref>

Not all European countries count coronavirus-related deaths with the same criteria. For instance, in some other European countries, a distinction is made between deaths caused by coronavirus and deaths of people infected with coronavirus, thus often excluding deaths of people with pre-existing conditions.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Caccia |first1=Fabrizio |title=Coronavirus, "il conteggio dei morti varia da paese a paese. La Germania esclude chi ha altre patologie" |url=https://www.corriere.it/cronache/20_marzo_22/coronavirus-il-conteggio-morti-varia-paese-paese-germania-esclude-chi-ha-altre-patologie-6a452e6a-6c19-11ea-8403-94d97cb6fb9f_preview.shtml?reason=unauthenticated&cat=1&cid=-iA_4dqs&pids=FR&credits=1&origin=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.corriere.it%2Fcronache%2F20_marzo_22%2Fcoronavirus-il-conteggio-morti-varia-paese-paese-germania-esclude-chi-ha-altre-patologie-6a452e6a-6c19-11ea-8403-94d97cb6fb9f.shtml |publisher=Corriere della Sera |date=22 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Arija Garcia |first1=Carlos |title=Morti da coronavirus: i conti non tornano |url=https://www.laleggepertutti.it/381401_morti-da-coronavirus-i-conti-non-tornano |publisher=La Legge per Tutti |date=26 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Burba |first1=Elisabetta |title=Coronavirus: ma come vengono conteggiati i morti in Europa? |url=https://www.panorama.it/news/cronaca/covid-conteggio-morti-europa |publisher=Panorama |date=20 April 2020}}</ref> In addition to this, some countries only report deaths in hospitals.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Giles |first1=Chris |title=Deaths from coronavirus far higher in England than first reported |url=https://www.ft.com/content/c07e267b-7bca-418f-ad9e-8631a29854cb |newspaper=Financial Times |date=7 April 2020}}</ref><ref name="Europa Today"/><ref>{{cite news |last1=Sevillano |first1=Elena G. |title=Tracking the coronavirus: why does each country count deaths differently? |url=https://english.elpais.com/society/2020-03-30/tracking-the-coronavirus-why-does-each-country-count-deaths-differently.html |publisher=El País |date=30 March 2020}}</ref>

== Foreign cases linked to Italy ==
{{Undue weight|date=March 2020|to=an aspect of the topic (individuals spreading the disease through travel), and consists only of links to [[primary sources]] without providing the necessary [[secondary sources]] that analyse the aspect}}

[[File:Countries and territories with COVID-19 cases linked directly to Italian cluster.svg|thumb|upright=1.36|right|Countries and territories with [[COVID-19]] cases linked directly to the Italian cluster]]
A number of COVID-19 cases have emerged worldwide that are linked to Italy, and especially to the northern regions.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Beaumont |first1=Peter |title=Europe's epidemic: how coronavirus radiated out from Italy |url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/feb/28/an-epidemic-is-coming-europe-struggles-to-contain-coronavirus |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=The Guardian |date=28 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |last1=Rome |first1=Eric Sylvers in Milan and Giovanni Legorano in |title=Coronavirus Spreads Outside of Italy, Prompting Fresh Restrictions |url=https://www.wsj.com/articles/coronavirus-spreads-outside-of-italy-prompting-fresh-restrictions-11582714949 |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=The Wall Street Journal |date=26 February 2020 |quote=Italy's coronavirus outbreak has crossed the Alps and is being linked to a growing number of infections around Europe}}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Coronavirus spreads in Europe from Italy, first case in Latin America |url=https://www.rnz.co.nz/news/world/410449/coronavirus-spreads-in-europe-from-italy-first-case-in-latin-america |accessdate=30 March 2020 |work=RNZ |date=26 February 2020 }}</ref><ref>{{cite news |title=Europe's coronavirus outbreak spreads from Italy |url=https://www.bbc.com/news/world-europe-51638095 |accessdate=31 March 2020 |work=BBC News |date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite journal |last1=Day |first1=Michael |title=Covid-19: Italy confirms 11 deaths as cases spread from north |journal=BMJ |date=26 February 2020 |volume=368 |pages=m757 |doi=10.1136/bmj.m757 |pmid=32102793 |s2cid=211535770 |url=https://www.bmj.com/content/368/bmj.m757 |accessdate=30 March 2020 |quote=Confirmed cases of COVID-19 in Italy leapt by 45% to reach 322 on 25 February and four more deaths were confirmed amid signs that the infection was spreading around the country and across borders. ...  Authorities in Austria and Croatia also reported their first cases of COVID-19 and said that the patients affected had recently travelled from Italy's Lombardy region, confirming fears that travellers were starting to carry the infection from its European epicentre. An Italian couple from the north of Italy tested positive on the Spanish island of Tenerife, forcing the quarantine of their hotel.}}</ref>

===Africa===
'''Algeria''' –
On 25 February 2020, Algeria confirmed its first case, an Italian man from [[Bertonico]], Lombardy who arrived in the country on 17 February.<ref name=":2" /><ref>{{cite web|url=https://news.trust.org/item/20200225190135-gnit5/|title=Algeria confirms first case of coronavirus – state TV|last=Foundation|first=Thomson Reuters|website=news.trust.org|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://africatimes.com/2020/02/25/algerian-health-minister-confirms-first-covid-19-case/|title=Algerian health minister confirms first COVID-19 case {{!}} Africa Times|date=25 February 2020|website=africatimes.com|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref>

'''Central African Republic''' –
On 14 March, the Central African minister of health announced the first confirmed case in the country, a 74-year-old Italian citizen coming from Milan.<ref>{{cite news |title=RCA: Un premier cas confirmé de Coronavirus à Bangui – Radio Ndeke Luka |url=https://www.radiondekeluka.org/actualites/sante/35266-rca-un-premier-cas-confirme-de-coronavirus-en-centrafrique.html |accessdate=15 March 2020 |work=radiondekeluka.org |language=fr-fr |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200320191045/https://www.radiondekeluka.org/actualites/sante/35266-rca-un-premier-cas-confirme-de-coronavirus-en-centrafrique.html |archive-date=20 March 2020 |url-status=dead }}</ref>

'''Côte d'Ivoire''' –
On Tuesday, 10 March, Côte d'Ivoire confirmed its first case, a 45-year-old Ivorien male who had sojourned in Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.africanews.com/2020/03/11/ivory-coast-records-first-coronavirus-case/|title=Ivory Coast confirms first coronavirus case|website=Africanews|date=11 March 2020|accessdate=12 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Morocco''' –
On 2 March, the Moroccan Ministry of Health reported its first case, a man who had lived in Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Morocco reports first coronavirus case: health ministry |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-morocco/morocco-reports-first-coronavirus-case-health-ministry-idUSKBN20P33T |accessdate=3 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=2 March 2020 }}</ref>

'''Nigeria''' –
On 28 February 2020, Nigeria confirmed its first case, an Italian man who tested positive after arriving from Milan on 25 February and falling ill the next day.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.pmnewsnigeria.com/2020/02/28/breaking-deadly-coronavirus-confirmed-in-lagos-nigeria-at-last/|title=Breaking: Deadly Coronavirus confirmed in Lagos Nigeria at last|date=28 February 2020|website=P.M. '''Senegal''' –
[[COVID-19 pandemic in Senegal|Senegal]] confirmed on 12 March that their fifth confirmed case was a Senegalese national who returned from Italy on 6 March.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.aa.com.tr/en/africa/senegal-confirms-fifth-case-of-covid-19/1762907|title=Senegal confirms the fifth case of COVID-19|website=aa.com.tr|accessdate=13 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Seychelles''' –

Both were people who were in contact with someone in Italy who tested positive.<ref>{{cite news |last1=Bonnelame |first1=Betyme |title=2 Seychellois test positive for COVID-19 as globe-sweeping virus reaches island nation|url=http://www.seychellesnewsagency.com/articles/12593/+Seychellois+test+positive+for+COVID-+as+globe-sweeping+virus+reaches+island+nation |accessdate=14 March 2020 |agency=[[Seychelles News Agency]] |date=14 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Tunisia''' –

===Americas===
'''Argentina''' –
On 3 March, Argentina confirmed its first case, a 43-year-old man who arrived in Argentina two days earlier after a trip that included northern Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Argentine health minister confirms country's first case of coronavirus |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-argentina/argentine-health-minister-confirms-countrys-first-case-of-coronavirus-idUSKBN20Q2SC |accessdate=4 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=3 March 2020 }}</ref>

'''Bolivia''' –
Two people who returned from Italy to Bolivia were tested positive.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://eldeber.com.bo/169041_confirman-dos-casos-de-coronavirus-en-bolivia|title=Confirman dos casos de coronavirus en Bolivia |publisher = El Deber|website=eldeber.com.bo|accessdate=11 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Brazil''' –
On 25 February, Brazil confirmed its first case, a 61-year-old man from [[São Paulo]] who travelled to Lombardy between 9 and 21 February. He showed mild symptoms and was quarantined at home.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://g1.globo.com/sp/sao-paulo/noticia/2020/02/25/ministerio-da-saude-investiga-possivel-paciente-com-coronavirus-em-sp-caso-foi-para-contraprova.ghtml|title=Ministério da Saúde investiga possível paciente com coronavírus em SP; caso foi para contraprova|website=G1|language=pt-br|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

'''Canada''' –
