'''Chile''' –
On 5 March, Chile confirmed its third case, a 56-year-old man who travelled across Europe and visited Northern Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=COVID-19: Chile confirms 3rd case of coronavirus |url=https://santiagotimes.cl/2020/03/05/covid-19-chile-confirms-3rd-case-of-coronavirus/ |accessdate=5 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=5 March 2020 |archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200306155150/https://santiagotimes.cl/2020/03/05/covid-19-chile-confirms-3rd-case-of-coronavirus/ |archive-date=6 March 2020 |url-status=dead }}</ref>

'''Bangladesh''' –

'''India''' –
On 2 March, New Delhi confirmed its first case, an Indian national who had returned from Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.indiatoday.in/india/story/coronavirus-india-outbreak-fresh-case-news-update-delhi-telangana-1651586-2020-03-02|title=Two fresh cases of coronavirus detected in India; one in Delhi, another in Telangana|website=India Today|date=2 March 2020|access-date=2 March 2020}}</ref> On the same day, an Italian tourist who had arrived in [[Jaipur]], Rajasthan on 29 February tested positive in a second test after having previously tested negative.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://timesofindia.indiatimes.com/india/coronavirus-live-updates-south-korea-reports-476-new-cases-total-at-4212/liveblog/74432985.cms|title=Coronavirus India Live Updates: Italian tests positive for coronavirus in Jaipur|website=The Times of India|access-date=2 March 2020}}</ref> On 3 March, his wife also tested positive.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.businesstoday.in/current/economy-politics/coronavirus-outbreak-case-live-updates-latest-news-covid-19-delhi-noida-agra-india/story/397426.html|title=Coronavirus Live Updates: Italian tourist's wife tests positive, number of cases rises to 7|website=Business Today|date=3 March 2020|access-date=3 March 2020}}</ref>
On 4 March 14 more Italian tourists who were kept at a quarantine facility in Delhi were confirmed positive, as well as the group's Indian driver.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/politics-and-nation/28-confirmed-cases-of-coronavirus-in-india-gom-to-meet-today-health-minister-harsh-vardhan/articleshow/74472369.cms|title=28 confirmed cases of coronavirus in India, GoM to meet today: Health minister Harsh Vardhan|date=4 March 2020|work=The Economic Times|access-date=4 March 2020}}</ref> A [[Paytm]] employee in [[Gurgaon]] who had returned from a vacation in Italy also tested positive.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.indiatoday.in/india/story/coronavirus-covid19-paytm-employee-tests-positive-gurugram-1652475-2020-03-04|title=29th coronavirus case in India: After 15 Italian tourists, Paytm employee tests positive for Covid-19|last1=DelhiMarch 4|first1=Aishwarya Paliwal New|last2=March 5|first2=2020 Updated|website=India Today|access-date=8 March 2020|last3=Ist|first3=2020 13:52}}</ref> On 8 March, five members of a family in [[Kerala]] tested positive, three of whom had returned from Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ndtv.com/india-news/5-of-family-infected-with-coronavirus-in-kerala-total-positive-cases-in-india-rise-to-39-2191757|title=5 Of Family in Kerala Get Coronavirus, 39 Cases in India: 10 Points|website=NDTV.com|access-date=8 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Israel''' –

On 28 February 2020, Iceland confirmed its first case, an Icelandic male in his 50s who had previously been to Northern Italy and was placed in strict [[Isolation (health care)|isolation]] in [[Landspítali]] in [[Reykjavík]].<ref name="ruv.is">{{cite web|url=https://www.ruv.is/frett/fyrsta-tilfelli-covid-19-greint-a-islandi|title=Fyrsta tilfelli COVID-19 greint á Íslandi|date=28 February 2020|website=RÚV}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://bnonews.com/index.php/2020/02/the-latest-coronavirus-cases/|title=Tracking coronavirus: Map, data and timeline|first=B. N. O.|last=News|date=18 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.mbl.is/frettir/innlent/2020/02/28/fyrsta_tilfelli_koronuveiru_greinist_a_islandi/|title=Fyrsta tilfelli kórónuveiru greinist á Íslandi|website=mbl.is|language=is|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>
On 5 March, a total of 34 cases had been confirmed in Iceland, most of which are imported cases from Italy.{{citation needed|date=June 2020}}

'''Ireland''' –
On 27 February 2020, Ireland's first case was confirmed by the [[Health Protection Surveillance Centre]]. The male patient had travelled to an affected region in Northern Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.rte.ie/news/coronavirus/2020/0229/1119357-coronavirus-ireland/ |title=First case of Covid-19 diagnosed in east of Ireland |date=1 March 2020 |access-date=4 March 2020 |publisher=Raidió Teilifís Éireann }}</ref> A second, unrelated case was confirmed on 3 March, a female in the eastern portion of Ireland who had travelled to Italy.<ref>{{cite web|first1=Paul|last1=Cullen|accessdate=3 March 2020|title=Second case of coronavirus is confirmed in east of Ireland|url=https://www.irishtimes.com/news/health/second-case-of-coronavirus-is-confirmed-in-east-of-ireland-1.4191961|website=The Irish Times}}</ref>

'''Latvia''' –
On 2 March, Latvia confirmed its first case, a person who had travelled from Milan to Munich and then to [[Riga]] on 29 February.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://eng.lsm.lv/article/society/health/first-case-of-covid-19-coronavirus-confirmed-in-latvia.a350338/|title=First case of COVID-19 coronavirus confirmed in Latvia|website=lsm.lv|access-date=3 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Lithuania''' –
On 28 February, Lithuania confirmed its first case, a 39-year-old woman who arrived in [[Kaunas]] from [[Verona]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.15min.lt/naujiena/aktualu/lietuva/koronavirusas-pasieke-lietuva-uzfiksuotas-pirmasis-atvejis-56-1282110|title=Lietuvoje patvirtintas pirmasis koronaviruso atvejis – susirgo 39 metų moteris, atskridusi į Kauną|website=15min.lt|language=lt|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

'''Luxembourg''' –
The nation's second and fourth cases were persons who had travelled to Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://5minutes.rtl.lu/actu/luxembourg/a/1479054.html|title=RTL 5minutes – Il revenait d'Italie: Un deuxième cas de coronavirus confirmé au Luxembourg|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://5minutes.rtl.lu/actu/luxembourg/a/1479918.html|title=Santé: Un 4e cas de coronavirus validé au Luxembourg|website=5minutes.rtl.lu|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Malta''' –
A 12-year-old Italian brought the infection to Malta.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.channelnewsasia.com/news/world/covid19-malta-first-coronavirus-case-italian-girl-12512852|title=Italian girl becomes Malta's first coronavirus case|website=CNA|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Moldova''' –
On 7 March, Moldova confirmed its first case, a 48-year-old woman who had returned from Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://deschide.md/ro/stiri/social/62248/BREAKING-NEWS-Primul-caz-de-coronavirus-depistat-%C3%AEn-Republica-Moldova-O-femeie-de-48-de-ani-infectat%C4%83.htm|title=Breaking News// Primul caz de coronavirus depistat în Republica Moldova. O femeie de 48 de ani, infectată|trans-title=Breaking News// First coronavirus case detected in Republic of Moldova. A 48-year-old woman, infected|language=ro|website=Deschide.md|date=7 March 2020|access-date=7 March 2020}}</ref> Moldova confirmed the existence of imported case from diseased Italy on 11 March.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://stiri.md/article/incidente/al-patrulea-caz-de-coronavirus-confirmat-in-r-moldova|title=Al patrulea caz de coronavirus, confirmat în R. Moldova|website=stiri.md|accessdate=13 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Netherlands''' –
On 27 February, the Netherlands confirmed its first case, a man who had been in Lombardy and was admitted to Elisabeth-TweeSteden Hospital in [[Tilburg]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.rivm.nl/nieuws/patient-met-nieuw-coronavirus-in-nederland|title=Patiënt met nieuw coronavirus in Nederland {{!}} RIVM|website=www.rivm.nl|access-date=1 March 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.telegraaf.nl/nieuws/214089776/rivm-eerste-coronageval-in-nederland|title=RIVM: eerste coronageval in Nederland|date=27 February 2020|website=De Telegraaf|language=nl|access-date=1 March 2020}}</ref>
On 28 February, a woman from [[Amsterdam]] who had visited Lombardy was in home isolation in [[Diemen]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.rivm.nl/nieuws/tweede-patient-in-nederland-met-covid-19|title=Tweede patiënt in Nederland met COVID-19 {{!}} RIVM|website=www.rivm.nl|access-date=1 March 2020}}</ref>

'''[[North Macedonia]]''' –
On 26 February, North Macedonia confirmed its first case, a woman who tested positive at the Clinic for Infectious Diseases, [[Skopje]]. She had stayed in Italy for a month and had been sick for two weeks. Upon returning to North Macedonia, she immediately reported to the clinic.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://vesti.mk/read/article/https%3A%2F%2Freporter.mk%2Fgjuture%2Fpotvrden-prv-sluchaj-od-koronavirus-vo-makedonija%2F|title=Потврден прв случај од коронавирус во Македонија |trans-title=First confirmed case of coronavirus in Macedonia |date=n.d.|language=mk}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://a1on.mk/macedonia/prv-sluchaj-na-zabolen-od-koronavirus-vo-makedonija/|title=Прв случај на заболен од коронавирус во Македонија|date=26 February 2020|website=А1он|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>

'''Norway''' –
On 27 February, Norway confirmed that two people who tested positive were linked to the outbreak in Italy. They were quarantined at home in [[Oslo]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.fhi.no/nyheter/2020/tre-nye-personer-har-testet-positivt-pa-koronavirus/|title=Tre nye personer har testet positivt på koronavirus|website=Folkehelseinstituttet|language=no|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref>
On 28 February, an individual from Bergen and an employee of [[Oslo University Hospital, Ullevål]] tested positive and were placed in home isolation. Both had visited Northern Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.nrk.no/vestland/over-hundre-kan-ha-hatt-kontakt-med-koronasmittet-ulleval-ansatt-1.14922358|title=Over hundre kan ha hatt kontakt med koronasmittet Ullevål-ansatt|last=Olsson|first=Svein Vestrum|date=28 February 2020|publisher=NRK|language=nb-NO|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.fhi.no/nyheter/2020/ytterligere-to-personer-har-testet-positivt-pa-koronavirus/|title=Ytterligere to personer har testet positivt på koronavirus|website=Folkehelseinstituttet|language=no|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>
On 6 March, the Norwegian Institute of Public Health reported that 79 of the 113 confirmed cases in Norway were linked to the outbreak in northern Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.fhi.no/en/news/2020/status-coronavirus-friday-6.-mars-2020/|title=Status coronavirus Friday 6. mars 2020|website=Folkehelseinstituttet|date=6 March 2020|access-date=7 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Poland''' –
Of the country's first five cases, two were from Italy, two were from Germany and one was from the UK.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://polandin.com/47007012/four-new-coronavirus-cases-confirmed-in-poland|title=Four new coronavirus cases confirmed in Poland|first=Telewizja Polska|last=S.A|website=polandin.com|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Portugal''' –
On 2 March, a doctor who had travelled to Northern Italy and became ill on 29 February was confirmed positive at Hospital de São João in [[Porto]]. On 4 March, a 44-year-old man who had travelled to Italy was confirmed positive at the same hospital.{{citation needed|date=June 2020}}

'''Romania''' –
On 26 February, Romania confirmed its first case, a man from [[Gorj County|Gorj]] who tested positive after having come in contact with a 71-year-old man from [[Cattolica]], Italy. The Italian man visited his wife's family and had several business meetings in Romania from 18 to 22 February. The Romanian man was admitted to National Institute of Infectious Diseases Prof. Dr. Matei Balș in [[Bucharest]].<ref name=":5" /><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.hotnews.ro/stiri-sanatate-23687251-primul-caz-infectie-coronavirus-confirmat-oficial-romania.htm|title=Ultima Orǎ Livevideotext Primul caz de infecție cu coronavirus, confirmat oficial în România: Un bărbat din Gorj care a intrat în contact cu italianul care a vizitat recent țara noastră – Sanatate – HotNews.ro|date=26 February 2020|website=hotnews.ro|language=ro|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>
On 28 February, a 45-year-old man from [[Maramureș]] who had returned from Italy on 25 February was admitted to the Clinic of Infectious Diseases and then transferred to [[Cluj County|Cluj]].<ref name=":9">{{cite web|url=https://www.digi24.ro/stiri/actualitate/doua-noi-posibile-cazuri-de-coronavirus-in-romania-1267704|title=Două noi cazuri de coronavirus confirmate în România|website=digi24.ro|language=ro|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref> A 38-year-old woman who had returned from Bergamo tested positive was admitted to a hospital in [[Timișoara]].<ref name=":9" />
On 3 March, a 47-year-old man who had travelled in the same plane with the 38-year-old woman was confirmed positive and admitted to the same hospital.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.digi24.ro/stiri/actualitate/al-patrulea-caz-de-coronavirus-confirmat-in-romania-1269577|title=Al patrulea caz de coronavirus a fost confirmat în România|trans-title=Fourth coronavirus case was confirmed in Romania|language=ro|website=Digi24|date=3 March 2020|access-date=3 March 2020}}</ref>
The majority of confirmed cases in Romania are related to Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.digi24.ro/stiri/actualitate/informatii-oficiale-despre-coronavirus-ministerul-de-interne-26-de-persoane-sunt-in-carantina-2077-sunt-monitorizate-la-domiciliu-1266261|title=Coronavirus România, Informații Oficiale: 36 de persoane au fost infectate. '''Russia''' –
On 2 March, a Russian citizen who had returned from Italy was diagnosed.<ref>{{cite news |title=Russian citizen who returned from Italy diagnosed with coronavirus: RIA cites ministry |url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-health-coronavirus-russia/russian-citizen-who-returned-from-italy-diagnosed-with-coronavirus-ria-cites-ministry-idUSKBN20P1JH |accessdate=4 March 2020 |agency=Reuters |date=2 March 2020 }}</ref>

'''San Marino''' –

'''Serbia''' –

At least one other case had been to Italy.<ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/serbian/lat/srbija-51831539|title=Korona virus: Potvrđeno šest novih slučajeva u Srbiji|newspaper=BBC News Na Srpskom|date=11 March 2020|accessdate=12 March 2020|via=bbc.com}}</ref>

'''Slovakia''' –
An asymptomatic man who had travelled to Venice between 14 and 15 February transmitted the virus to his father and his wife.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://spectator.sme.sk/c/22352401/three-coronavirus-cases-in-slovakia.html|title=Three coronavirus cases confirmed in Slovakia|first=Petit Press|last=a.s|date=7 March 2020|website=spectator.sme.sk|accessdate=8 March 2020}}</ref>

'''Slovenia''' –
Many Slovenian cases are linked to Italy, including the nation's first case.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.24ur.com/novice/slovenija/epidemiologi-iscejo-vse-s-katerimi-je-imel-okuzeni-slovenec-stike.html|title=Okužbo s koronavirusom potrdili že pri šestih osebah, ne gre samo za motoriste iz Maroka|website=24ur.com|accessdate=8 March 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200309190342/https://www.24ur.com/novice/slovenija/epidemiologi-iscejo-vse-s-katerimi-je-imel-okuzeni-slovenec-stike.html|archive-date=9 March 2020|url-status=dead}}</ref>

'''Spain''' –
On 24 February, a 69-year-old medical doctor from Lombardy who had been vacationing in [[Tenerife]] since 17 February tested positive at the [[Hospital Universitario Nuestra Señora de Candelaria|University Hospital of the Nuestra Señora de Candelaria]]. A 25-year-old man returning from a holiday in Italy also tested positive in [[Asturias]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/cronaca/2020/02/24/news/coronavirus_italiano_positivo_al_test_a_tenerife_e_il_terzo_caso_di_contagio_in_spagna-249508945/|title=Turista italiano positivo al test a Tenerife. Primo caso sospetto nelle Asturie: è un giovane di ritorno dall'Italia|date=24 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=24 February 2020}}</ref><ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Tenerife">{{cite web|url=https://www.repubblica.it/esteri/2020/02/25/news/coronavirus_contagiati_in_italia-249569108/|title=Coronavirus, positivi due italiani a Tenerife. Mille persone nell'hotel in quarantena|date=25 February 2020|website=la Repubblica|language=it|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.rtve.es/noticias/20200224/italiano-da-positivo-coronavirus-sur-tenerife/2004321.shtml|title=Un italiano da positivo por coronavirus en el sur de Tenerife|last=RTVE.es/AGENCIAS|date=24 February 2020|website=RTVE.es|language=es|access-date=25 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.theguardian.com/world/2020/feb/25/tenerife-coronavirus-guests-hotel-quarantined|title=Tenerife coronavirus: 1,000 guests at hotel quarantined|date=25 February 2020|website=The Guardian|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>
On 25 February, the wife of the doctor from Lombardy tested positive and was admitted to the same hospital where her husband was being treated.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://diariodeavisos.elespanol.com/2020/02/un-ciudadano-italiano-da-positivo-en-coronavirus-en-el-sur-de-tenerife/|title=Un ciudadano italiano da positivo en el sur de Tenerife por coronavirus|last=Gutiérrez|first=Juan Jesús|date=25 February 2020|website=Diario de Avisos|language=es-ES|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> A 36-year-old Italian woman living in [[Barcelona]] who had visited Bergamo and Milan from 12 to 22 February also tested positive.<ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Europe" /><ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Tenerife" /><ref>{{cite news|url=https://www.thelocal.es/20200225/woman-in-barcelona-tests-positive-to-coronavirus-the-first-confirmed-case-in-mainland-spain|title=Woman in Barcelona tests positive to coronavirus, the first confirmed case on mainland Spain|date=25 February 2020|work=thelocal.es|accessdate=26 February 2020}}</ref> A man from [[Villarreal]] who had recently travelled to Milan tested positive and was admitted to Hospital Universitario de La Plana.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.levante-emv.com/comunitat-valenciana/2020/02/25/coronavirus-caso-valencia-positivo/1982275.html|title=Sanidad confirma el primer caso de coronavirus en la C. Valenciana|last=Levante-EMV|website=levante-emv.com|language=es|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> A 24-year-old man from [[Madrid]] who had recently returned from Northern Italy tested positive and was admitted to [[Hospital Carlos III]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.levante-emv.com/espana/2020/02/25/confirmado-primer-caso-coronavirus-cataluna/1982130.html|title=Un caso de coronavirus en Madrid eleva a siete los infectados en España|last=Levante-EMV|website=levante-emv.com|language=es|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite news|url=http://www.telemadrid.es/noticias/madrid/Confirmado-primer-caso-coronavirus-Madrid-0-2207779217--20200225111539.html|title=Confirmado el primer caso de coronavirus en Madrid|date=25 February 2020|work=telemadrid.es|accessdate=26 February 2020|language=es}}</ref>
On 26 February, two Italian tourists who were vacationing with the Lombardy doctor and his wife also tested positive. The group were transferred to University Hospital of the Nuestra Señora de Candelaria and underwent quarantine.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.rtve.es/noticias/20200226/dos-nuevos-positivos-coronavirus-entre-italianos-del-hotel-adeje-canarias/2004660.shtml|title=Dos nuevos positivos por coronavirus entre los italianos del hotel de Adeje de Canarias|last=EFE|first=RTVE es /|date=26 February 2020|website=RTVE.es|language=es|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref> A 22-year-old man from Barcelona who travelled to Milan between 22 and 25 February tested positive and was admitted to Hospital Clínic.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.ara.cat/societat/segon-cas-coronavirus-catalunya-noi-22-anys-italia_0_2406359478.html|title=Un noi de 22 anys que havia viatjat a Milà és el segon cas de coronavirus a Catalunya|last=Bassas|first=Antoni|date=26 February 2020|website=Ara.cat|language=ca-ES|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.vilaweb.cat/noticies/almenys-setze-infectats-per-coronavirus-i-250-persones-en-quarantena-al-nord-ditalia/|title=[En Directe] Confirmat un segon cas de coronavirus a Catalunya|website=VilaWeb|language=ca|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> A woman from [[La Gomera]] who travelled to Italy between 4 and 8 February tested positive and was admitted to Hospital General de La Gomera in Tenerife.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.20minutos.es/noticia/4166583/0/nuevo-positivo-gomera-eleva-11-numero-infectados-coronavirus-espana/|title=Un nuevo positivo en La Gomera eleva a 11 el número de infectados por coronavirus en España|last=20minutos|date=26 February 2020|website=20minutos.es – Últimas Noticias|language=es|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref>
On 27 February, a 44-year-old man from [[Valencia]] who worked as a sportswriter and had travelled to Milan's [[San Siro]] Stadium on 19 February to watch a football game tested positive and was admitted to Hospital Clínico [[University of Valencia|Universitario de València]]. Two other people with whom he had made contact also tested positive and were admitted to the same hospital. Two more people who had visited the same football game in Milan were hospitalised at the same place.<ref>{{Cite news|last=Linde|first=Pablo|url=https://elpais.com/sociedad/2020/01/31/actualidad/1580509404_469734.html|title=Sanidad confirma en La Gomera el primer caso de coronavirus en España|date=1 February 2020|work=El País|access-date=27 February 2020|language=es|issn=1134-6582}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://en.as.com/en/2020/02/27/football/1582794092_036585.html|title=Valencia fan in Milan last week for UCL tie tests positive for coronavirus|date=27 February 2020|website=AS.com|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{Cite news|last=Bono|first=Ferran|url=https://elpais.com/sociedad/2020/02/27/actualidad/1582795523_075914.html|title=Un periodista que viajó a Milán para cubrir el Valencia-Atalanta, positivo por coronavirus|date=27 February 2020|work=El País|access-date=27 February 2020|language=es|issn=1134-6582}}</ref><ref name=":6">{{cite web|url=https://www.levante-emv.com/comunitat-valenciana/2020/02/27/coronavirus-valencia-nuevos-casos-infectados/1983062.html|title=Sanidad confirma 6 nuevos casos de coronavirus en la C. Valenciana|last=Levante-EMV|website=levante-emv.com|language=es|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> A woman who had visited Milan was hospitalised at Hospital de Sagunto, Valencia.<ref name=":6" /> An Italian student studying in Valencia who had visited Northern Italy was admitted to Hospital Universitario Doctor Peset.<ref name=":6" /> A 22-year-old woman from Tenerife who had travelled to Italy from 19 to 25 February was admitted to Hospital Clínic.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.abc.es/espana/catalunya/abci-mujer-22-anos-viajo-italia-tercer-caso-importado-coronavirus-cataluna-202002271249_noticia.html|title=Una tinerfeña de 22 años que viajó a Italia, tercer caso "importado" de coronavirus en Cataluña|date=27 February 2020|website=abc|language=es|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> An 18-year-old Italian student studying at IE University, [[Segovia]], who had just returned from Milan, was admitted to Hospital General de Segovia.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.elnortedecastilla.es/segovia/ingresado-joven-habitaciones-20200227182120-nt.html|title=Un alumno italiano de IE University en Segovia, primer caso positivo de coronavirus en la región|date=27 February 2020|website=El Norte de Castilla|language=es|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.leonoticias.com/castillayleon/primer-coronavirus-castilla-20200227184850-nt.html|title=Confirmados en Segovia y Valladolid los dos primeros casos registrados en Castilla y León|date=27 February 2020|website=Leonoticias|language=es|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref>
On 28 February, a 27-year-old man from [[Aragon]] with a history of recent trips to Milan tested positive.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.elespanol.com/ciencia/salud/|title=Noticias sobre Salud y Medicina en El Español|website=El Español|language=es-ES|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

'''Sweden''' –
On 26 February, Sweden confirmed that a 30-year-old man who previously visited Northern Italy fell ill three days after returning to Sweden and was admitted to [[Sahlgrenska University Hospital]] in [[Gothenburg]].<ref>{{Cite news|last=Bolin|first=Mattias|url=https://www.svt.se/nyheter/lokalt/vast/bekraftat-coronafall-i-goteborg-person-vardas-pa-sahlgrenska|title=Bekräftat coronafall i Göteborg – person vårdas på Sahlgrenska|date=26 February 2020|work=SVT Nyheter|access-date=26 February 2020|language=sv}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.expressen.se/gt/en-person-i-goteborg-har-testats-positivt-for-corona/|title=Bekräftat fall av Coronavirus i Göteborg – personen har varit i Italien|last=Ekström|first=reas|website=Expressen|language=sv|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.folkhalsomyndigheten.se/nyheter-och-press/nyhetsarkiv/2020/februari/nytt-bekraftat-fall-av-covid-19/|title=Nytt bekräftat fall av covid-19 – Folkhälsomyndigheten|website=folkhalsomyndigheten.se|language=sv|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>
On 27 February, three patients in their 30s were confirmed positive in [[Västra Götaland County|Västra Götaland]]. Two of them had been in contact with the Gothenburg patient, while the other had previously visited Italy.<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.folkhalsomyndigheten.se/nyheter-och-press/nyhetsarkiv/2020/februari/ytterligare-fall-av-covid-19-i-flera-regioner/|title=Ytterligare fall av covid-19 i flera regioner – Folkhälsomyndigheten|website=folkhalsomyndigheten.se|language=sv|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref><ref>{{cite web|url=https://news.cision.com/se/vastra-gotalandsregionen/r/tre-nya-bekraftade-fall-av-coronavirusinfektion--covid-19--i-vastra-gotaland,c3048641|title=Tre nya bekräftade fall av coronavirusinfektion (Covid-19) i Västra Götaland|website=News Powered by Cision|language=sv|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref><ref name=":18">{{cite web|url=https://www.thelocal.se/20200227/five-new-cases-of-the-coronavirus-in-sweden|title=Sweden confirms five new coronavirus cases, including first patient in Stockholm|last=Löfgren|first=Emma|date=27 February 2020|website=thelocal.se|publisher=The Local|accessdate=27 February 2020}}</ref>
On 28 February, a man in his 50s who had returned from Northern Italy on 24 February tested positive and was admitted to a hospital in [[Jönköping]].<ref>{{cite web|url=http://www.rjl.se/nyheter/nyheter-och-pressmeddelanden/pressmeddelande-28-februari-2020-ytterligare-bekraftat-fall-i-jonkopings-lan-av-nya-coronaviruset-covid-19--45553|title=Pressmeddelande 28 februari 2020: Ytterligare bekräftat fall i Jönköpings län av nya coronaviruset (covid-19), Region Jönköpings län|website=rjl.se|language=sv|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

'''Switzerland''' –
On 25 February, Switzerland confirmed its first case, a 70-year-old man in the canton of [[Canton of Ticino|Ticino]] who had previously visited Milan.<ref name="Repubblica_25Feb_Tenerife" /><ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-switzerland-coronavirus-idUSKBN20J1ZO|title=Swiss authorities confirm first case of coronavirus|date=25 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=26 February 2020}}</ref>
On 27 February, a 28-year-old IT worker from [[Geneva]] who had recently returned from Milan tested positive and was admitted to [[Geneva University Hospitals|Geneva University Hospital]].<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.bag.admin.ch/bag/en/home/das-bag/aktuell/medienmitteilungen.msg-id-78268.html|title=New coronavirus Covid-19: three new confirmed cases in Switzerland|website=bag.admin.ch|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref name=":02">{{cite web|url=https://www.swissinfo.ch/eng/politics/covid-19_switzerland-confirms-second-coronavirus-case/45582788|title=Switzerland confirms total of four coronavirus cases|last1=swissinfo.ch|first1=S. W. I.|last2=Corporation|first2=a branch of the Swiss Broadcasting|website=SWI swissinfo.ch|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> Two Italian children on vacation in [[Canton of Grisons|Graubünden]] tested positive and were hospitalised.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.gr.ch/DE/institutionen/verwaltung/djsg/ga/coronavirus/Seiten/Info.aspx|title=Informationen zum Coronavirus|website=gr.ch|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref><ref name=":02" /><ref name=":92">{{cite web|url=https://www.bielertagblatt.ch/nachrichten/schweiz/graubuenden-sagt-den-engadiner-skimarathon-ab|title=Graubünden sagt den Engadiner Skimarathon ab|website=Bieler Tagblatt|language=de|access-date=27 February 2020|archive-url=https://web.archive.org/web/20200227174547/https://www.bielertagblatt.ch/nachrichten/schweiz/graubuenden-sagt-den-engadiner-skimarathon-ab|archive-date=27 February 2020|url-status=dead}}</ref> A 26-year-old man in [[Canton of Aargau|Aargau]] who had visited Verona on a business trip the previous week tested positive and was hospitalised.<ref name=":02" /> A 30-year-old woman who visited Milan was admitted to a hospital in [[Zürich|Zurich]].<ref name=":02" /> A young woman who had travelled to Milan tested positive in [[Canton of Basel-Stadt|Basel-City]]. She worked for a daycare centre in [[Riehen]], and after her test was confirmed, the children at the daycare were put into a two-week quarantine.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.reuters.com/article/us-china-health-swiss-idUSKCN20L167|title=Swiss coronavirus cases rise to nine as children placed in precautionary quarantine|date=27 February 2020|agency=Reuters|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref> On 28 February, her partner, a 23-year-old man, also tested positive in [[Canton of Basel-Landschaft|Basel-Country]].<ref name=":21">{{cite web|url=https://www.rts.ch/info/suisse/11127000-manifestations-d-ampleur-interdites-en-raison-du-coronavirus-conference-de-presse-du-conseil-federal-en-direct.html|title=Les manifestations d'ampleur interdites en Suisse en raison du coronavirus|date=28 February 2020|website=rts.ch|language=fr|access-date=1 March 2020}}</ref> On 29 February, the man's mother tested positive as well.
On 28 February, a 45-year-old-man who had travelled to Milan tested positive in [[Zürich]].<ref name=":21" />

'''Ukraine''' –
On 3 March, Ukraine confirmed its first case in [[Chernivtsi]], a man who had travelled from Italy by plane to the Romanian city of [[Suceava]] and then to Ukraine by car with his wife.<ref>{{cite web|url=https://www.forbes.com/sites/katyagorchinskaya/2020/03/03/first-case-of-coronavirus-registered-in-ukraine/|title=First Case Of Coronavirus Registered in Ukraine|date=3 March 2020|access-date=3 March 2020}}</ref>

'''United Kingdom''' –
On 27 February, the United Kingdom confirmed that a patient who had visited Milan tested positive and was admitted to [[Royal Free Hospital]] in London.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/uk-51656609|title=Two more coronavirus cases confirmed in England|date=27 February 2020|work=BBC News|access-date=27 February 2020}}</ref> Northern Ireland reported its first case, an adult who had travelled from Northern Italy via Dublin and was admitted to Royal Victoria Hospital in [[Belfast]].<ref>{{cite web|last=Kearney|first=Vincent|date=27 February 2020|title=NI coronavirus case had travelled through Dublin|url=https://www.rte.ie/news/health/2020/0227/1117991-ireland-coronavirus/}}</ref>
On 28 February, Wales reported its first case, a patient who had returned from northern Italy was treated at a specialist unit in England.<ref>{{Cite news|url=https://www.bbc.com/news/uk-wales-51450517|title=First case of coronavirus in Wales confirmed|date=28 February 2020|work=BBC News|access-date=28 February 2020}}</ref>

===Oceania===

'''New Zealand''' –
On 4 March, the New Zealand Ministry of Health confirmed its second case, a woman in her 30s who returned to [[Auckland]] from Northern Italy.<ref>{{cite news |title=Second Case of COVID-19 Confirmed in NZ |url=https://www.health.govt.nz/news-media/media-releases/second-case-covid-19-confirmed-nz |accessdate=4 March 2020 |work=Ministry of Health NZ }}</ref>
